**[January](/wiki/January "January")** **[2025](/wiki/2025 "2025")** was the first month of the current common year. The month, which began on a [Wednesday](/wiki/Wednesday "Wednesday"), ended on a [Friday](/wiki/Friday "Friday") after 31 days.

## [Portal:Current events](/wiki/Portal%3ACurrent_events "Portal:Current events")

[edit](/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/January_2025&action=edit&section=1 "Edit section: Portal:Current events")

*This is an [archived version](/wiki/Portal%3ACurrent_events/How_to_archive_the_portal "Portal:Current events/How to archive the portal") of Wikipedia's [Current events Portal](/wiki/Portal%3ACurrent_events "Portal:Current events") from January 2025.*

January 1, 2025 (2025-01-01) (Wednesday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_1&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_1&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_1&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip](/wiki/Israeli_invasion_of_the_Gaza_Strip "Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip")
    - [Israeli](/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces "Israel Defense Forces") airstrikes across the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip") kill at least 26 [Palestinians](/wiki/Palestinians "Palestinians"), including four children. At least ten others are missing and believed to be buried under [rubble](/wiki/Rubble "Rubble"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/1/israel-kills-at-least-22-palestinians-across-gaza-on-new-year-day)
* [2025 New Orleans truck attack](/wiki/2025_New_Orleans_truck_attack "2025 New Orleans truck attack")
  + A man kills 14 people and injures 35 others, including two police officers, in a [vehicle-ramming](/wiki/Vehicle-ramming_attack "Vehicle-ramming attack") and [shooting attack](/wiki/Mass_shooting "Mass shooting") on [Bourbon Street](/wiki/Bourbon_Street "Bourbon Street") in [New Orleans](/wiki/New_Orleans "New Orleans"), [Louisiana](/wiki/Louisiana "Louisiana"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), before being shot dead. The [FBI](/wiki/FBI "FBI") says that it found an [Islamic State](/wiki/Islamic_State "Islamic State") flag in the suspect's vehicle. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/multiple-fatalities-truck-crashes-into-new-orleans-crowd-cbs-news-says-2025-01-01/)
* [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)")
  + The [African Union Support and Stabilisation Mission](/wiki/African_Union_Support_and_Stabilization_Mission_in_Somalia "African Union Support and Stabilization Mission in Somalia"), endorsed by the [United Nations Security Council](/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council "United Nations Security Council") on December 27, replaces the [African Union Transition Mission](/wiki/African_Union_Transition_Mission_in_Somalia "African Union Transition Mission in Somalia") as the [African Union](/wiki/African_Union "African Union")'s [peacekeeping](/wiki/Peacekeeping "Peacekeeping") mission in [Somalia](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia"). [(Voice of Nigeria)](https://von.gov.ng/un-approves-new-au-force-in-somalia/) [(UN Press)](https://press.un.org/en/2024/sc15955.doc.htm)

**Arts and culture**

* [Public Domain Day](/wiki/Public_Domain_Day "Public Domain Day"), [2025 in public domain](/wiki/2025_in_public_domain "2025 in public domain")
  + The novel *[A Farewell to Arms](/wiki/A_Farewell_to_Arms "A Farewell to Arms")* and the cartoon characters [Popeye](/wiki/Popeye "Popeye") and [Tintin](/wiki/Tintin_%28character%29 "Tintin (character)") enter the [public domain](/wiki/Public_domain "Public domain") in the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"). [(*Rolling Stone*)](https://www.rollingstone.com/culture/culture-news/popeye-skeleton-dance-singin-in-the-rain-maltese-falcon-public-domain-1235218802/)

**Business and economy**

* [2022–2023 Russia–European Union gas dispute](/wiki/2022%E2%80%932023_Russia%E2%80%93European_Union_gas_dispute "2022–2023 Russia–European Union gas dispute")
  + [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia")'s gas firm [Gazprom](/wiki/Gazprom "Gazprom") suspends exports of [Russian natural gas](/wiki/Natural_gas_in_Russia "Natural gas in Russia") through [Ukrainian pipelines](/wiki/Natural_gas_transmission_system_of_Ukraine "Natural gas transmission system of Ukraine") after [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine") refused to renew the transit agreement between its operator [Naftogaz](/wiki/Naftogaz "Naftogaz") and Gazprom. However, [Hungary](/wiki/Hungary "Hungary") will continue receiving Russian [natural gas](/wiki/Natural_gas "Natural gas") via the [TurkStream](/wiki/TurkStream "TurkStream") pipeline. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/business/energy/russia-halts-gas-exports-europe-via-ukraine-2025-01-01/)
* [Foreign relations of Mexico](/wiki/Foreign_relations_of_Mexico "Foreign relations of Mexico")
  + [Mexico](/wiki/Mexico "Mexico")'s [Tax Administration Service](/wiki/Servicio_de_Administraci%C3%B3n_Tributaria "Servicio de Administración Tributaria") implements new [tariffs](/wiki/Tariff "Tariff"), including a 19% [duty](/wiki/Duty_%28tax%29 "Duty (tax)") on goods from countries without international [trade agreements](/wiki/Trade_agreement "Trade agreement") with Mexico and a 17% duty on goods from [Canada](/wiki/Canada "Canada") and the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") under certain value thresholds. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/mexico-unveils-new-tariffs-popular-e-tailers-like-shein-temu-may-be-crosshairs-2024-12-31/)
* [Moldova–Russia relations](/wiki/Moldova%E2%80%93Russia_relations "Moldova–Russia relations")
  + As announced, [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia")'s [Gazprom](/wiki/Gazprom "Gazprom") halts its gas supplies both to [Moldova](/wiki/Moldova "Moldova") and the self-proclaimed [Transnistrian Republic](/wiki/Transnistria "Transnistria") alleging non-compliance with payment obligations. [(bne IntelliNews)](https://www.intellinews.com/russia-cuts-gas-deliveries-to-moldova-in-attempt-to-undermine-political-stability-359712/), [(Politico)](https://www.politico.eu/article/moldova-gas-russia-cut-off-russia-cuts-off-gas-to-moldovan-separatists-risking-humanitarian-crisis/)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [European migrant crisis](/wiki/European_migrant_crisis "European migrant crisis")
  + Twenty-seven migrants from [sub-Saharan Africa](/wiki/Sub-Saharan_Africa "Sub-Saharan Africa") are killed, and 83 others are rescued after two boats capsize off the [Kerkennah Islands](/wiki/Kerkennah_Islands "Kerkennah Islands") near [Tunisia](/wiki/Tunisia "Tunisia"), with searches ongoing for additional missing passengers. [(France 24)](https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20250102-27-sub-saharan-african-migrants-die-off-tunisia-in-shipwrecks)
* Three people are killed and over twenty others are injured in a fireworks explosion at a house in [Honolulu](/wiki/Honolulu "Honolulu"), [Hawaii](/wiki/Hawaii "Hawaii"), United States. [(CTV News)](https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/rescuers-find-gruesome-scene-at-a-honolulu-home-after-a-fireworks-blast-kills-3-injures-over-20-1.7162295)
* A tour bus crashed into a tree in [Surat Thani province](/wiki/Surat_Thani_province "Surat Thani province"), [Thailand](/wiki/Thailand "Thailand"), killing five and 30.[(The Straits Times)](https://www.straitstimes.com/asia/se-asia/tour-bus-crash-in-thailands-surat-thani-leaves-5-dead-30-injured)

**International relations**

* [Honduras–United States relations](/wiki/Honduras%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Honduras–United States relations")
  + [Honduran President](/wiki/President_of_Honduras "President of Honduras") [Xiomara Castro](/wiki/Xiomara_Castro "Xiomara Castro") warns that she might remove all [US military bases](/wiki/US_military_bases "US military bases") from [Honduras](/wiki/Honduras "Honduras") and seek to cancel the military cooperation with the United States if [President-elect](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") fulfills his threat to order mass deportations of [Hondurans](/wiki/Honduran_diaspora "Honduran diaspora") when he takes office next January 20. [(*The Tico Times*)](https://ticotimes.net/2025/01/02/honduras-threatens-to-expel-u-s-military-bases-over-trumps-deportation-plans)

**Law and crime**

* + Five people are killed, several others are injured, and at least 330 people are arrested due to mishandling of [pyrotechnics](/wiki/Pyrotechnics "Pyrotechnics") during [New Year's celebrations](/wiki/New_Year%27s_Eve "New Year's Eve") in [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany"). [(RNZ)](https://www.rnz.co.nz/news/world/538011/five-dead-in-germany-from-new-year-s-fireworks-accidents) [(1News)](https://www.1news.co.nz/2025/01/02/german-government-condemns-violence-that-killed-five-on-nye/)
* [2025 Cetinje shootings](/wiki/2025_Cetinje_shootings "2025 Cetinje shootings")
  + Twelve people are killed and four others are injured in a [shooting spree](/wiki/Spree_killer "Spree killer") in [Cetinje](/wiki/Cetinje "Cetinje"), [Montenegro](/wiki/Montenegro "Montenegro"). The perpetrator kills himself. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/montenegro-shooting-gunman-suicide-cetinje-7ab4ac905c4d08bca357251823dd4ee6) [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/2/at-least-10-killed-in-mass-shooting-in-montenegro-suspect-kills-himself)
* [Al Jazeera controversies and criticism](/wiki/Al_Jazeera_controversies_and_criticism "Al Jazeera controversies and criticism")
  + The [Palestinian Authority](/wiki/Palestinian_Authority "Palestinian Authority") suspends [Al Jazeera](/wiki/Al_Jazeera_Media_Network "Al Jazeera Media Network")'s broadcasts and operations in [Palestine](/wiki/State_of_Palestine "State of Palestine"), accusing the network of interfering in internal affairs and spreading [incitement](/wiki/Incitement "Incitement") and [misinformation](/wiki/Misinformation "Misinformation"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/palestinian-authority-suspends-broadcast-qatars-al-jazeera-tv-temporarily-2025-01-01/)
* [Capital punishment in Saudi Arabia](/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_Saudi_Arabia "Capital punishment in Saudi Arabia")
  + [Saudi Arabia](/wiki/Saudi_Arabia "Saudi Arabia") announces the [execution](/wiki/Capital_punishment "Capital punishment") of six [Iranian](/wiki/Iran "Iran") nationals convicted of [smuggling](/wiki/Illegal_drug_trade "Illegal drug trade") [hashish](/wiki/Hashish "Hashish"). In [Tehran](/wiki/Tehran "Tehran"), the [Iranian Foreign Ministry](/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_%28Iran%29 "Ministry of Foreign Affairs (Iran)") summoned the Saudi ambassador in protest. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/iran-saudi-arabia-hashish-executions-efd48a3efcdbf2664e14c8ccf879f323)
* [LGBTQ rights in Liechtenstein](/wiki/LGBTQ_rights_in_Liechtenstein "LGBTQ rights in Liechtenstein")
  + [Liechtenstein](/wiki/Liechtenstein "Liechtenstein") becomes the 37th country to legalize [same-sex marriage](/wiki/Same-sex_marriage_in_Liechtenstein "Same-sex marriage in Liechtenstein"). [(GCN)](https://gcn.ie/liechtenstein-legalise-same-sex-marriage/)
* [Trump International Hotel Las Vegas Tesla Cybertruck explosion](/wiki/Trump_International_Hotel_Las_Vegas_Tesla_Cybertruck_explosion "Trump International Hotel Las Vegas Tesla Cybertruck explosion")
  + A [Tesla Cybertruck](/wiki/Tesla_Cybertruck "Tesla Cybertruck") containing firework mortars and gas canisters explodes outside the [Trump International Hotel Las Vegas](/wiki/Trump_International_Hotel_Las_Vegas "Trump International Hotel Las Vegas") in [Paradise](/wiki/Paradise%2C_Nevada "Paradise, Nevada"), [Nevada](/wiki/Nevada "Nevada"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), injuring seven people. The driver died from a self-inflicted gunshot prior to the explosion. [The Federal Bureau of Investigation](/wiki/The_Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation "The Federal Bureau of Investigation") (FBI) is currently investigating the incident as a possible terrorist attack. [(ABC News)](https://abc7.com/post/trump-tower-fire-police-investigating-vehicle-explosion-las-vegas-nevada-hotel-driver-dead/15737979/)
* Five people are killed in a [familicide](/wiki/Familicide "Familicide") [mass stabbing](/wiki/Mass_stabbing "Mass stabbing") when a son kills his four sisters and mother in [Lucknow](/wiki/Lucknow "Lucknow"), [Uttar Pradesh](/wiki/Uttar_Pradesh "Uttar Pradesh"), [India](/wiki/India "India"). [(*The Hindu*)](https://www.thehindu.com/news/national/uttar-pradesh/five-of-family-found-dead-in-lucknow-hotel-accused-held/article69049292.ece)
* [Myanmar](/wiki/Myanmar "Myanmar")'s [Tatmadaw](/wiki/Tatmadaw "Tatmadaw") enacts a [cybersecurity](/wiki/Cybersecurity "Cybersecurity") [law](/wiki/Constitution_of_Myanmar "Constitution of Myanmar") imposing [strict controls](/wiki/Censorship_in_Myanmar "Censorship in Myanmar") on digital communications, requiring service providers to store [user data](/wiki/User_data "User data") for three years, penalizing [VPN](/wiki/VPN "VPN") use without government approval, and allowing authorities to block or shut down platforms deemed to spread disinformation or disrupt stability. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/internet-online-censorship-law-repression-8128ba7a2c02555217c6a64ab641eaf6)
* A [police officer](/wiki/New_Zealand_Police "New Zealand Police") is killed and four other people are injured in a vehicle-ramming attack during a patrol in [Nelson](/wiki/Nelson%2C_New_Zealand "Nelson, New Zealand"), [New Zealand](/wiki/New_Zealand "New Zealand"). A 32-year-old suspect is arrested. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/police-officer-killed-zealand-nelson-lyn-fleming-475f2a6aa1a5e7739b19d3fd1e724733)
* Eleven people are injured during a [mass shooting](/wiki/Mass_shooting "Mass shooting") outside a nightclub in [Queens](/wiki/Queens "Queens"), [New York](/wiki/New_York_%28state%29 "New York (state)"), United States. [(*The Nightly*)](https://thenightly.com.au/world/new-york-nightclub-mass-shooting-11-people-reportedly-injured-after-incident-at-amazura-night-club-in-queens-c-17263836)
* [FBI](/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Investigation "Federal Bureau of Investigation") agents announce the seizure of more than 150 homemade [pipe bombs](/wiki/Pipe_bomb "Pipe bomb") and other [explosive devices](/wiki/Explosive_device "Explosive device") from a home in [Isle of Wight County](/wiki/Isle_of_Wight_County%2C_Virginia "Isle of Wight County, Virginia"), [Virginia](/wiki/Virginia "Virginia"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), "the largest seizure by number of finished explosive devices in FBI history". [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/homemade-bombs-seized-virginia-firearms-c68488480ef8bd3de7b432272399aa28)

**Politics and elections**

* [Bulgaria](/wiki/Bulgaria "Bulgaria") and [Romania](/wiki/Romania "Romania") finalize the process of joining the [Schengen Area](/wiki/Schengen_Area "Schengen Area") and lift their land [border controls](/wiki/Border_control "Border control"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/bulgaria-romania-full-membership-schengen-area-8f63edc2d0dfa7e1d14934ea1cd9b2a2)
* [Karin Keller-Sutter](/wiki/Karin_Keller-Sutter "Karin Keller-Sutter") is sworn in as [President of Switzerland](/wiki/President_of_Switzerland "President of Switzerland"). [(*Le News*)](https://lenews.ch/2024/12/27/switzerlands-new-president-in-2025/)
* [Poland](/wiki/Poland "Poland") takes over the [Presidency of the Council of the European Union](/wiki/Presidency_of_the_Council_of_the_European_Union "Presidency of the Council of the European Union") after [Hungary](/wiki/Hungary "Hungary"). [(Polsat News)](https://www.polsatnews.pl/wiadomosc/2025-01-03/inauguracja-polskiej-prezydencji-w-ue/) [(TVN24)](https://tvn24.pl/polska/polska-prezydencja-w-radzie-unii-europejskiej-oficjalna-inauguracja-przemowienie-premiera-donalda-tuska-st8245824)

January 2, 2025 (2025-01-02) (Thursday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_2&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_2&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_2&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war")
  + [Israeli invasion of Syria](/wiki/Israeli_invasion_of_Syria_%282024%E2%80%93present%29 "Israeli invasion of Syria (2024–present)")
    - [Israeli warplanes](/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force "Israeli Air Force") carry out airstrikes on defense factories and a research center in [Al-Safira](/wiki/Al-Safira "Al-Safira"), [Aleppo Governorate](/wiki/Aleppo_Governorate "Aleppo Governorate"), [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria"). [(Xinhua)](https://english.news.cn/20250103/755c955446c44a73a4034e7ca9c6efde/c.html)
  + [US intervention in the Syrian civil war](/wiki/US_intervention_in_the_Syrian_civil_war "US intervention in the Syrian civil war")
    - According to the [Syrian Observatory for Human Rights](/wiki/Syrian_Observatory_for_Human_Rights "Syrian Observatory for Human Rights"), [U.S. forces](/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces "United States Armed Forces") are deploying a new convoy to areas controlled by the [Syrian Democratic Forces](/wiki/Syrian_Democratic_Forces "Syrian Democratic Forces") in [Kobani](/wiki/Kobani "Kobani"), Aleppo Governorate, as part of operations to establish a new [US military base](/wiki/List_of_American_military_installations "List of American military installations") in north-eastern Syria. [(SOHR)](https://www.syriahr.com/en/352729/)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip](/wiki/Israeli_invasion_of_the_Gaza_Strip "Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip")
    - Eleven people are killed, including a [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") police chief, in an [Israeli](/wiki/Israel "Israel") airstrike on a [refugee camp](/wiki/Palestinian_refugee_camp "Palestinian refugee camp") in [al-Mawasi](/wiki/Al-Mawasi%2C_Rafah "Al-Mawasi, Rafah") in the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cq62dver40yo)
  + [Israeli Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel "Prime Minister of Israel") [Benjamin Netanyahu](/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu "Benjamin Netanyahu")'s office announces that it has approved a delegation to [Doha](/wiki/Doha "Doha"), [Qatar](/wiki/Qatar "Qatar") for [ceasefire](/wiki/Ceasefire "Ceasefire") talks. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/israeli-delegation-resume-ceasefire-talks-doha-pms-office-says-2025-01-02/)
* [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)"), [War against the Islamic State](/wiki/War_against_the_Islamic_State "War against the Islamic State")
  + [Islamic State insurgency in Puntland](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland")
    - [Puntland forces](/wiki/Puntland_Security_Force "Puntland Security Force") conduct airstrikes on [ISIL](/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_Somalia_Province "Islamic State – Somalia Province") hideouts in [Bari](/wiki/Bari%2C_Somalia "Bari, Somalia"), [Puntland](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland"), [Somalia](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia"), after they announced a military offensive against ISIL and [Al-Shabaab](/wiki/Al-Shabaab_%28militant_group%29 "Al-Shabaab (militant group)"). [(Idil News)](https://www.idilnews.com/puntland-forces-conduct-airstrikes-on-isis-positions-in-bari-region/) [(VOA)](https://www.voasomali.com/a/puntland-oo-sheegatay-duqeyn-ka-dhan-ah-daacish/7922007.html)
* [2025 New Orleans truck attack](/wiki/2025_New_Orleans_truck_attack "2025 New Orleans truck attack"), [2025 Las Vegas Trump Hotel bombing](/wiki/Trump_International_Hotel_Las_Vegas_Tesla_Cybertruck_explosion "Trump International Hotel Las Vegas Tesla Cybertruck explosion")
  + [Christopher Raia](/w/index.php?title=Christopher_Raia&action=edit&redlink=1 "Christopher Raia (page does not exist)"), the deputy assistant director of the [FBI](/wiki/FBI "FBI")'s counterterrorism division, says he believes that there is "no definitive link" between the two alleged [U.S. Army](/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces "United States Armed Forces") servicemen perpetrators of the attacks, Shamsud-Din Jabbar in New Orleans and Matthew Alan Livelsberger in Las Vegas. [(BBC)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/crl378x8nnjo)
* [Moro conflict](/wiki/Moro_conflict "Moro conflict")
  + A wave of attacks since two days ago against police in [Mindanao](/wiki/Mindanao "Mindanao"), [Philippines](/wiki/Philippines "Philippines"), results in the killing of two perpetrators and one officer. [(Rappler)](https://www.rappler.com/philippines/mindanao/attacks-cops-new-year-eve-december-31-2024/)

**Business and economy**

* [German economic crisis](/wiki/German_economic_crisis_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "German economic crisis (2022–present)")
  + The [Handelsblatt Research Institute](/wiki/Handelsblatt "Handelsblatt") reports that the [German economy](/wiki/Economy_of_Germany "Economy of Germany") is in its "greatest crisis in [post-war history](/wiki/History_of_Germany_%281990%E2%80%93present%29 "History of Germany (1990–present)")" after projecting that the economy will enter its third year of [recession](/wiki/Recession "Recession") in 2025 with a 0.1% contraction, following a 0.3% contraction in both 2023 and 2024. [(TVP World)](https://tvpworld.com/84331034/german-recession-projected-to-enter-its-third-year)

**Disasters and accidents**

* A small plane crashes through the roof of a commercial warehouse in [Fullerton](/wiki/Fullerton%2C_California "Fullerton, California"), [California](/wiki/California "California"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), causing a fire, killing two people and injuring at least 18 others. [(KABC-TV)](https://abc7.com/post/small-plane-crashes-fullerton-resulting-4-alarm-fire-police-say/15742833/) [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/california-plane-crash-fullerton-08ec23f1c117be7bc07fc9b8f4064f91)
* Two officers were injured in an explosion of an unknown object at a police fence in [Berlin-Wittenau](/wiki/Berlin-Wittenau "Berlin-Wittenau"); the reasons for this are still unclear. [(*tagesschau*)](https://www.tagesschau.de/inland/regional/berlin/polizisten-explosion-verletzungen-berlin-100.html)

**International relations**

* [Iran–Italy relations](/wiki/Iran%E2%80%93Italy_relations "Iran–Italy relations")
  + [Italy](/wiki/Italy "Italy") summons [Iran](/wiki/Iran "Iran")'s ambassador to demand the release of *[Il Foglio](/wiki/Il_Foglio "Il Foglio")* reporter [Cecilia Sala](/wiki/Cecilia_Sala "Cecilia Sala"), [detained](/wiki/List_of_foreign_nationals_detained_in_Iran "List of foreign nationals detained in Iran") in [Tehran](/wiki/Tehran "Tehran") for alleged legal violations. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/italy-iran-journalist-arrest-ambassador-6656e7f9df9db8b7216a180d69dde52c)
* [Syria–Ukraine relations](/wiki/Syria%E2%80%93Ukraine_relations "Syria–Ukraine relations")
  + [Ukrainian president](/wiki/President_of_Ukraine "President of Ukraine") [Volodymyr Zelenskyy](/wiki/Volodymyr_Zelenskyy "Volodymyr Zelenskyy") says that [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine") will pledge support to the [Syrian transitional government](/wiki/First_Syrian_transitional_government "First Syrian transitional government"). [(*The Press Democrat*)](https://www.pressdemocrat.com/article/news/middle-east-latest-ukraine-pledges-support-for-a-new-syria-once-a-key-rus/)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024 Venezuelan political crisis](/wiki/2024_Venezuelan_political_crisis "2024 Venezuelan political crisis")
  + The [government](/wiki/Government_of_Venezuela "Government of Venezuela") of [Venezuelan president](/wiki/President_of_Venezuela "President of Venezuela") [Nicolás Maduro](/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro "Nicolás Maduro") offers a [US$](/wiki/United_States_dollar "United States dollar")100,000 reward for the capture of exiled opposition leader [Edmundo González Urrutia](/wiki/Edmundo_Gonz%C3%A1lez_Urrutia "Edmundo González Urrutia"), who claims that he is ready to take office as the legitimate president on January 10. [(*El Universal*)](https://www.eluniversal.com/politica/198116/gobierno-nacional-ofrece-recompensa-de-100000-por-la-captura-de-edmundo-gonzalez-urrutia) [(*El País*)](https://elpais.com/america/2024-11-25/edmundo-gonzalez-asegura-que-tomara-posesion-como-presidente-el-10-de-enero-en-caracas.html)
* [Ecuadorian president](/wiki/President_of_Ecuador "President of Ecuador") [Daniel Noboa](/wiki/Daniel_Noboa "Daniel Noboa") decrees the suspension of his [vice president](/wiki/Vice_President_of_Ecuador "Vice President of Ecuador") [Verónica Abad](/wiki/Ver%C3%B3nica_Abad "Verónica Abad") accusing her of contempt, and the handover of her functions to national planning secretary [Sariha Moya](/wiki/Sariha_Moya "Sariha Moya"). Noboa already appointed Moya to replace Abad in November 2024, but a [constitutional judge](/wiki/Constitutional_Court_of_Ecuador "Constitutional Court of Ecuador") reversed the decree in December. [(Swiss Info)](https://www.swissinfo.ch/spa/noboa-vuelve-a-designar-vice-interina-de-ecuador-en-medio-de-pugna-con-abad/88668546)
* The [Parliament of Ghana](/wiki/Parliament_of_Ghana "Parliament of Ghana") prevents a potential [government shutdown](/wiki/Government_shutdown "Government shutdown") by approving a provisional [budget](/wiki/Government_budget "Government budget") of [₵](/wiki/Ghanaian_cedi "Ghanaian cedi")68.1 billion ($4.65 billion) to fund [government](/wiki/Government_of_Ghana "Government of Ghana") operations through March, amid a transition to [John Mahama](/wiki/John_Mahama "John Mahama")'s [presidency](/wiki/Presidency_of_John_Mahama "Presidency of John Mahama"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/ghanas-parliament-passes-provisional-budget-averts-government-shutdown-2025-01-03/)
* The [Constitutional Court of Indonesia](/wiki/Constitutional_Court_of_Indonesia "Constitutional Court of Indonesia") rules that the 20% [electoral threshold](/wiki/Electoral_threshold "Electoral threshold") for [political parties](/wiki/List_of_political_parties_in_Indonesia "List of political parties in Indonesia") to nominate a [presidential](/wiki/President_of_Indonesia "President of Indonesia") candidate is not legally binding, potentially enabling smaller parties to participate in future presidential [elections](/wiki/Elections_in_Indonesia "Elections in Indonesia") without the need to form coalition with larger parties. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/indonesia-court-says-vote-threshold-presidential-candidates-not-legally-binding-2025-01-02/)
* The [Chilean president](/wiki/President_of_Chile "President of Chile"), [Gabriel Boric](/wiki/Gabriel_Boric "Gabriel Boric"), begins a historic three-day trip to [Antarctica](/wiki/Antarctica "Antarctica") along with civil, scientific and military authorities. According to the Chilean Government, the codenamed *Operación Estrella Polar III* seeks to strengthen the country's presence in the territory. [(Government of Chile)](https://www.gob.cl/noticias/presidente-gabriel-boric-realiza-historico-viaje-polo-sur-operacion-estrella-polar/)
* [Jenniffer González Colón](/wiki/Jenniffer_Gonz%C3%A1lez_Col%C3%B3n "Jenniffer González Colón") takes office as [Governor of Puerto Rico](/wiki/Governor_of_Puerto_Rico "Governor of Puerto Rico"). [(PBS)](https://www.pbs.org/newshour/nation/puerto-ricos-new-governor-takes-office-amid-anger-following-major-blackout)

**Science and technology**

* [2025 in paleontology](/wiki/2025_in_paleontology "2025 in paleontology"), [Dinosaur finds in the United Kingdom](/wiki/List_of_dinosaur_finds_in_the_United_Kingdom "List of dinosaur finds in the United Kingdom")
  + The largest site of [dinosaur footprints](/wiki/Fossil_track "Fossil track") of the *[Cetiosaurus](/wiki/Cetiosaurus "Cetiosaurus")* and *[Megalosaurus](/wiki/Megalosaurus "Megalosaurus")* dating back to the [Middle Jurassic](/wiki/Middle_Jurassic "Middle Jurassic") [Bathonian](/wiki/Bathonian "Bathonian") stage 166 million years ago is discovered at a [quarry](/wiki/Quarry "Quarry") in [Oxfordshire](/wiki/Oxfordshire "Oxfordshire"), [England](/wiki/England "England"), [United Kingdom](/wiki/United_Kingdom "United Kingdom"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c24nzeqq1l2o)

January 3, 2025 (2025-01-03) (Friday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_3&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_3&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_3&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war")
  + [East Aleppo offensive](/wiki/East_Aleppo_offensive_%282024%E2%80%93present%29 "East Aleppo offensive (2024–present)")
    - Clashes between the [Kurdish](/wiki/Kurds_in_Syria "Kurds in Syria")-led [Syrian Democratic Forces](/wiki/Syrian_Democratic_Forces "Syrian Democratic Forces") (SDF) and the [Turkish](/wiki/Turkey "Turkey")-backed [Syrian National Army](/wiki/Syrian_National_Army "Syrian National Army") escalate near the [Tishrin Dam](/wiki/Tishrin_Dam "Tishrin Dam") in [Aleppo Governorate](/wiki/Aleppo_Governorate "Aleppo Governorate"), [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria"). The [Turkish Air Force](/wiki/Turkish_Air_Force "Turkish Air Force") also conducts [airstrikes](/wiki/Airstrike "Airstrike") on SDF positions. [(SOHR)](https://www.syriahr.com/en/352816/) [(SOHR 2)](https://www.syriahr.com/en/352846/)
  + [US intervention in the Syrian civil war](/wiki/US_intervention_in_the_Syrian_civil_war "US intervention in the Syrian civil war")
    - Deputy [U.S. Defense](/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Defense "United States Department of Defense") Press Secretary [Sabrina Singh](/wiki/Sabrina_Singh "Sabrina Singh") says that, despite local reports, the [U.S. Army](/wiki/U.S._Army "U.S. Army") has "no plans" to build a military base in [Kobani](/wiki/Kobani "Kobani"), [Aleppo Governorate](/wiki/Aleppo_Governorate "Aleppo Governorate"), which is currently under the control of the [Syrian Democratic Forces](/wiki/Syrian_Democratic_Forces "Syrian Democratic Forces"). [(Rudaw)](https://manage.rudaw.net/english/middleeast/syria/030120254)
* [Haitian crisis](/wiki/Haitian_crisis_%282018%E2%80%93present%29 "Haitian crisis (2018–present)")
  + [Gang war in Haiti](/wiki/Gang_war_in_Haiti "Gang war in Haiti"), [Guatemala–Haiti relations](/wiki/Guatemala%E2%80%93Haiti_relations "Guatemala–Haiti relations"), [El Salvador–Haiti relations](/wiki/El_Salvador%E2%80%93Haiti_relations "El Salvador–Haiti relations"), [El Salvador–Guatemala relations](/wiki/El_Salvador%E2%80%93Guatemala_relations "El Salvador–Guatemala relations")
    - A contingent of [peacekeeping](/wiki/Peacekeeping "Peacekeeping") troops from [Guatemala](/wiki/Guatemala "Guatemala") and [El Salvador](/wiki/El_Salvador "El Salvador") arrive in [Port-au-Prince](/wiki/Port-au-Prince "Port-au-Prince"), [Haiti](/wiki/Haiti "Haiti"), to enforce a [United Nations](/wiki/United_Nations "United Nations")-backed [multinational security mission](/wiki/Multinational_Security_Support_Mission_in_Haiti "Multinational Security Support Mission in Haiti") to restore order to Port-au-Prince amid an increase in gang violence. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/central-american-troops-arrive-haiti-fight-gangs-2025-01-03/)
* [Red Sea crisis](/wiki/Red_Sea_crisis "Red Sea crisis")
  + The [Israeli Defense Forces](/wiki/Israeli_Defense_Forces "Israeli Defense Forces") report the interception of a [ballistic missile](/wiki/Ballistic_missile "Ballistic missile") and a [drone](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") launched from [Yemen](/wiki/Yemen "Yemen"). [(France 24)](https://www.france24.com/en/middle-east/20250103-israel-intercepts-new-missile-launched-from-yemen-says-idf)

**Business and economy**

* [Proposed acquisition of U.S. Steel by Nippon Steel](/wiki/Proposed_acquisition_of_U.S._Steel_by_Nippon_Steel "Proposed acquisition of U.S. Steel by Nippon Steel")
  + [U.S. President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Joe Biden](/wiki/Joe_Biden "Joe Biden") blocks a [buyout](/wiki/Buyout "Buyout") bid by [Japanese](/wiki/Japan "Japan") [Nippon Steel](/wiki/Nippon_Steel "Nippon Steel") for [U.S. Steel](/wiki/U.S._Steel "U.S. Steel"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cx2vz83pg9eo)
* [Qatar Airways](/wiki/Qatar_Airways "Qatar Airways") announces the resumption of flights to [Damascus International Airport](/wiki/Damascus_International_Airport "Damascus International Airport") in [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria") beginning on January 7, becoming the first major international [airline](/wiki/Airline "Airline") to resume scheduled service to Syria since the [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war") began in 2011. [(Aviation Week)](https://aviationweek.com/air-transport/airports-networks/qatar-airways-resume-syria-flights)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [January 2025 North American winter storm](/wiki/January_5%E2%80%936%2C_2025_United_States_blizzard "January 5–6, 2025 United States blizzard")
  + The [National Weather Service](/wiki/National_Weather_Service "National Weather Service") issues [winter storm warnings](/wiki/Winter_storm_warning "Winter storm warning") across the central [Great Plains](/wiki/Great_Plains "Great Plains") and an [ice storm warning](/wiki/Ice_storm_warning "Ice storm warning") in [Missouri](/wiki/Missouri "Missouri"), in anticipation of severe [freezing rain](/wiki/Freezing_rain "Freezing rain") and [icing events](/wiki/Ice_storm "Ice storm"). The winter storm begins impacting the northwestern [continental United States](/wiki/Contiguous_United_States "Contiguous United States") with heavy snowfall. [(*The Weather Channel*)](https://weather.com/storms/winter/news/2025-01-02-winter-storm-blair-forecast-snow-ice-plains-midwest-mid-atlantic)
* [2024–25 Ethiopian earthquakes](/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_Ethiopian_earthquakes "2024–25 Ethiopian earthquakes")
  + Evacuations are ordered in central [Ethiopia](/wiki/Ethiopia "Ethiopia") due to increasing [volcanic tremor](/wiki/Harmonic_tremor "Harmonic tremor") and other unrest at the [Mount Fentale](/wiki/Mount_Fentale "Mount Fentale") stratovolcano, which last erupted in the 19th century. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/risk-ethiopian-volcano-eruption-prompts-evacuation-residents-2025-01-03/)
* At least twelve people are killed and 30 others are injured after a bus carrying tourists falls into a ravine near the [Pan-American Highway](/wiki/Pan-American_Highway "Pan-American Highway") between [Pasto](/wiki/Pasto%2C_Colombia "Pasto, Colombia") and [Rumichaca](/wiki/Rumichaca_Bridge "Rumichaca Bridge") in [Nariño Department](/wiki/Nari%C3%B1o_Department "Nariño Department"), [Colombia](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia"). [(EFE)](https://efe.com/mundo/2025-01-04/colombia-accidente-autobus/)

**Health and environment**

* [Air quality technology company](/wiki/Air_quality_index "Air quality index") [IQAir](/wiki/IQAir "IQAir") reports that [Hanoi](/wiki/Hanoi "Hanoi"), [Vietnam](/wiki/Vietnam "Vietnam"), has the worst [air pollution](/wiki/Air_pollution "Air pollution") of any city on [Earth](/wiki/Earth "Earth"), with levels of hazardous small particles, known as [PM2.5](/wiki/Particulate_pollution "Particulate pollution"), measured at 266 micrograms per cubic metre. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/hanoi-declared-worlds-most-polluted-city-authorities-seek-action-2025-01-03/)

**International relations**

* [Egypt–Syria relations](/wiki/Egypt%E2%80%93Syria_relations "Egypt–Syria relations")
  + [Egypt](/wiki/Egypt "Egypt") bans the entry of [Syrians](/wiki/Syrians "Syrians") from all countries worldwide, except for those holding temporary residency permits for non-tourism purposes. The ban also includes Syrians married to Egyptians unless they obtain a [security clearance](/wiki/Security_clearance "Security clearance"). [(*The New Arab*)](https://www.newarab.com/news/egypt-bans-entry-syrians-anywhere-world)
* [Germany–Syria relations](/wiki/Germany%E2%80%93Syria_relations "Germany–Syria relations"), [France–Syria relations](/wiki/France%E2%80%93Syria_relations "France–Syria relations")
  + [German Foreign Minister](/wiki/Foreign_Minister_of_Germany "Foreign Minister of Germany") [Annalena Baerbock](/wiki/Annalena_Baerbock "Annalena Baerbock") and [French Foreign Minister](/wiki/Foreign_minister_of_France "Foreign minister of France") [Jean-Noël Barrot](/wiki/Jean-No%C3%ABl_Barrot "Jean-Noël Barrot") become the first [European Union](/wiki/European_Union "European Union") foreign ministers to travel to [Damascus](/wiki/Damascus "Damascus"), [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria"), after the [fall of the Assad regime](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Assad_regime "Fall of the Assad regime") to discuss new diplomatic relations with the [Syrian Transitional Government](/wiki/First_Syrian_transitional_government "First Syrian transitional government") and Syrian civil society. [(*Der Spiegel*)](https://www.spiegel.de/politik/deutschland/syrien-annalena-baerbock-reist-als-erste-eu-aussenministerin-nach-damaskus-a-6884f1be-3006-454b-9664-3ee76c0eda2e) [(*France 24*)](https://www.france24.com/en/middle-east/20250103-french-fm-visits-syria-with-german-counterpart-to-promote-peaceful-transition)

**Law and crime**

* [2024 South Korean martial law crisis](/wiki/2024_South_Korean_martial_law_crisis "2024 South Korean martial law crisis")
  + [Arrest of Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Arrest_of_Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Arrest of Yoon Suk Yeol")
    - [Corruption investigators and prosecutors](/wiki/Corruption_Investigation_Office_for_High-ranking_Officials "Corruption Investigation Office for High-ranking Officials") raid the central [Seoul](/wiki/Seoul "Seoul") residence of [recently-impeached](/wiki/Impeachment_of_Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Impeachment of Yoon Suk Yeol") [South Korean President](/wiki/President_of_South_Korea "President of South Korea") [Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Yoon Suk Yeol") to arrest Yoon for refusing to respond to three [court summons](/wiki/Summons "Summons"). The raid is unsuccessful due to the [Presidential Security Service](/wiki/Presidential_Security_Service_%28South_Korea%29 "Presidential Security Service (South Korea)") blocking further entrance into the residence, leading to a multi-hour standoff. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/world/live/2025/jan/02/south-korea-police-on-way-to-arrest-president-yoon-suk-yeol-latest-updates?filterKeyEvents=false#maincontent) [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/south-korea-yoon-martial-law-impeachment-detention-c8dc1758647979455dbf0d56e70369a4)
* [2024 Estlink 2 incident](/wiki/2024_Estlink_2_incident "2024 Estlink 2 incident")
  + A [district court](/wiki/Judicial_system_of_Finland#District_Courts "Judicial system of Finland") in [Helsinki](/wiki/Helsinki "Helsinki"), [Finland](/wiki/Finland "Finland"), denies a request to release the [impounded](/wiki/Vehicle_impoundment "Vehicle impoundment") oil tanker *[Eagle S](/wiki/Eagle_S "Eagle S")*, suspected of damaging the [Estlink 2](/wiki/Estlink_2 "Estlink 2") [submarine power cable](/wiki/Submarine_power_cable "Submarine power cable") and carrying [sanctioned Russian oil](/wiki/Embargo_of_Russian_oil_during_the_Russo-Ukrainian_War "Embargo of Russian oil during the Russo-Ukrainian War"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/3/finnish-court-upholds-oil-tanker-seizure-in-undersea-cables-probe)
* [War crimes in the Syrian civil war](/wiki/War_crimes_in_the_Syrian_civil_war "War crimes in the Syrian civil war")
  + The [Syrian government](/wiki/First_Syrian_transitional_government "First Syrian transitional government") arrests Aws Salloum, known as the "[Angel of Death](/wiki/Azrael "Azrael")" of [Sednaya Prison](/wiki/Sednaya_Prison "Sednaya Prison"). Salloum is accused of multiple [murders](/wiki/Murder "Murder") and [abuse](/wiki/Prisoner_abuse "Prisoner abuse") of prisoners at Sednaya, including the murder of [Mazen al-Hamada](/wiki/Mazen_al-Hamada "Mazen al-Hamada"). [(Al Sharq Al Awsat)](https://english.aawsat.com/arab-world/5097881-arrest-aws-salloum-what-we-know-about-%E2%80%98azrael-sednaya%E2%80%99)
* A suspect is arrested in [Rotterdam](/wiki/Rotterdam "Rotterdam"), [Netherlands](/wiki/Netherlands "Netherlands"), for shooting and killing three men between December 21 and January 2. The victims were selected at random. [(*The Sun*)](https://thesun.my/world-news/dutch-police-arrest-suspect-in-random-rotterdam-shootings-BO13480760)
* [Human trafficking in Southeast Asia](/wiki/Human_trafficking_in_Southeast_Asia "Human trafficking in Southeast Asia")
  + Chinese actor [Wang Xing went missing](/wiki/Disappearance_of_Wang_Xing "Disappearance of Wang Xing") at the Thailand-Myanmar border. He was rescued later (Jan 7) by Thai authorities. [(*The Star*)](https://www.thestar.com.my/lifestyle/entertainment/2025/01/08/chinese-actor-wang-xing-says-he-was-forcibly-shaved-and-trained-as-scammer-in-myanmar)

**Politics and elections**

* [2025 Speaker of the United States House of Representatives election](/wiki/2025_Speaker_of_the_United_States_House_of_Representatives_election "2025 Speaker of the United States House of Representatives election")
  + The [United States House of Representatives](/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives "United States House of Representatives"), composed of 219 [Republicans](/wiki/Republican_Party_%28United_States%29 "Republican Party (United States)") and 215 [Democrats](/wiki/Democratic_Party_%28United_States%29 "Democratic Party (United States)"), re-elects [Mike Johnson](/wiki/Mike_Johnson "Mike Johnson") as [House Speaker](/wiki/Speaker_of_the_United_States_House_of_Representatives "Speaker of the United States House of Representatives") over incumbent [House Minority Leader](/wiki/Party_leaders_of_the_United_States_House_of_Representatives "Party leaders of the United States House of Representatives") [Hakeem Jeffries](/wiki/Hakeem_Jeffries "Hakeem Jeffries"). [(CBS News)](https://www.cbsnews.com/live-updates/2025-new-congress-sworn-in/)
* [Next Ukrainian presidential election](/wiki/Next_Ukrainian_presidential_election "Next Ukrainian presidential election")
  + [Ukrainian President](/wiki/President_of_Ukraine "President of Ukraine") [Volodymyr Zelenskyy](/wiki/Volodymyr_Zelenskyy "Volodymyr Zelenskyy") says that the country will not hold [presidential elections](/wiki/Ukrainian_presidential_elections "Ukrainian presidential elections") as long as the country is under [martial law](/wiki/Martial_law_in_Ukraine "Martial law in Ukraine"), even if [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia") puts it as a pre-condition for negotiations. [(*Kyiv Independent*)](https://kyivindependent.com/zelensky-again-rejects-elections-under-martial-law/)
* [Pula Nikolao Pula](/wiki/Pula_Nikolao_Pula "Pula Nikolao Pula") is sworn in as [Governor of American Samoa](/wiki/Governor_of_American_Samoa "Governor of American Samoa"). [(Samoa Observer)](https://www.samoaobserver.ws/category/samoa/112622)

**Science and technology**

* [SpaceX](/wiki/SpaceX "SpaceX") successfully launches the [United Arab Emirates Space Agency](/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates_Space_Agency "United Arab Emirates Space Agency")'s [communications satellite](/wiki/Communications_satellite "Communications satellite") [Thuraya 4-NGS](/wiki/Thuraya "Thuraya") via a [Falcon 9](/wiki/Falcon_9 "Falcon 9") rocket from [Cape Canaveral Space Force Station](/wiki/Cape_Canaveral_Space_Force_Station "Cape Canaveral Space Force Station"), [Florida](/wiki/Florida "Florida"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"). [(Space News)](https://spacenews.com/spacex-launches-uaes-thuraya-4-mobile-connectivity-satellite/)

**Sports**

* [2025 PDC World Darts Championship](/wiki/2025_PDC_World_Darts_Championship "2025 PDC World Darts Championship")
  + [Luke Littler](/wiki/Luke_Littler "Luke Littler") defeats [Michael van Gerwen](/wiki/Michael_van_Gerwen "Michael van Gerwen") 7–3 in the final at [Alexandra Palace](/wiki/Alexandra_Palace "Alexandra Palace") in [London](/wiki/London "London"), [England](/wiki/England "England"), to claim his first [World Darts Championship](/wiki/PDC_World_Darts_Championship "PDC World Darts Championship") title, becoming the youngest player to win a world title at the age of 17 years. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.co.uk/sport/darts/live/c4gwz153e7et)

January 4, 2025 (2025-01-04) (Saturday)
