**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Eastern Ukraine campaign](/wiki/Eastern_Ukraine_campaign "Eastern Ukraine campaign"), [Journalists killed during the Russo-Ukrainian War](/wiki/List_of_journalists_killed_during_the_Russo-Ukrainian_War "List of journalists killed during the Russo-Ukrainian War")
    - A [war correspondent](/wiki/War_correspondent "War correspondent") for the [Russian](/wiki/Russia "Russia") newspaper *[Izvestia](/wiki/Izvestia "Izvestia")* is killed in a [Ukrainian](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_Ukraine "Armed Forces of Ukraine") [drone strike](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") in [Donetsk Oblast](/wiki/Donetsk_Oblast "Donetsk Oblast"), [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/russias-izvestia-says-reporter-killed-drone-strike-eastern-ukraine-2025-01-04/)
  + The [Russian Armed Forces](/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces "Russian Armed Forces") claims to have shot down eight [American](/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces "United States Armed Forces") [ATACMS](/wiki/ATACMS "ATACMS") missiles fired by Ukraine and vows retaliation. [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/04/europe/russia-retaliation-eight-atacms-missiles-intl/index.html)
* [Haitian crisis](/wiki/Haitian_crisis_%282018%E2%80%93present%29 "Haitian crisis (2018–present)"), [Guatemala–Haiti relations](/wiki/Guatemala%E2%80%93Haiti_relations "Guatemala–Haiti relations")
  + [Gang war in Haiti](/wiki/Gang_war_in_Haiti "Gang war in Haiti")
    - Another 75 [Guatemalan Army](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_Guatemala "Armed Forces of Guatemala") troops arrive in [Haiti](/wiki/Haiti "Haiti"), joining 75 that arrived yesterday, to combat escalating gang violence. [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/01/03/americas/haiti-gang-violence-guatemala-el-salvador-soldiers-intl-latam/index.html) [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c2ld49lqq5qo)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip](/wiki/Israeli_invasion_of_the_Gaza_Strip "Israeli invasion of the Gaza Strip")
    - At least 70 [Palestinians](/wiki/Palestinians "Palestinians") are killed and 14 others are reported missing in [Israeli](/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force "Israeli Air Force") airstrikes on [Gaza City](/wiki/Gaza_City "Gaza City") and [Khan Younis](/wiki/Khan_Yunis "Khan Yunis") in the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip"). [(Middle East Monitor)](https://www.middleeastmonitor.com/20250104-27-palestinians-killed-14-missing-from-israeli-airstrikes-on-gaza/) [(*India Today*)](https://www.indiatoday.in/world/story/israel-hamas-war-70-dead-injured-in-fresh-strikes-2659873-2025-01-05)
* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [M23 offensive](/wiki/M23_offensive_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "M23 offensive (2022–present)")
    - [M23 rebels](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") capture the strategic town of Katale in [Masisi Territory](/wiki/Masisi_Territory "Masisi Territory"), [North Kivu Province](/wiki/North_Kivu_Province "North Kivu Province"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"). [(Chimp Reports)](https://chimpreports.com/drc-m23-rebels-capture-strategic-town-of-katale-in-masisi-territory/)
* [Anglophone Crisis](/wiki/Anglophone_Crisis "Anglophone Crisis")
  + Gunmen from [Nigeria](/wiki/Nigeria "Nigeria") kill at least five [Cameroonian soldiers](/wiki/Army_of_Cameroon "Army of Cameroon") and injure several others in Bakinjaw, [Southwest Region](/wiki/Southwest_Region_%28Cameroon%29 "Southwest Region (Cameroon)"), [Cameroon](/wiki/Cameroon "Cameroon"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/gunmen-nigeria-kill-five-cameroonian-soldiers-mp-says-2025-01-04/)
* [Insurgency in Balochistan](/wiki/Insurgency_in_Balochistan "Insurgency in Balochistan")
  + One person is killed and 35 others are injured, including [soldiers](/wiki/Pakistan_Armed_Forces "Pakistan Armed Forces"), in a [car bombing](/wiki/Car_bomb "Car bomb") in [Turbat](/wiki/Turbat "Turbat"), [Balochistan](/wiki/Balochistan "Balochistan"), [Pakistan](/wiki/Pakistan "Pakistan"). The [Balochistan Liberation Army](/wiki/Balochistan_Liberation_Army "Balochistan Liberation Army") claims responsibility for the attack, which states it targeted a military convoy. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/pakistan-balochistan-turbat-explosion-soldiers-72c4df692f4f0950d882d1b3961c32f2)
* [Boko Haram insurgency](/wiki/Boko_Haram_insurgency "Boko Haram insurgency")
  + The [Nigerian Army](/wiki/Nigerian_Army "Nigerian Army") repels an ambush in [Borno State](/wiki/Borno_State "Borno State") and kills 34 Islamist militants in a gun battle in which six soldiers also die. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/nigerian-troops-repel-boko-haram-ambush-borno-kill-34-insurgents-2025-01-08/)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [January 2025 North American storm complex](/wiki/January_2025_North_American_storm_complex "January 2025 North American storm complex")
  + [Kentucky Governor](/wiki/Governor_of_Kentucky "Governor of Kentucky") [Andy Beshear](/wiki/Andy_Beshear "Andy Beshear") declares a [state of emergency](/wiki/State_of_emergency "State of emergency") for [Kentucky](/wiki/Kentucky "Kentucky"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), amidst the upcoming winter storm. [(WNKY)](https://www.wnky.com/release-gov-beshear-declares-state-of-emergency-ahead-of-winter-storm-system/)
* At least eight people are killed and 15 others are injured in a fire at a market in [Zhangjiakou](/wiki/Zhangjiakou "Zhangjiakou"), [Hebei](/wiki/Hebei "Hebei"), [China](/wiki/China "China"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/4/fire-at-market-in-hebei-china-kills-and-wounds-several-people)
* The [Taiwanese Coast Guard](/wiki/Coast_Guard_Administration_%28Taiwan%29 "Coast Guard Administration (Taiwan)") intercepts the [Cameroon](/wiki/Cameroon "Cameroon")-registered [container ship](/wiki/Container_ship "Container ship") *Shunxin39* after it was suspected of damaging an undersea cable north of [Taiwan](/wiki/Taiwan "Taiwan") yesterday. [(Taiwan News)](https://www.taiwannews.com.tw/)
* A fishing boat ran aground near [Gageodo](/wiki/Gageodo "Gageodo"), [South Korea](/wiki/South_Korea "South Korea") after colliding with coastal rocks. Three people were killed, 19 were rescued. [(NOS)](https://nos.nl/artikel/2550531)

**Law and crime**

* [Myanmar](/wiki/Myanmar "Myanmar") [state media](/wiki/Media_in_Myanmar "Media in Myanmar") reports that the [ruling military junta](/wiki/State_Administration_Council "State Administration Council") will release 5,864 prisoners, including 180 foreigners, under an amnesty marking the country's [national independence day](/wiki/Independence_Day_%28Myanmar%29 "Independence Day (Myanmar)"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/myanmar-junta-free-5864-prisoners-under-amnesty-2025-01-04/)
* The [Danish](/wiki/Denmark "Denmark") [Security and Intelligence Service](/wiki/Danish_Security_and_Intelligence_Service "Danish Security and Intelligence Service") and [police](/wiki/Police_of_Denmark "Police of Denmark") announce an investigation into sightings of unknown [drones](/wiki/UFO "UFO") reportedly flying over [Køge](/wiki/K%C3%B8ge "Køge"), [Region Zealand](/wiki/Region_Zealand "Region Zealand"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/danish-police-investigate-mystery-drone-sightings/a-71217317)
* Four teenagers are arrested in [Yekaterinburg](/wiki/Yekaterinburg "Yekaterinburg"), [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia"), for allegedly planning a [terrorist](/wiki/Terrorism "Terrorism") attack in the city. Two of the suspects are also accused of being involved in an [arson attack](/wiki/Arson_attack "Arson attack") on a [Ministry of Internal Affairs](/wiki/Ministry_of_Internal_Affairs_%28Russia%29 "Ministry of Internal Affairs (Russia)") vehicle in December. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/russia-four-arrested-for-plotting-terrorist-attack/a-71216812)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024–2025 Georgian protests](/wiki/2024%E2%80%932025_Georgian_protests "2024–2025 Georgian protests"), [2024–2025 Georgian constitutional crisis](/wiki/2024%E2%80%932025_Georgian_constitutional_crisis "2024–2025 Georgian constitutional crisis")
  + [Georgia](/wiki/Georgia_%28country%29 "Georgia (country)")'s [Ministry of Internal Affairs](/wiki/Ministry_of_Internal_Affairs_of_Georgia "Ministry of Internal Affairs of Georgia") announces the expulsion of 91 foreign citizens, including 25 who participated in anti-[Georgian Dream](/wiki/Georgian_Dream "Georgian Dream") and pro-[EU](/wiki/European_Union "European Union") protests. [(TVP World)](https://tvpworld.com/84360400/georgia-deports-foreigners-amid-anti-government-protests)
* [2024–2025 Austrian government formation](/wiki/2024_Austrian_legislative_election#Government_formation "2024 Austrian legislative election")
  + [Austrian Chancellor](/wiki/Federal_Chancellor_of_Austria "Federal Chancellor of Austria") [Karl Nehammer](/wiki/Karl_Nehammer "Karl Nehammer") announces his resignation after talks on forming the new [post-election](/wiki/2024_Austrian_legislative_election "2024 Austrian legislative election") coalition government between his [Austrian People's Party](/wiki/Austrian_People%27s_Party "Austrian People's Party"), the [Social Democratic Party](/wiki/Social_Democratic_Party_of_Austria "Social Democratic Party of Austria") and [NEOS](/wiki/NEOS_%28Austria%29 "NEOS (Austria)") collapsed. [(Euronews)](https://www.euronews.com/my-europe/2025/01/04/the-austrian-chancelor-karl-nehammer-resignes-after-talks-on-forming-a-government-collapse)

January 5, 2025 (2025-01-05) (Sunday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_5&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_5&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_5&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Kursk offensive](/wiki/Kursk_offensive_%282024%E2%80%93present%29 "Kursk offensive (2024–present)")
    - The [Ukrainian Army](/wiki/Army_of_Ukraine "Army of Ukraine") launches a new offensive in [Kursk Oblast](/wiki/Kursk_Oblast "Kursk Oblast"), [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c86wz0vd1dwo)
* [Boko Haram insurgency](/wiki/Boko_Haram_insurgency "Boko Haram insurgency")
  + Six [soldiers](/wiki/Nigerian_Armed_Forces "Nigerian Armed Forces") and 34 [Boko Haram](/wiki/Boko_Haram "Boko Haram") gunmen are killed during a [shootout](/wiki/Shootout "Shootout") in [Borno State](/wiki/Borno_State "Borno State"), [Nigeria](/wiki/Nigeria "Nigeria"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/nigeria-borno-extremists-boko-haram-clash-237e12f721343e21253a4ce60fd78201)

**Arts and culture**

* [82nd Golden Globe Awards](/wiki/82nd_Golden_Globe_Awards "82nd Golden Globe Awards")
  + The film *[Emilia Pérez](/wiki/Emilia_P%C3%A9rez "Emilia Pérez")* and the television series *[Shōgun](/wiki/Sh%C5%8Dgun_%282024_TV_series%29 "Shōgun (2024 TV series)")* win the most awards at the 82nd Golden Globes with four each. *[The Brutalist](/wiki/The_Brutalist "The Brutalist")* wins the awards for [Best Motion Picture – Drama](/wiki/Golden_Globe_Award_for_Best_Motion_Picture_%E2%80%93_Drama "Golden Globe Award for Best Motion Picture – Drama"), [Best Director](/wiki/Golden_Globe_Award_for_Best_Director "Golden Globe Award for Best Director") ([Brady Corbet](/wiki/Brady_Corbet "Brady Corbet")) and [Best Actor in a Motion Picture – Drama](/wiki/Golden_Globe_Award_for_Best_Actor_in_a_Motion_Picture_%E2%80%93_Drama "Golden Globe Award for Best Actor in a Motion Picture – Drama") for [Adrien Brody](/wiki/Adrien_Brody "Adrien Brody"). [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/pop-culture/pop-culture-news/golden-globes-2025-winners-complete-list-rcna186300)
  + [Fernanda Torres](/wiki/Fernanda_Torres "Fernanda Torres") becomes the first [Brazilian](/wiki/Brazilians "Brazilians") actress to win the award for [Best Actress in a Motion Picture – Drama](/wiki/Golden_Globe_Award_for_Best_Actress_in_a_Motion_Picture_%E2%80%93_Drama "Golden Globe Award for Best Actress in a Motion Picture – Drama") for her performance in *[I'm Still Here](/wiki/I%27m_Still_Here_%282024_film%29 "I'm Still Here (2024 film)")*. [(Variety)](https://variety.com/2025/film/news/fernanda-torres-golden-globes-best-actress-drama-film-1236262309/)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [January 2025 North American storm complex](/wiki/January_2025_North_American_storm_complex "January 2025 North American storm complex")
  + The [National Weather Service](/wiki/National_Weather_Service "National Weather Service") issues [winter storm alerts](/wiki/Winter_storm_warning "Winter storm warning") for areas covering nearly 70 million people from the [Great Plains](/wiki/Great_Plains "Great Plains") to the [East Coast](/wiki/East_Coast_of_the_United_States "East Coast of the United States") of the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), with nearly 4 million currently under [blizzard warnings](/wiki/Blizzard_warning "Blizzard warning"). [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/01/05/weather/winter-storm-weather-weekend/index.html)

**International relations**

* [Israel–United States relations](/wiki/Israel%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Israel–United States relations"), [United States support for Israel in the Israel-Hamas war](/wiki/United_States_support_for_Israel_in_the_Israel-Hamas_war "United States support for Israel in the Israel-Hamas war")
  + The [U.S. State Department](/wiki/United_States_Department_of_State "United States Department of State") notifies [Congress](/wiki/United_States_Congress "United States Congress") of a planned [$](/wiki/United_States_dollar "United States dollar")8 billion arms sale to [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel") consisting of [air-to-air](/wiki/Air-to-air_missile "Air-to-air missile") and [Hellfire](/wiki/AGM-114_Hellfire "AGM-114 Hellfire") [missiles](/wiki/Missile "Missile"), [artillery shells](/wiki/Shell_%28projectile%29 "Shell (projectile)"), and other [ammunitions](/wiki/Ammunition "Ammunition"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cpvne94v1rdo)

**Law and crime**

* [Capital punishment in the Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Capital punishment in the Democratic Republic of the Congo")
  + The [Congolese government](/wiki/Government_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Government of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") [executes](/wiki/Capital_punishment "Capital punishment") 102 individuals convicted of armed robbery and [urban banditry](/wiki/Banditry "Banditry"), with an additional 70 prisoners reportedly awaiting execution. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/congo-executes-kulunas-bandits-dc460aa0fc69489f2c1005b33796e0c9)
* Former [Ecuadorian Vice President](/wiki/Vice_President_of_Ecuador "Vice President of Ecuador") [Jorge Glas](/wiki/Jorge_Glas "Jorge Glas") is evacuated from [La Roca Prison](/wiki/Litoral_Penitentiary "Litoral Penitentiary") in [Guayaquil](/wiki/Guayaquil "Guayaquil") following an alleged [assassination attempt](/wiki/Assassination_attempt "Assassination attempt"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/ecuadors-ex-vp-glas-evacuated-prison-after-attempted-killing-lawyer-says-2025-01-05/)
* Resurfaced videos show [Syrian](/wiki/Syria "Syria") [Justice Minister](/wiki/Ministry_of_Justice_%28Syria%29 "Ministry of Justice (Syria)") [Shadi al-Waisi](/wiki/Shadi_al-Waisi "Shadi al-Waisi") overseeing the execution of two women in 2015 on [prostitution](/wiki/Prostitution "Prostitution") charges according to [Sharia](/wiki/Sharia "Sharia"). [(The New Arab)](https://www.newarab.com/news/syrian-minister-oversaw-execution-women-prostitution)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024–2025 Austrian government formation](/wiki/2024_Austrian_legislative_election#Government_formation "2024 Austrian legislative election")
  + The ruling [Austrian People's Party](/wiki/Austrian_People%27s_Party "Austrian People's Party") appoints [Christian Stocker](/wiki/Christian_Stocker "Christian Stocker") as its acting chairman to succeed [Karl Nehammer](/wiki/Karl_Nehammer "Karl Nehammer"), who resigned as party leader and [Chancellor of Austria](/wiki/Federal_Chancellor_of_Austria "Federal Chancellor of Austria") yesterday. Stocker says that he is open to negotiate with the [Freedom Party of Austria](/wiki/Freedom_Party_of_Austria "Freedom Party of Austria") to form the new [post-election](/wiki/2024_Austrian_legislative_election "2024 Austrian legislative election") coalition government. [(DNYUZ)](https://dnyuz.com/2025/01/05/new-austrian-conservative-leader-ready-for-coalition-talks-with-far-right/)
* The [German government](/wiki/Cabinet_of_Germany "Cabinet of Germany") reduces funding for two [Israeli](/wiki/Israel "Israel") [human rights groups](/wiki/Human_rights_group "Human rights group"), [Zochrot](/wiki/Zochrot "Zochrot") and [New Profile](/wiki/New_Profile "New Profile"), that had advocated for [Palestinian rights](/wiki/Pro-Palestine "Pro-Palestine") and [antimilitarism](/wiki/Antimilitarism "Antimilitarism"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/germany-defunds-2-israeli-human-rights-groups/a-71217628)

**Sports**

* [2025 United Cup](/wiki/2025_United_Cup "2025 United Cup")
  + In [tennis](/wiki/Tennis "Tennis"), the [United States](/wiki/Tennis_in_the_United_States "Tennis in the United States") wins its second [United Cup](/wiki/United_Cup "United Cup") title after defeating [Poland](/wiki/Sport_in_Poland "Sport in Poland") 2–0 in the final at the [Ken Rosewall Arena](/wiki/Ken_Rosewall_Arena "Ken Rosewall Arena") in [Sydney](/wiki/Sydney "Sydney"), [Australia](/wiki/Australia "Australia"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/sports/tennis/united-states-claim-second-united-cup-title-with-win-over-poland-2025-01-05/)

January 6, 2025 (2025-01-06) (Monday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_6&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_6&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_6&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Islamist insurgency in the Sahel](/wiki/Islamist_insurgency_in_the_Sahel "Islamist insurgency in the Sahel")
  + [French military withdrawal from West Africa](/wiki/French_military_withdrawal_from_West_Africa_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "French military withdrawal from West Africa (2022–present)")
    - [French President](/wiki/President_of_France "President of France") [Emmanuel Macron](/wiki/Emmanuel_Macron "Emmanuel Macron") says [France](/wiki/France "France") was right to intervene militarily in the [African](/wiki/Africa "Africa") [Sahel](/wiki/Sahel "Sahel") against the [mujahideen](/wiki/Mujahideen "Mujahideen"), that he is still waiting for the Sahel states to thank France and that the [French Armed Forces](/wiki/French_Armed_Forces "French Armed Forces") were not forced out. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/still-awaiting-thanks-stopping-islamists-sahel-macron-says-2025-01-06/)
* [Israeli–Palestinian conflict](/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict "Israeli–Palestinian conflict")
  + [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war"), [Israeli incursions in the West Bank](/wiki/Israeli_incursions_in_the_West_Bank_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Israeli incursions in the West Bank (2023–present)")
    - [2025 al-Funduq shooting](/wiki/2025_al-Funduq_shooting "2025 al-Funduq shooting")
      * Three [Israelis](/wiki/Israelis "Israelis") are killed and eight others are injured in a [mass shooting](/wiki/Mass_shooting "Mass shooting") by [Palestinian gunmen](/wiki/Palestinian_political_violence "Palestinian political violence") firing at a bus and two vehicles on [Highway 55](/wiki/Highway_55_%28Israel%29 "Highway 55 (Israel)") in [Al-Funduq](/wiki/Al-Funduq "Al-Funduq") in the [West Bank](/wiki/West_Bank "West Bank"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cdjgv1r4x81o)
* [Naxalite–Maoist insurgency](/wiki/Naxalite%E2%80%93Maoist_insurgency "Naxalite–Maoist insurgency")
  + [2025 Bijapur Naxal attack](/wiki/2025_Bijapur_Naxal_attack "2025 Bijapur Naxal attack")
    - A bomb blast attributed to [Maoist rebels](/wiki/Communist_Party_of_India_%28Maoist%29 "Communist Party of India (Maoist)") in [Bijapur](/wiki/Bijapur_district%2C_Chhattisgarh "Bijapur district, Chhattisgarh"), [Chhattisgarh](/wiki/Chhattisgarh "Chhattisgarh"), [India](/wiki/India "India"), kills eight [police](/wiki/Indian_Police_Service "Indian Police Service") officers and a driver traveling in a police vehicle. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/india/ten-policemen-feared-killed-bomb-blast-central-india-tv-report-says-2025-01-06/)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Kherson strikes](/wiki/Kherson_strikes_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "Kherson strikes (2022–present)"), [Attacks on civilians in the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Attacks_on_civilians_in_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Attacks on civilians in the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
    - A [Russian](/wiki/Russia "Russia") [drone attacks](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") a civilian passenger bus in [Kherson](/wiki/Kherson "Kherson"), [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"), reportedly killing at least one person and injuring at least nine others. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/russian-drone-kills-one-injures-nine-passenger-bus-ukraines-kherson-2025-01-06/)
* [2024 Magdeburg car attack](/wiki/2024_Magdeburg_car_attack "2024 Magdeburg car attack")
  + The death toll in the [vehicle-ramming attack](/wiki/Vehicle-ramming_attack "Vehicle-ramming attack") at the [Magdeburg Christmas market](/wiki/Magdeburg_Christmas_market "Magdeburg Christmas market") in [Magdeburg](/wiki/Magdeburg "Magdeburg"), [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany"), on December 20, increases to six after a 52-year-old woman dies from injuries sustained in the attack. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cql5nlrp374o)
* [North Korean missile tests](/wiki/List_of_North_Korean_missile_tests "List of North Korean missile tests")
  + The [South Korean](/wiki/South_Korea "South Korea") [military](/wiki/Republic_of_Korea_Armed_Forces "Republic of Korea Armed Forces") reports that [North Korea](/wiki/Korean_People%27s_Army "Korean People's Army") has fired what appears to be an [intermediate-range ballistic missile](/wiki/Intermediate-range_ballistic_missile "Intermediate-range ballistic missile") toward the [Sea of Japan](/wiki/Sea_of_Japan "Sea of Japan"), in what would be [the country](/wiki/North_Korea "North Korea")'s first missile launch in two months. The launch comes as [U.S. Secretary of State](/wiki/U.S._Secretary_of_State "U.S. Secretary of State") [Antony Blinken](/wiki/Antony_Blinken "Antony Blinken") visits [Seoul](/wiki/Seoul "Seoul"), South Korea, for talks with South Korean leaders. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/crrwyv75g5xo)
* [Mexican drug war](/wiki/Mexican_drug_war "Mexican drug war")
  + At least eight gunmen are killed and three [policemen](/wiki/Federal_Police_%28Mexico%29 "Federal Police (Mexico)") are wounded after security agents repels an attack near the Buenavista de Libertad, [Yuriria](/wiki/Yuriria "Yuriria"), [Guanajuato](/wiki/Guanajuato "Guanajuato"), [Mexico](/wiki/Mexico "Mexico"). Security forces members seize four vehicles, ballistic vests, and twelve firearms. In the same area, another encounter was reported two months ago, leaving three officers wounded. [(*Revista Proceso*)](https://www.proceso.com.mx/nacional/estados/2025/1/6/fuerzas-de-seguridad-abaten-ocho-presuntos-criminales-en-yuriria-guanajuato-343294.html)
* Two people are killed and two others are injured in an [IED](/wiki/Improvised_explosive_device "Improvised explosive device") attack at a school near [Abuja](/wiki/Abuja "Abuja"), [Nigeria](/wiki/Nigeria "Nigeria"), with [police](/wiki/Nigeria_Police_Force "Nigeria Police Force") identifying three men as suspects in bringing the device to the site. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/suspected-bomb-explosion-kills-two-people-nigerian-school-police-say-2025-01-06/)

**Business and economy**

* [2022–2023 Russia–European Union gas dispute](/wiki/2022%E2%80%932023_Russia%E2%80%93European_Union_gas_dispute "2022–2023 Russia–European Union gas dispute")
  + According to [Slovakia](/wiki/Slovakia "Slovakia"), a planned meeting between Slovak, [Ukrainian](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"), and [European Commission](/wiki/European_Commission "European Commission") officials over gas supplies scheduled for Tuesday has been cancelled due to Ukraine's refusal to participate in the meeting. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/slovakia-says-gas-supply-meeting-with-ukraine-european-commission-cancelled-2025-01-06/)
* The [Brazilian government](/wiki/Politics_of_Brazil "Politics of Brazil") announces that [Indonesia](/wiki/Indonesia "Indonesia") has joined the [BRICS](/wiki/BRICS "BRICS") [trade bloc](/wiki/Trade_bloc "Trade bloc") as a full member. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/indonesia-join-brics-bloc-full-member-brazil-says-2025-01-06/)
* [Colombian](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia") bank [Davivienda](/wiki/Davivienda "Davivienda") and [Canadian](/wiki/Canada "Canada") bank [Scotiabank](/wiki/Scotiabank "Scotiabank") announces a [merger](/wiki/Mergers_and_acquisitions "Mergers and acquisitions") where Davivienda will absorb Scotiabank's operations in Colombia, [Costa Rica](/wiki/Costa_Rica "Costa Rica") and [Panama](/wiki/Panama "Panama"), and, Scotiabank will acquire 20% of Davidienda's stakes. [(Scotiabank)](https://www.scotiabank.com/corporate/en/home/media-centre/media-centre/news-release.html.html?id=4186&language=en)

**Disasters and accidents**

* 18 people are killed in a multi-vehicle collision on [Van Reenen's Pass](/wiki/Van_Reenen%27s_Pass "Van Reenen's Pass") in [KwaZulu-Natal](/wiki/KwaZulu-Natal "KwaZulu-Natal"), [South Africa](/wiki/South_Africa "South Africa"). [(ENCA)](https://www.enca.com/news/18-killed-multi-vehicle-crash-van-reenens-pass)
* Several miners are trapped in a [coal mine](/wiki/Coal_mine "Coal mine") in [Dima Hasao](/wiki/Dima_Hasao_district "Dima Hasao district"), [Assam](/wiki/Assam "Assam"), India, with rescue efforts underway involving the [State Disaster Response Force](/wiki/State_Disaster_Response_Force_%28Assam%29 "State Disaster Response Force (Assam)"), the [National Disaster Response Force](/wiki/National_Disaster_Response_Force "National Disaster Response Force"), and the [Indian Army](/wiki/Indian_Army "Indian Army"). Local authorities state that flooding may have caused the incident. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/india/several-miners-trapped-coal-mine-indias-assam-2025-01-06/)

**Health and environment**

* [2020–2025 H5N1 outbreak](/wiki/2020%E2%80%932025_H5N1_outbreak "2020–2025 H5N1 outbreak")
  + The [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") reports its first death from [H5N1](/wiki/H5N1 "H5N1") bird flu after a man died in the hospital in [Louisiana](/wiki/Louisiana "Louisiana"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/louisiana-reports-first-bird-flu-related-death-us-state-agency-says-2025-01-06/)

**International relations**

* [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war")
  + [Humanitarian aid during the Syrian civil war](/wiki/Humanitarian_aid_during_the_Syrian_civil_war "Humanitarian aid during the Syrian civil war")
    - The [International Committee of the Red Cross](/wiki/International_Committee_of_the_Red_Cross "International Committee of the Red Cross") announces plans to expand its operations in [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria") beyond an initial [US$](/wiki/United_States_dollar "United States dollar")100 million program, citing urgent needs in the [health](/wiki/Health_in_Syria "Health in Syria"), [water](/wiki/Water_supply_and_sanitation_in_Syria "Water supply and sanitation in Syria"), and [power sectors](/wiki/Energy_in_Syria "Energy in Syria"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/icrc-expand-syria-humanitarian-efforts-beyond-100-mln-programme-2025-01-06/)
* [International reactions to the 2024 Venezuelan presidential election](/wiki/International_reactions_to_the_2024_Venezuelan_presidential_election "International reactions to the 2024 Venezuelan presidential election"), [Paraguay–Venezuela relations](/wiki/Paraguay%E2%80%93Venezuela_relations "Paraguay–Venezuela relations")
  + The [Venezuelan](/wiki/Venezuela "Venezuela") government suspends diplomatic relations with [Paraguay](/wiki/Paraguay "Paraguay"), after [Paraguayan President](/wiki/President_of_Paraguay "President of Paraguay") [Santiago Peña](/wiki/Santiago_Pe%C3%B1a "Santiago Peña") recognizes [Edmundo González](/wiki/Edmundo_Gonz%C3%A1lez "Edmundo González") as [president-elect of Venezuela](/wiki/President_of_Venezuela "President of Venezuela"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/venezuela-breaks-diplomatic-relations-with-paraguay-2025-01-06/)

**Law and crime**

* [Volksverhetzung](/wiki/Volksverhetzung "Volksverhetzung")
  + [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany") reports a significant increase in [far-right](/wiki/Far-right_politics "Far-right politics") crime, primarily from increasing [online expression offenses](/wiki/Online_hate_speech "Online hate speech") and [hate speech](/wiki/Hate_speech "Hate speech"), as well as an increase in [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")-related resentment. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/germany-sees-rise-far-right-crime-with-online-offences-main-driver-2025-01-06/)
* The [Court of Appeal of Malaysia](/wiki/Court_of_Appeal_of_Malaysia "Court of Appeal of Malaysia") orders a [lower court](/wiki/Judiciary_of_Malaysia "Judiciary of Malaysia") to reconsider former [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Malaysia "Prime Minister of Malaysia") [Najib Razak](/wiki/Najib_Razak "Najib Razak")'s claim of a royal order granting him [home detention](/wiki/Home_detention "Home detention"), which he alleges was issued alongside his reduced prison sentence for his involvement in the [1MDB corruption scandal](/wiki/1MDB_corruption_scandal "1MDB corruption scandal"). The ruling follows the disclosure of a letter confirming the existence of such an order, which the [government](/wiki/Government_of_Malaysia "Government of Malaysia") asserts they have not received. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/malaysia-court-grants-jailed-ex-pm-najibs-request-see-document-he-says-allows-2025-01-06/)
* [Venezuelan Interior Minister](/wiki/Ministry_of_Interior%2C_Justice_and_Peace_%28Venezuela%29 "Ministry of Interior, Justice and Peace (Venezuela)") [Diosdado Cabello](/wiki/Diosdado_Cabello "Diosdado Cabello") says that 125 foreign citizens have been arrested on suspicion of serving as [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") [mercenaries](/wiki/Mercenaries "Mercenaries") in order to cause a [coup](/wiki/Coup "Coup") in Venezuela. [(*The Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/venezuela-says-125-foreigners-including-one-israeli-arrested-on-suspicion-of-being-us-mercenaries/)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024 Austrian legislative election](/wiki/2024_Austrian_legislative_election "2024 Austrian legislative election")
  + After the [Austrian People's Party](/wiki/Austrian_People%27s_Party "Austrian People's Party") fails to form a government, [President of Austria](/wiki/President_of_Austria "President of Austria") [Alexander van der Bellen](/wiki/Alexander_van_der_Bellen "Alexander van der Bellen") gives the mandate to form a [post-election](/wiki/2024_Austrian_legislative_election "2024 Austrian legislative election") government to the [Freedom Party](/wiki/Freedom_Party_of_Austria "Freedom Party of Austria")'s leader [Herbert Kickl](/wiki/Herbert_Kickl "Herbert Kickl"), who is expected to rule within a coalition of the two parties. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/de/van-der-bellen-erteilt-fp%C3%B6-auftrag-zur-regierungsbildung/a-71227474)
* [Conscription in Israel](/wiki/Conscription_in_Israel "Conscription in Israel"), [Exemption from military service in Israel](/wiki/Exemption_from_military_service_in_Israel "Exemption from military service in Israel")
  + More than 50 [Haredi Jews](/wiki/Haredi_Judaism "Haredi Judaism") join the [Israel Defense Forces](/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces "Israel Defense Forces") for the first time since the start of the [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war"), forming the Haredi [Hasmonean Brigade](/wiki/Hasmonean_Brigade "Hasmonean Brigade"), after repeated protests against the [conscription of yeshiva students](/wiki/Conscription_of_yeshiva_students "Conscription of yeshiva students"). [(*The Economic Times*)](https://economictimes.indiatimes.com/news/international/us/israel-defense-forces-recruit-first-ultra-orthodox-soldiers-for-hasmonean-brigade/articleshow/117000437.cms?from=mdr)
* [Proposals for the United States to purchase Greenland](/wiki/Proposals_for_the_United_States_to_purchase_Greenland "Proposals for the United States to purchase Greenland")
  + The [King of Denmark](/wiki/Frederik_X "Frederik X") officially changes the [Danish coat of arms](/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_Denmark "Coat of arms of Denmark") to feature [Greenland](/wiki/Greenland "Greenland") and the [Faroe Islands](/wiki/Faroe_Islands "Faroe Islands") more prominently, following suggestions from [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") [president-elect](/wiki/President-elect_of_the_United_States "President-elect of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") about the nation purchasing Greenland. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/jan/06/danish-king-changes-coat-of-arms-in-apparent-rebuke-to-donald-trump)
* [Resignation of Justin Trudeau](/wiki/Resignation_of_Justin_Trudeau "Resignation of Justin Trudeau")
  + [Canadian Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Canada "Prime Minister of Canada") [Justin Trudeau](/wiki/Justin_Trudeau "Justin Trudeau") announces his resignation as leader of the [Liberal Party](/wiki/Liberal_Party_of_Canada "Liberal Party of Canada") and also announces that he will resign as Prime Minister once [a new Liberal Party leader is chosen](/wiki/2025_Liberal_Party_of_Canada_leadership_election "2025 Liberal Party of Canada leadership election"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/live/clyjmy7vl64t)
* [Second presidential transition of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_presidential_transition_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidential transition of Donald Trump")
  + The [U.S. Congress](/wiki/United_States_Congress "United States Congress") [certifies](/wiki/2025_United_States_Electoral_College_vote_count "2025 United States Electoral College vote count") the results of the [2024 presidential election](/wiki/2024_United_States_presidential_election "2024 United States presidential election"). [U.S. Vice President](/wiki/Vice_President_of_the_United_States "Vice President of the United States") and [Democratic Party candidate](/wiki/Kamala_Harris_2024_presidential_campaign "Kamala Harris 2024 presidential campaign") in the [2024 presidential election](/wiki/2024_United_States_presidential_election "2024 United States presidential election"). [Kamala Harris](/wiki/Kamala_Harris "Kamala Harris") presides over the ceremony and certifies her defeat, officially making [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") the [President-elect](/wiki/President-elect_of_the_United_States "President-elect of the United States") and [JD Vance](/wiki/JD_Vance "JD Vance") the [Vice President-elect](/wiki/Vice_President-elect_of_the_United_States "Vice President-elect of the United States"). Trump and Vance are expected to be sworn-in on [January 20](/wiki/Second_inauguration_of_Donald_Trump "Second inauguration of Donald Trump"). [(ABC News)](https://abcnews.go.com/Politics/congress-meets-certify-trumps-2024-election-victory/story?id=117380065)
* [Pope Francis](/wiki/Pope_Francis "Pope Francis") appoints Sister [Simona Brambilla](/wiki/Simona_Brambilla "Simona Brambilla") as Prefect of the [Dicastery for Institutes of Consecrated Life and Societies of Apostolic Life](/wiki/Dicastery_for_Institutes_of_Consecrated_Life_and_Societies_of_Apostolic_Life "Dicastery for Institutes of Consecrated Life and Societies of Apostolic Life"), becoming the [Vatican](/wiki/Vatican_City "Vatican City")'s first female prefect of the [Roman Curia](/wiki/Roman_Curia "Roman Curia"). [(Vatican News)](https://www.vaticannews.va/en/pope/news/2025-01/vatican-first-female-prefect-simona-brambilla-consecrated-life.html)
* The [President of São Tomé and Príncipe](/wiki/President_of_S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "President of São Tomé and Príncipe"), [Carlos Vila Nova](/wiki/Carlos_Vila_Nova "Carlos Vila Nova"), dismisses the Government of [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "Prime Minister of São Tomé and Príncipe") [Patrice Trovoada](/wiki/Patrice_Trovoada "Patrice Trovoada"). [(Africa News)](https://www.africanews.com/2025/01/06/sao-tome-and-principe-president-dismisses-government-by-decree/)

January 7, 2025 (2025-01-07) (Tuesday)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Insurgency in Khyber Pakhtunkhwa](/wiki/Insurgency_in_Khyber_Pakhtunkhwa "Insurgency in Khyber Pakhtunkhwa")
  + Three [Pakistani soldiers](/wiki/Pakistan_Army "Pakistan Army") and 19 [Taliban](/wiki/Pakistani_Taliban "Pakistani Taliban") insurgents are killed in shootouts in [Khyber Pakhtunkhwa](/wiki/Khyber_Pakhtunkhwa "Khyber Pakhtunkhwa"), [Pakistan](/wiki/Pakistan "Pakistan"). **Business and economy**

* [Argentine debt restructuring](/wiki/Argentine_debt_restructuring "Argentine debt restructuring")
  + [Argentina](/wiki/Economy_of_Argentina "Economy of Argentina")'s [country risk](/wiki/Country_risk "Country risk") index, measured by the [JPMorgan GBI-EM Index](/wiki/JPMorgan_GBI-EM_Index "JPMorgan GBI-EM Index"), briefly drops to 444 points, its lowest level since 2018, before closing at 561 points due to technical adjustments linked to upcoming [bond](/wiki/Bond_%28finance%29 "Bond (finance)") payment amid improved [market sentiment](/wiki/Market_sentiment "Market sentiment") driven by cooling [inflation](/wiki/Inflation "Inflation") and signs of economic recovery. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/argentina-country-risk-plummets-lowest-level-since-may-2018-2025-01-07/)
* International flights resume from [Damascus International Airport](/wiki/Damascus_International_Airport "Damascus International Airport") in [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria") for the first time since the [fall of the Assad regime](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Assad_regime "Fall of the Assad regime"). [(France 24)](https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20250107-international-flights-resume-at-damascus-airport)
* The merger of the providers of [stock photography](/wiki/Stock_photography "Stock photography") [Getty Images](/wiki/Getty_Images "Getty Images") and [Shutterstock](/wiki/Shutterstock "Shutterstock"), by the acquisition of the latter by the former, is announced. [(AP News)](https://apnews.com/article/shutterstock-getty-images-e883ef74736e016315417c758ab17093)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - An exceptional [Santa Ana](/wiki/Santa_Ana_winds "Santa Ana winds") [wind event](/wiki/2025_Southern_California_windstorm "2025 Southern California windstorm") reaching hurricane-force in some locations in [southern](/wiki/Southern_California "Southern California") [California](/wiki/California "California"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), cause multiple [power outages](/wiki/Power_outage "Power outage") and [wildfire outbreaks](/wiki/Wildfire "Wildfire"), including a rapidly-spreading >2,900 acre [wildfire](/wiki/2025_Palisades_wildfire "2025 Palisades wildfire") in [Los Angeles County](/wiki/Los_Angeles_County%2C_California "Los Angeles County, California") which causes several [burn injuries](/wiki/Burn "Burn") and forces 30,000 people to evacuate. [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/01/07/weather/california-windstorm-fire-los-angeles-climate/index.html) [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/weather/wildfires/live-blog/live-updates-pacific-palisades-wildfire-rapidly-grows-california-rcna186685)
* [2025 Tibet earthquake](/wiki/2025_Tibet_earthquake "2025 Tibet earthquake")
  + At least 126 people are killed and dozens of others are injured when a magnitude Mw 7.1 (Ms 6.8) earthquake strikes [Tingri County](/wiki/Tingri_County "Tingri County"), [Shigatse](/wiki/Shigatse "Shigatse"), [Tibet Autonomous Region](/wiki/Tibet_Autonomous_Region "Tibet Autonomous Region"), [China](/wiki/China "China"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/7/earthquake-hits-tibets-shigatse-city-tremors-felt-in-nepals-kathmandu) [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/china-nepal-tibet-earthquake-himalayas-ca21bd4848209370b9eebcaf107208df)
* A [light aircraft](/wiki/Light_aircraft "Light aircraft") crashes near [Rottnest Island](/wiki/Rottnest_Island "Rottnest Island"), [Western Australia](/wiki/Western_Australia "Western Australia"), killing the pilot and two [tourists](/wiki/Tourism_in_Australia "Tourism in Australia") from [Denmark](/wiki/Danes "Danes") and [Switzerland](/wiki/Swiss_people "Swiss people") while injuring three other passengers. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/swiss-danish-tourists-among-three-dead-australian-plane-crash-2025-01-08/)
* Thirteen [Cuban soldiers](/wiki/Cuban_Revolutionary_Armed_Forces "Cuban Revolutionary Armed Forces") go missing after explosions at an arms and ammunition depot in [Holguín Province](/wiki/Holgu%C3%ADn_Province "Holguín Province"). [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/08/americas/cuban-soldiers-missing-explosion-ammo-depot-intl-hnk/index.html)

**Health and environment**

* [HMPV outbreak in East Asia](/wiki/HMPV_outbreak_in_East_Asia_%282024%E2%80%93present%29 "HMPV outbreak in East Asia (2024–present)")
  + [India](/wiki/India "India") confirms their first cases of the [human metapneumovirus](/wiki/Human_metapneumovirus "Human metapneumovirus") disease. [(CBS News)](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/hmpv-human-metapneumovirus-india-cases-confirmed-symptoms/)

**International relations**

* [Denmark–United States relations](/wiki/Denmark%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Denmark–United States relations"), [Proposals for the United States to purchase Greenland](/wiki/Proposals_for_the_United_States_to_purchase_Greenland "Proposals for the United States to purchase Greenland"), [Panama–United States relations](/wiki/Panama%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Panama–United States relations")
  + [U.S. president-elect](/wiki/President-elect_of_the_United_States "President-elect of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") refuses to rule out using [military](/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces "United States Armed Forces") force to take control of [Greenland](/wiki/Greenland "Greenland") and the [Panama Canal](/wiki/Panama_Canal "Panama Canal"), declaring U.S. control of both to be "vital to American [national security](/wiki/National_security "National security")". [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/trump-biden-offshore-drilling-gulf-of-america-fa66f8d072eb39c00a8128a8941ede75)
  + Trump's son [Donald Trump Jr.](/wiki/Donald_Trump_Jr. "Donald Trump Jr.") makes a personal visit to Greenland weeks after Trump announced that "ownership and control of Greenland is an absolute necessity". In response to the visit, [Danish prime minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Denmark "Prime Minister of Denmark") [Mette Frederiksen](/wiki/Mette_Frederiksen "Mette Frederiksen") states that "Greenland belongs to the [Greenlanders](/wiki/Greenlanders "Greenlanders")". [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c5yv10knyd9o)
  + [Panamanian foreign minister](/wiki/Minister_of_Foreign_Affairs_%28Panama%29 "Minister of Foreign Affairs (Panama)") Javier Martínez-Acha asserts that only [Panamanians](/wiki/Panamanians "Panamanians") operate the Panama Canal and that its sovereignty is non-negotiable, dismissing Trump's claims that [China](/wiki/China "China") operates the canal and his suggestion of potential [U.S. military](/wiki/U.S._military "U.S. military") action to [regain control](/wiki/United_States_invasion_of_Panama "United States invasion of Panama"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/panama-tells-trump-canal-sovereignty-is-non-negotiable/a-71243119)
* [Hungary–United States relations](/wiki/Hungary%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Hungary–United States relations")
  + The [U.S. Treasury](/wiki/U.S._Treasury "U.S. Treasury") imposes [sanctions](/wiki/United_States_sanctions "United States sanctions") on [Hungarian cabinet](/wiki/Cabinet_of_Hungary "Cabinet of Hungary") minister [Antal Rogán](/wiki/Antal_Rog%C3%A1n "Antal Rogán") for alleged [corruption](/wiki/Corruption_in_Hungary "Corruption in Hungary"), accusing him of using his position to secure financial benefits for himself and [political](/wiki/Politics_of_Hungary "Politics of Hungary") allies. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us-imposes-sanctions-senior-hungarian-official-suspected-corruption-2025-01-07/)
* [Sudan–United States relations](/wiki/Sudan%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Sudan–United States relations")
  + The [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") accuses the [Rapid Support Forces](/wiki/Rapid_Support_Forces "Rapid Support Forces") of committing [genocide](/wiki/Genocide "Genocide") in [Sudan](/wiki/Sudan "Sudan") during the [ongoing civil war](/wiki/Sudanese_civil_war_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Sudanese civil war (2023–present)") and imposes sanctions on the group's leader [Hemedti](/wiki/Hemedti "Hemedti"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/biden-sudan-genocide-7a0d20f857af3fd428750cf2dfd231ae)

**Law and crime**

* [2024 Venezuelan political crisis](/wiki/2024_Venezuelan_political_crisis "2024 Venezuelan political crisis")
  + [Venezuelan opposition](/wiki/Venezuelan_opposition "Venezuelan opposition") leader [Edmundo González](/wiki/Edmundo_Gonz%C3%A1lez "Edmundo González") reports the kidnapping of his son-in-law Rafael Tudares by masked men in [Caracas](/wiki/Caracas "Caracas"), as political tensions persist following González's contested claim of victory in [the country's July presidential election](/wiki/2024_Venezuelan_presidential_election "2024 Venezuelan presidential election"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/7/venezuelan-opposition-candidate-claims-son-in-law-has-been-kidnapped)
* Former [Cambodian](/wiki/Cambodia "Cambodia") [opposition](/wiki/Opposition_%28politics%29 "Opposition (politics)") [lawmaker](/wiki/Parliament_of_Cambodia "Parliament of Cambodia") [Lim Kimya](/wiki/Lim_Kimya "Lim Kimya") is shot dead by a [gunman on a motorcycle](/wiki/Drive-by_shooting "Drive-by shooting") in [Bangkok](/wiki/Bangkok "Bangkok"), [Thailand](/wiki/Thailand "Thailand"). [Cambodian officials](/wiki/Politics_of_Cambodia "Politics of Cambodia") deny allegations of involvement in Lim's death. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/jan/08/former-cambodian-opposition-politician-shot-dead-in-bangkok-reports)
* [Lebanon](/wiki/Lebanon "Lebanon") approves the [extradition](/wiki/Extradition "Extradition") of [Abdul Rahman Yusuf](/wiki/Abdul_Rahman_Yusuf "Abdul Rahman Yusuf"), the son of late [Egyptian](/wiki/Egyptians "Egyptians") *[ulama](/wiki/Ulama "Ulama")* [Yusuf al-Qaradawi](/wiki/Yusuf_al-Qaradawi "Yusuf al-Qaradawi"), to the [United Arab Emirates](/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates "United Arab Emirates") following his detention on December 28 after returning from Syria. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/lebanon-extradite-son-late-senior-muslim-cleric-al-qaradawi-uae-pms-office-says-2025-01-07/)
* [Mauritius](/wiki/Mauritius "Mauritius") issues an [arrest warrant](/wiki/Arrest_warrant "Arrest warrant") for former [finance minister](/wiki/Ministry_of_Finance_and_Economic_Development_%28Mauritius%29 "Ministry of Finance and Economic Development (Mauritius)") [Renganaden Padayachy](/wiki/Renganaden_Padayachy "Renganaden Padayachy") over alleged [embezzlement](/wiki/Embezzlement "Embezzlement") involving the disbursement of [Rs.](/wiki/Mauritian_rupee "Mauritian rupee") 45 million ([US$](/wiki/United_States_dollar "United States dollar")1 million) from the Mauritius Investment Corporation. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/mauritius-issues-arrest-order-against-former-finance-minister-local-newspaper-2025-01-07/)
* Two people are killed and one is injured in a [mass shooting](/wiki/Mass_shooting "Mass shooting") at Zahnradfabrik Hanel in [Bad Friedrichshall](/wiki/Bad_Friedrichshall "Bad Friedrichshall"), [Baden-Württemberg](/wiki/Baden-W%C3%BCrttemberg "Baden-Württemberg"), [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany"). The perpetrator is arrested. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/germany-two-dead-after-shooting-in-baden-w%C3%BCrttemberg/a-71242451)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024 Venezuelan political crisis](/wiki/2024_Venezuelan_political_crisis "2024 Venezuelan political crisis")
  + [Venezuelan president](/wiki/President_of_Venezuela "President of Venezuela") [Nicolás Maduro](/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro "Nicolás Maduro") announces [the arrest](/wiki/Political_prisoners_in_Venezuela "Political prisoners in Venezuela") of seven [foreign individuals](/wiki/International_reactions_to_the_2024_Venezuelan_presidential_election "International reactions to the 2024 Venezuelan presidential election"), whom he accuses of planning terrorist acts to disrupt his upcoming inauguration, with [security forces](/wiki/National_Bolivarian_Armed_Forces_of_Venezuela "National Bolivarian Armed Forces of Venezuela") conducting a [nationwide](/wiki/Venezuela "Venezuela") deployment. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/8/venezuelas-maduro-says-us-nationals-among-group-of-mercenaries-detained)
* [Death and state funeral of Jimmy Carter](/wiki/Death_and_state_funeral_of_Jimmy_Carter "Death and state funeral of Jimmy Carter")
  + The body of former [U.S. president](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Jimmy Carter](/wiki/Jimmy_Carter "Jimmy Carter") arrives in [Washington, D.C.](/wiki/Washington%2C_D.C. "Washington, D.C.") for a three-day mourning period, including a [lying in state](/wiki/Lying_in_state "Lying in state") at the [Capitol](/wiki/United_States_Capitol "United States Capitol"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/jimmy-carter-lie-state-us-capitol-before-funeral-2025-01-07/)
* [Libyan crisis](/wiki/Libyan_crisis_%282011%E2%80%93present%29 "Libyan crisis (2011–present)")
  + The [House of Representatives](/wiki/House_of_Representatives_%28Libya%29 "House of Representatives (Libya)") of [Libya](/wiki/Libya "Libya") approves a national reconciliation and [transitional justice](/wiki/Transitional_justice "Transitional justice") law aimed at unifying the country after over a decade of conflict. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/libyas-eastern-parliament-approves-transitional-justice-law-unity-move-mps-say-2025-01-08/)
* [John Mahama](/wiki/John_Mahama "John Mahama") is sworn in for a second term as [President of Ghana](/wiki/President_of_Ghana "President of Ghana"), having previously served as president from 2012 to 2017. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/ghanas-mahama-returns-president-facing-old-problems-2025-01-07/)

**Science and technology**

* [Meta Platforms](/wiki/Meta_Platforms "Meta Platforms") announces an end to its third-party fact-checking program and a transition to a crowd-sourced model similar to [X](/wiki/Twitter "Twitter")'s [Community Notes](/wiki/Community_Notes "Community Notes"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/meta-facts-trump-musk-community-notes-413b8495939a058ff2d25fd23f2e0f43)

January 8, 2025 (2025-01-08) (Wednesday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_8&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Boko Haram insurgency](/wiki/Boko_Haram_insurgency "Boko Haram insurgency")
  + [2025 N'Djamena attack](/wiki/2025_N%27Djamena_attack "2025 N'Djamena attack")
    - Gunfire and military vehicles are reported near the [Presidential Palace](/wiki/Official_residence#Chad "Official residence") in [N'Djamena](/wiki/N%27Djamena "N'Djamena"), [Chad](/wiki/Chad "Chad"), with the [Chadian government](/wiki/Government_of_Chad "Government of Chad") accusing [Boko Haram](/wiki/Boko_Haram "Boko Haram") of being behind the attack. The [Chad National Army](/wiki/Chad_National_Army "Chad National Army") has reportedly regained stable control of the capital, with 18 insurgents and one security force member being killed in the attack. [(Devdiscourse)](https://www.devdiscourse.com/article/law-order/3219554-tense-moments-in-ndjamena-gunfire-near-presidential-palace) [(Deutsche Welle)](https://www.dw.com/en/chad-gunfire-heard-near-presidency-in-ndjamena/a-71251244)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip](/wiki/Israeli_bombing_of_the_Gaza_Strip "Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip")
    - [Israeli airstrikes](/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force "Israeli Air Force") across the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip") kill at least 27 people. [(Arab News)](https://www.arabnews.com/node/2585653/middle-east)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Zaporizhzhia strikes](/wiki/Zaporizhzhia_strikes_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "Zaporizhzhia strikes (2022–present)"), [Attacks on civilians in the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Attacks_on_civilians_in_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Attacks on civilians in the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
    - [Russian forces](/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces "Russian Armed Forces") attack an industrial facility in [Zaporizhzhia](/wiki/Zaporizhzhia "Zaporizhzhia"), [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"), killing 13 people and injuring 18 others. Further strikes on Zaporizhzhia with [guided aerial bombs](/wiki/Aerial_bomb "Aerial bomb") kill 13 more people and injure 32 others. [(*Ukrainska Pravda*)](https://www.pravda.com.ua/eng/news/2025/01/8/7492571/) [(*Ukrainska Pravda* 2)](https://www.pravda.com.ua/eng/news/2025/01/8/7492614/)
* [Insurgency in the Maghreb](/wiki/Insurgency_in_the_Maghreb_%282002%E2%80%93present%29 "Insurgency in the Maghreb (2002–present)")
  + [2025 Point Triple attack](/wiki/2025_Point_Triple_attack "2025 Point Triple attack")
    - Twenty-eight [soldiers](/wiki/Benin_Armed_Forces "Benin Armed Forces") are killed during a [mass shooting](/wiki/Mass_shooting "Mass shooting") in northern [Benin](/wiki/Benin "Benin") near the border with [Burkina Faso](/wiki/Burkina_Faso "Burkina Faso"). [(Punch)](https://punchng.com/28-beninese-soldiers-killed-in-attack-near-burkina-faso-border/)
* [Myanmar civil war](/wiki/Myanmar_civil_war_%282021%E2%80%93present%29 "Myanmar civil war (2021–present)")
  + At least 40 people are killed and 12 others are injured in [Tatmadaw](/wiki/Tatmadaw "Tatmadaw") airstrikes on [Ramree](/wiki/Ramree "Ramree"), [Rakhine State](/wiki/Rakhine_State "Rakhine State"), [Myanmar](/wiki/Myanmar "Myanmar"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/11/dozens-killed-in-myanmar-military-air-attack-in-rakhine-state-un) [(*India Today*)](https://www.indiatoday.in/world/story/myanmar-army-airstike-12-killed-500-house-destroyed-rakhine-state-2663336-2025-01-11)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - [Palisades Fire](/wiki/Palisades_Fire "Palisades Fire"), [Eaton Fire](/wiki/Eaton_Fire "Eaton Fire"), [Hurst Fire](/wiki/Hurst_Fire "Hurst Fire")
      * More than 100,000 people are evacuated from approaching [wildfires](/wiki/Wildfires "Wildfires") in the [Pacific Palisades](/wiki/Pacific_Palisades%2C_Los_Angeles "Pacific Palisades, Los Angeles") and [Hollywood](/wiki/Hollywood%2C_Los_Angeles "Hollywood, Los Angeles") neighborhoods of [Los Angeles](/wiki/Los_Angeles "Los Angeles") and [Altadena](/wiki/Altadena%2C_California "Altadena, California"), [California](/wiki/California "California"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), that have burnt more than 3,000 acres, aggravated by an ongoing extreme [windstorm](/wiki/Windstorm "Windstorm") and [drought conditions](/wiki/Drought "Drought"). Five people are killed, dozens of others are injured, and around 1,000 structures are destroyed. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/live/live-updates-wildfire-los-angeles-palisades) [(*The Independent*)](https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/americas/pacific-palisades-fire-la-california-map-latest-b2675408.html) [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/weather/wildfires/live-blog/live-updates-pacific-palisades-wildfire-rapidly-grows-california-rcna186685) [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/palisades-fire-live-tens-thousands-flee-wildfires-rage-los-angeles-2025-01-08/)
    - The [CALNEV Pipeline](/wiki/Calnev_Pipeline "Calnev Pipeline") connecting [oil refineries](/wiki/Oil_refinery "Oil refinery") in [southern California](/wiki/Southern_California "Southern California") to [Clark County, Nevada](/wiki/Clark_County%2C_Nevada "Clark County, Nevada"), shuts down due to [power outages](/wiki/Power_outage "Power outage"), temporarily cutting off the [gasoline](/wiki/Gasoline "Gasoline") supply to [Las Vegas](/wiki/Las_Vegas "Las Vegas") and [Nellis Air Force Base](/wiki/Nellis_Air_Force_Base "Nellis Air Force Base"). The [Kinder Morgan](/wiki/Kinder_Morgan "Kinder Morgan") SFPP Pipeline connecting southern California to [Phoenix, Arizona](/wiki/Phoenix%2C_Arizona "Phoenix, Arizona"), also shuts down. [(KTNV)](https://www.ktnv.com/news/good-morning-las-vegas/good-morning-las-vegas-fuel-supply-concerns-swirling-as-wildfires-disrupt-california-pipelines) [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/business/energy/kinder-morgan-fuel-pipelines-shut-due-power-outages-southern-california-2025-01-10/)
* [Deadly human stampedes in Hindu temples](/wiki/List_of_deadly_human_stampedes_in_Hindu_temples "List of deadly human stampedes in Hindu temples")
  + Six people are killed and over forty others are injured in a [stampede](/wiki/Stampede "Stampede") at the [Hindu](/wiki/Hinduism "Hinduism") [Venkateswara Temple](/wiki/Venkateswara_Temple%2C_Tirumala "Venkateswara Temple, Tirumala") in [Tirupati](/wiki/Tirupati "Tirupati"), [Andhra Pradesh](/wiki/Andhra_Pradesh "Andhra Pradesh"), [India](/wiki/India "India"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/india-stampede-andhra-pradesh-temple-7855dcf993849b31f78de56f988058e8) [(Business Today)](https://www.businesstoday.in/india/story/tirupati-stampede-6-dead-40-injured-as-devotees-rush-to-get-tickets-for-vaikunta-dwara-darshanam-460093-2025-01-09)

**International relations**

* [Iran–Italy relations](/wiki/Iran%E2%80%93Italy_relations "Iran–Italy relations")
  + The [Iranian government](/wiki/Government_of_Iran "Government of Iran") releases [Italian](/wiki/Italy "Italy") journalist [Cecilia Sala](/wiki/Cecilia_Sala "Cecilia Sala") from prison, with Sala arriving back in [Rome](/wiki/Rome "Rome") later that day. [(Euronews)](https://www.euronews.com/2025/01/08/tehran-releases-italian-journalist-cecilia-sala-from-prison) [(Yahoo! News)](https://uk.news.yahoo.com/italian-journalist-cecilia-sala-arrives-040525478.html?guccounter=1)
* [Lithuania–Russia relations](/wiki/Lithuania%E2%80%93Russia_relations "Lithuania–Russia relations")
  + [Lithuanian prime minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Lithuania "Prime Minister of Lithuania") [Gintautas Paluckas](/wiki/Gintautas_Paluckas "Gintautas Paluckas") deploys [the police](/wiki/Lithuanian_Police_Force "Lithuanian Police Force") to secure [the country](/wiki/Lithuania "Lithuania")'s [electricity link](/wiki/LitPol_Link "LitPol Link") with [Poland](/wiki/Poland "Poland") in response to reported attempts to disrupt the planned decoupling of the [Baltic states](/wiki/Baltic_states "Baltic states")' power systems from [the grid shared](/wiki/IPS/UPS "IPS/UPS") with [Belarus](/wiki/Belarus "Belarus") and Russia. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/lithuania-boosts-power-grid-security-ahead-russia-decoupling-2025-01-08/)
* [Azerbaijan](/wiki/Azerbaijan "Azerbaijan") [protests](/wiki/Diplomatic_correspondence "Diplomatic correspondence") [Eritrea](/wiki/Eritrea "Eritrea")'s detention of three Azerbaijani-flagged vessels and 18 crew members since November 2024, stating the ships entered Eritrean waters due to adverse weather en route to [Abu Dhabi](/wiki/Abu_Dhabi "Abu Dhabi"), [United Arab Emirates](/wiki/United_Arab_Emirates "United Arab Emirates"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/azerbaijan-protests-eritrea-over-detention-three-vessels-crews-2025-01-08/)

**Law and crime**

* The [British government](/wiki/Government_of_the_United_Kingdom "Government of the United Kingdom") freezes the assets of [neo-Nazi](/wiki/Neo-Nazism "Neo-Nazism") music network [Blood & Honour](/wiki/Blood_%26_Honour "Blood & Honour"), becoming the first [far-right group in the UK](/wiki/Far-right_politics_in_the_United_Kingdom "Far-right politics in the United Kingdom") to be sanctioned by the government. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/cqjzj4zrppko)

**Politics and elections**

* [Politics of New Caledonia](/wiki/Politics_of_New_Caledonia "Politics of New Caledonia")
  + [Alcide Ponga](/wiki/Alcide_Ponga "Alcide Ponga") of the pro-France [The Rally](/wiki/The_Rally_%28New_Caledonia%29 "The Rally (New Caledonia)") party is elected [President of New Caledonia](/wiki/President_of_New_Caledonia "President of New Caledonia") by six of the eleven government ministers. [(Radio New Zealand)](https://www.rnz.co.nz/international/pacific-news/538534/alcide-ponga-is-new-caledonia-s-new-president)
* The ruling party in [São Tomé and Príncipe](/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "São Tomé and Príncipe"), [Independent Democratic Action](/wiki/Independent_Democratic_Action "Independent Democratic Action"), proposes [Hélio Vaz de Almeida](/w/index.php?title=H%C3%A9lio_Vaz_de_Almeida&action=edit&redlink=1 "Hélio Vaz de Almeida (page does not exist)") as [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "Prime Minister of São Tomé and Príncipe") to replace [Patrice Trovoada](/wiki/Patrice_Trovoada "Patrice Trovoada"), who was fired by [President](/wiki/President_of_S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "President of São Tomé and Príncipe") [Carlos Vila Nova](/wiki/Carlos_Vila_Nova "Carlos Vila Nova") two days ago. [(RFI)](https://www.rfi.fr/pt/%C3%A1frica-lus%C3%B3fona/20250108-s%C3%A3o-tom%C3%A9-e-pr%C3%ADncipe-adi-prop%C3%B5e-h%C3%A9lio-almeida-para-novo-primeiro-ministro)

January 9, 2025 (2025-01-09) (Thursday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_9&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
