**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)"), [War against the Islamic State](/wiki/War_against_the_Islamic_State "War against the Islamic State")
  + [Islamic State insurgency in Puntland](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland")
    - [Puntland forces](/wiki/Puntland_Security_Force "Puntland Security Force") carry out [drone strikes](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") on [Islamic State](/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_Somalia_Province "Islamic State – Somalia Province") targets in the [Cal Miskaad](/wiki/Cal_Miskaad "Cal Miskaad") mountains near [Balidhidhin District](/wiki/Balidhidhin_District "Balidhidhin District"), [Bari](/wiki/Bari%2C_Somalia "Bari, Somalia"), [Puntland](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland"), [Somalia](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia"), killing several militants. [(Idil News)](https://www.idilnews.com/puntland-forces-conduct-airstrikes-on-isis-positions-around-balodhidin-of-bari-region/) [(VOA)](https://www.voasomali.com/a/duqeymo-ka-dhacay-degaano-ka-mid-ah-gobolka-bari/7931018.html)
    - Puntland [counterterrorism](/wiki/Counterterrorism "Counterterrorism") forces capture four foreign Islamic State fighters from [Ethiopia](/wiki/Ethiopia "Ethiopia"), [Yemen](/wiki/Yemen "Yemen"), and [Tanzania](/wiki/Tanzania "Tanzania"), while intercepting and destroying multiple explosive-carrying drones in Bari, Puntland. [(Idil News)](https://www.idilnews.com/puntland-forces-conduct-airstrikes-on-isis-positions-around-balodhidin-of-bari-region/) [(VOA)](https://www.voasomali.com/a/duqeymo-ka-dhacay-degaano-ka-mid-ah-gobolka-bari/7931018.html) [(Garowe Online)](https://www.garoweonline.com/en/news/puntland/islamic-state-foreign-fighters-surrender-in-somalia-s-puntland-amid-offensive)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip](/wiki/Israeli_bombing_of_the_Gaza_Strip "Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip")
    - [Israeli airstrikes](/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force "Israeli Air Force") across the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip") kill at least 22 people. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2025/1/9/live-israel-kills-50-people-in-gaza-recovers-body-of-captive-from-rafah)
  + A study published in *[The Lancet](/wiki/The_Lancet "The Lancet")* claims that around 3% of the Gaza Strip population has died from traumatic injury due to the conflict with Israel, with the death toll from other causes due to the military campaign likely higher. [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/09/middleeast/gaza-death-toll-underreported-study-intl/index.html)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Attacks on civilians in the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Attacks_on_civilians_in_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Attacks on civilians in the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
    - [Russian](/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces "Russian Armed Forces") [artillery](/wiki/Artillery "Artillery") strikes kill two people in [Siversk](/wiki/Siversk "Siversk"), [Donetsk Oblast](/wiki/Donetsk_Oblast "Donetsk Oblast"), [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"), according to the region's governor. In the Russian-controlled area of [Kamianka-Dniprovska](/wiki/Kamianka-Dniprovska "Kamianka-Dniprovska"), [Zaporizhzhia Oblast](/wiki/Zaporizhzhia_Oblast "Zaporizhzhia Oblast"), Ukraine, the region's Russia-appointed governor says that two people were killed by Ukrainian artillery strikes. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/four-dead-shelling-incidents-ukraine-officials-say-2025-01-09/)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - At least six people are killed due to spreading [wildfires](/wiki/Wildfire "Wildfire") in [Los Angeles County](/wiki/Los_Angeles_County%2C_California "Los Angeles County, California"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States").
    - The Kenneth Fire ignites in [Woodland Hills](/wiki/Woodland_Hills%2C_Los_Angeles "Woodland Hills, Los Angeles"), adding to the 179,000 people placed under evacuation orders. [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/weather/wildfires/live-blog/california-wildfires-live-updates-deadly-blazes-spread-hollywood-hills-rcna186927)
* [2024–25 European winter](/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_European_winter "2024–25 European winter")
  + Two people are killed and 20 others are injured in a [snowstorm](/wiki/Winter_storm "Winter storm") in northern [France](/wiki/France "France"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/france-europe-cold-snap-snow-weather-deaths-eb1cd5d181c6ce4b8ca32b5e8e29b727)
* Twelve [miners](/wiki/Miner "Miner") are trapped in a collapsed [coal mine](/wiki/Coal_mine "Coal mine") in [Balochistan](/wiki/Balochistan%2C_Pakistan "Balochistan, Pakistan"), [Pakistan](/wiki/Pakistan "Pakistan"), following a [methane](/wiki/Methane "Methane") [gas explosion](/wiki/Gas_explosion "Gas explosion"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/pakistan-coal-miners-trapped-southwest-5befdfc30cdda20919a3ad74acd2c6dd)

**International relations**

* [Armenia–European Union relations](/wiki/Armenia%E2%80%93European_Union_relations "Armenia–European Union relations")
  + The [Armenian government](/wiki/Government_of_Armenia "Government of Armenia") approves a bill to launch a bid for [the country](/wiki/Armenia "Armenia") to join the [European Union](/wiki/European_Union "European Union"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/armenian-government-approves-bill-launch-eu-accession-bid-2025-01-09/)
* [Azerbaijan–Russia relations](/wiki/Azerbaijan%E2%80%93Russia_relations "Azerbaijan–Russia relations")
  + [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia") declines to confirm whether [Russian forces](/wiki/Air_and_Missile_Defense_Forces "Air and Missile Defense Forces") accidentally shot down [Azerbaijan Airlines Flight 8243](/wiki/Azerbaijan_Airlines_Flight_8243 "Azerbaijan Airlines Flight 8243"), despite calls by [Azerbaijan](/wiki/Azerbaijan "Azerbaijan") to do so. [(*The Straits Times*)](https://www.straitstimes.com/world/europe/kremlin-declines-to-accept-responsibility-for-plane-crash)
* [Guyana–Venezuela territorial dispute](/wiki/Guyana%E2%80%93Venezuela_territorial_dispute "Guyana–Venezuela territorial dispute")
  + [Guyana](/wiki/Guyana "Guyana") says that it will resort to the [United Nations](/wiki/United_Nations "United Nations") to deter [Venezuela](/wiki/Venezuela "Venezuela") from unilaterally appointing a governor for the [Essequibo](/wiki/Regions_of_Guyana "Regions of Guyana"), a region under Guyanese control but claimed by Venezuela. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/guyana-venezuela-un-top-court-essequibo-ae871c1b8514d555aed9f6182207466f)

**Law and crime**

* [International Criminal Court arrest warrants for Israeli leaders](/wiki/International_Criminal_Court_arrest_warrants_for_Israeli_leaders "International Criminal Court arrest warrants for Israeli leaders")
  + [Poland](/wiki/Poland "Poland")'s government confirms that it will not comply with an [International Criminal Court](/wiki/International_Criminal_Court "International Criminal Court") (ICC) warrant to arrest [Israeli Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel "Prime Minister of Israel") [Benjamin Netanyahu](/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu "Benjamin Netanyahu") for [war crimes](/wiki/War_crime "War crime") if he chooses to attend a ceremony at [Auschwitz concentration camp](/wiki/Auschwitz_concentration_camp "Auschwitz concentration camp") later this month. [(*Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/polish-president-seeks-to-shield-netanyahu-as-warrant-scuppers-auschwitz-memorial-visit/) [(Notes from Poland)](https://notesfrompoland.com/2025/01/09/poland-confirms-it-will-not-arrest-netanyahu-on-icc-warrant-if-he-attends-auschwitz-anniversary/)
  + The [U.S. House of Representatives](/wiki/U.S._House_of_Representatives "U.S. House of Representatives") votes 243 to 140 to sanction the ICC for issuing arrest warrants for Benjamin Netanyahu and former [Israeli Defense Minister](/wiki/Ministry_of_Defense_%28Israel%29 "Ministry of Defense (Israel)") [Yoav Gallant](/wiki/Yoav_Gallant "Yoav Gallant"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us-house-votes-sanction-international-criminal-court-over-israel-2025-01-09/) [(Middle East Eye)](https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/us-lawmakers-vote-sanction-icc-officials-issuing-netanyahu-warrant) [(*Haaretz*)](https://www.haaretz.com/us-news/2025-01-09/ty-article/.premium/u-s-house-votes-to-sanction-icc-over-alleged-targeting-of-senior-israeli-officials/00000194-4c7e-d6f4-a9b5-5cfe67660000)
  + [U.S. Senate](/wiki/United_States_Senate "United States Senate") [majority leader](/wiki/Party_leaders_of_the_United_States_Senate "Party leaders of the United States Senate") [John Thune](/wiki/John_Thune "John Thune") promises swift consideration of the Illegitimate Court Counteraction Act so [President-elect](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") can sign it into law shortly after [taking office](/wiki/Second_inauguration_of_Donald_Trump "Second inauguration of Donald Trump"). Under the act, any foreigner who investigates, arrests, detains or prosecutes [U.S. citizens](/wiki/U.S._citizens "U.S. citizens") or those of an allied country, including Israel, not under ICC jurisdiction would be sanctioned along with their family members. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us-house-votes-sanction-international-criminal-court-over-israel-2025-01-09/) [(*The New York Times*)](https://www.nytimes.com/2025/01/09/us/politics/icc-sanctions-house-israel.html)
* [2024 Venezuelan political crisis](/wiki/2024_Venezuelan_political_crisis "2024 Venezuelan political crisis")
  + [Venezuelan](/wiki/Venezuela "Venezuela") [opposition](/wiki/Venezuelan_opposition "Venezuelan opposition") leader [María Corina Machado](/wiki/Mar%C3%ADa_Corina_Machado "María Corina Machado") makes her first public appearance in 133 days and is briefly arrested when her convoy is intercepted by [security forces](/wiki/National_Bolivarian_Armed_Forces_of_Venezuela "National Bolivarian Armed Forces of Venezuela") as it departs an anti-government protest in [Caracas](/wiki/Caracas "Caracas"). The incident occurs the day before the ruling party-controlled [National Assembly](/wiki/National_Assembly_of_Venezuela "National Assembly of Venezuela") is scheduled to swear in [Nicolás Maduro](/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro "Nicolás Maduro") for a third term as [president](/wiki/President_of_Venezuela "President of Venezuela"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/venezuela-election-inauguration-maduro-protests-edmundo-machado-db8a045f2614cb71022674dc6b73bd88) [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/jan/09/venezuela-maria-corina-machado-kidnapped)
* The [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo") bans [Al Jazeera](/wiki/Al_Jazeera_Media_Network "Al Jazeera Media Network") from operating in the country and revokes its [press credentials](/wiki/Press_credentials "Press credentials"), citing the network's interview with [M23 rebel](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") leader [Bertrand Bisimwa](/wiki/Bertrand_Bisimwa "Bertrand Bisimwa") as an [endorsement of terrorism](/wiki/Al_Jazeera_controversies_and_criticism "Al Jazeera controversies and criticism"). Authorities warn against reporting on the group, with the [justice minister](/wiki/Ministry_of_Justice_%28Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo%29 "Ministry of Justice (Democratic Republic of the Congo)") threatening to invoke the [death penalty](/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Capital punishment in the Democratic Republic of the Congo"), although no [formal law](/wiki/Constitution_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Constitution of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") bans such [coverage](/wiki/Mass_media_in_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Mass media in the Democratic Republic of the Congo"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/congo-al-jazeera-ban-92871abe63d84f798ecf6d229e6f74de)
* The [Kuwaiti](/wiki/Kuwait "Kuwait") public prosecution detains media personality [Fajer Al-Saeed](/wiki/Fajer_Al-Saeed "Fajer Al-Saeed") for 21 days and after investigating charges related to "calling for normalization with the [Israeli](/wiki/Israel "Israel") occupation and harming the state's interests". [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.net/misc/2025/1/9/%D8%A8%D8%AA%D9%87%D9%85%D8%A9-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%AA%D8%B7%D8%A8%D9%8A%D8%B9-%D8%B3%D8%AC%D9%86-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%A5%D8%B9%D9%84%D8%A7%D9%85%D9%8A%D8%A9-%D8%A7%D9%84%D9%83%D9%88%D9%8A%D8%AA%D9%8A%D8%A9)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024 Mozambican general election](/wiki/2024_Mozambican_general_election "2024 Mozambican general election")
  + [2024 Mozambican protests](/wiki/2024_Mozambican_protests "2024 Mozambican protests")
    - [PODEMOS](/wiki/Optimist_Party_for_the_Development_of_Mozambique "Optimist Party for the Development of Mozambique") [presidential](/wiki/President_of_Mozambique "President of Mozambique") candidate [Venâncio Mondlane](/wiki/Ven%C3%A2ncio_Mondlane "Venâncio Mondlane"), who alleges that the October election was [rigged](/wiki/Electoral_fraud "Electoral fraud"), returns to [Mozambique](/wiki/Mozambique "Mozambique") from exile in [South Africa](/wiki/South_Africa "South Africa") amid protests. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/mozambique-opposition-leader-returns-after-fleeing-post-election-safety-fears-2025-01-09/)
* [2022–2025 Lebanese presidential election](/wiki/2022%E2%80%932025_Lebanese_presidential_election "2022–2025 Lebanese presidential election")
  + [Military](/wiki/Lebanese_Armed_Forces "Lebanese Armed Forces") [commander](/wiki/Commander_of_the_Lebanese_Armed_Forces "Commander of the Lebanese Armed Forces") [Joseph Aoun](/wiki/Joseph_Aoun "Joseph Aoun") is elected as [President of Lebanon](/wiki/President_of_Lebanon "President of Lebanon"), ending the [power vacuum](/wiki/Power_vacuum "Power vacuum") that began in October 2022. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/lebanon-parliament-president-joseph-aoun-hezbollah-942ce2e5d5619f072c8b23850ebce7b5)
* [Death and state funeral of Jimmy Carter](/wiki/Death_and_state_funeral_of_Jimmy_Carter "Death and state funeral of Jimmy Carter")
  + The [state funeral](/wiki/State_funeral "State funeral") for former [U.S. president](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Jimmy Carter](/wiki/Jimmy_Carter "Jimmy Carter") is held at the [National Cathedral](/wiki/Washington_National_Cathedral "Washington National Cathedral") in [Washington, D.C.](/wiki/Washington%2C_D.C. "Washington, D.C.") All five living presidents, including incumbent president [Joe Biden](/wiki/Joe_Biden "Joe Biden") and [president-elect](/wiki/President-elect_of_the_United_States "President-elect of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump"), attend the funeral. [(CBS News)](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/jimmy-carters-funeral-living-presidents-together-national-cathedral/)
* [President](/wiki/President_of_S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "President of São Tomé and Príncipe") of [São Tomé and Príncipe](/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "São Tomé and Príncipe") [Carlos Vila Nova](/wiki/Carlos_Vila_Nova "Carlos Vila Nova") rejects a proposal by his [Independent Democratic Action](/wiki/Independent_Democratic_Action "Independent Democratic Action") party to elect Hélio Vaz de Almeida as [prime minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "Prime Minister of São Tomé and Príncipe"). Vila Nova instead appoints [Ilza Amado Vaz](/wiki/Ilza_Amado_Vaz "Ilza Amado Vaz"). [(RFI)](https://www.rfi.fr/pt/%C3%A1frica-lus%C3%B3fona/20250109-presidente-rejeita-nome-de-h%C3%A9lio-vaz-de-almeida-para-primeiro-ministro), [(Xinhua)](https://english.news.cn/africa/20250110/8cb26230d24645d2ba4e9ff3d4ae696d/c.html)

January 10, 2025 (2025-01-10) (Friday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_10&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)"), [War against the Islamic State](/wiki/War_against_the_Islamic_State "War against the Islamic State")
  + [Islamic State insurgency in Puntland](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland")
    - [Puntland forces](/wiki/Puntland_Security_Force "Puntland Security Force") fight against [ISIS](/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_Somalia_Province "Islamic State – Somalia Province") in the IL-Ameira mountains, stopping seven [drones loaded with bombs](/wiki/Loitering_munition "Loitering munition") and removing ten [landmines](/wiki/Landmines "Landmines"). The forces also destroy five ISIS bases. They capture [military bases](/wiki/Military_bases "Military bases"), including a [water well](/wiki/Water_well "Water well") in Jeceel Valley near [Cal Miskaad](/wiki/Cal_Miskaad "Cal Miskaad") mountains of [Balidhidhin District](/wiki/Balidhidhin_District "Balidhidhin District"), [Bari](/wiki/Bari%2C_Somalia "Bari, Somalia"), [Puntland](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland"). [(Horseed Media)](https://horseedmedia.net/puntland-forces-gain-ground-in-offensive-against-isis-stronghold/398718/) [(Hiiraan Online)](https://www.hiiraan.com/news/2025/Jan/wararka_maanta10-188970.htm?utm_source=hiiraan&utm_medium=WararkaMaantaFront)
* [Red Sea crisis](/wiki/Red_Sea_crisis "Red Sea crisis")
  + The [Israeli Air Force](/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force "Israeli Air Force") launches airstrikes on a power station and two ports in [Houthi](/wiki/Houthi "Houthi")-controlled [Yemen](/wiki/Yemen "Yemen") in retaliation for Houthi drone and missile attacks on [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel"), with pro-Houthi media reporting that at least three people were injured. [(Al Arabiya)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/gulf/2025/01/10/security-firm-says-airstrikes-reported-in-houthi-controlled-yemen-including-oil-port)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - Amid ongoing wildfires, authorities in [Los Angeles County](/wiki/Los_Angeles_County "Los Angeles County"), [California](/wiki/California "California"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), impose a curfew and announce the deployment of the [California National Guard](/wiki/California_National_Guard "California National Guard") in order to protect homes in evacuated areas from [looting](/wiki/Looting "Looting"). [(KNBC-TV)](https://www.nbclosangeles.com/news/california-wildfires/curfew-la-county-wildfires/3600157/)
    - The [United States Department of Health and Human Services](/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Health_and_Human_Services "United States Department of Health and Human Services") issues a [public health emergency](/wiki/Public_health_emergency_%28United_States%29 "Public health emergency (United States)") for California in response to injuries and [mental health](/wiki/Mental_health "Mental health") impacts caused by the ongoing wildfires. [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/weather/live-news/los-angeles-wildfires-palisades-eaton-california-01-10-25-hnk/index.html)
* Three of the twelve miners that were reported missing yesterday in an explosion at a coal mine in Singidi, [Balochistan](/wiki/Balochistan%2C_Pakistan "Balochistan, Pakistan"), [Pakistan](/wiki/Pakistan "Pakistan"), are found dead by rescue workers. [(CTV News)](https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/bodies-found-after-gas-explosion-causes-coal-mine-to-collapse-in-southwest-pakistan-1.7171084)
* Three women are killed and five children are injured in a [stampede](/wiki/Crowd_collapses_and_crushes#crowd_"stampedes" "Crowd collapses and crushes") at the [Umayyad Mosque](/wiki/Umayyad_Mosque "Umayyad Mosque") in [Damascus](/wiki/Damascus "Damascus"), [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/stampede-kills-three-women-injures-five-children-umayyad-mosque-damascus-2025-01-10/)
* Three people on the ground are killed and three others are injured when a [Cessna 172](/wiki/Cessna_172 "Cessna 172") aircraft crashes into a road near [Malindi](/wiki/Malindi "Malindi"), [Kenya](/wiki/Kenya "Kenya"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/kenya-plane-crash-malindi-3c41baec5aa126b1d25d93313566f14d)

**Health and environment**

* [2024 in climate change](/wiki/2024_in_climate_change "2024 in climate change")
  + The [Copernicus Climate Change Service](/wiki/Copernicus_Climate_Change_Service "Copernicus Climate Change Service") confirms that 2024 was the warmest calendar year since records began in 1850, with the [average global temperature](/wiki/Global_surface_temperature "Global surface temperature") reaching 1.6 °C above [pre-industrial](/wiki/Pre-industrial_society "Pre-industrial society") levels, surpassing the 1.5 °C [warming](/wiki/Climate_change "Climate change") benchmark set in 2016 by the [Paris Agreement](/wiki/Paris_Agreement "Paris Agreement") for the first time. [(C3S)](https://climate.copernicus.eu/global-climate-highlights-2024) [(Politico)](https://www.politico.eu/article/world-edge-breaching-paris-agreement-scientists-say-planet-heating-hottest-year-climate-change/) [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cd7575x8yq5o)

**International relations**

* [2025 Moldovan energy crisis](/wiki/2025_Moldovan_energy_crisis "2025 Moldovan energy crisis")
  + [Moldova](/wiki/Moldova "Moldova")'s [unrecognized breakaway region](/wiki/List_of_states_with_limited_recognition "List of states with limited recognition") of [Transnistria](/wiki/Transnistria "Transnistria") extends its [state of emergency](/wiki/State_of_emergency "State of emergency") for another month due to an [energy crisis](/wiki/Energy_crisis "Energy crisis") following the suspension of [Russian gas supplies](/wiki/Russia_in_the_European_energy_sector "Russia in the European energy sector"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/moldovas-pro-russian-separatists-extend-state-emergency-amid-gas-cutoff-2025-01-10/)
* [Colombia–Venezuela relations](/wiki/Colombia%E2%80%93Venezuela_relations "Colombia–Venezuela relations")
  + The [government of Venezuela](/wiki/Government_of_Venezuela "Government of Venezuela") closes the [border](/wiki/Colombia%E2%80%93Venezuela_border "Colombia–Venezuela border") with [Colombia](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia") ahead of the swearing-in of [Nicolás Maduro](/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro "Nicolás Maduro") for a third term as [President of Venezuela](/wiki/President_of_Venezuela "President of Venezuela"). [(*Le Monde*)](https://www.lemonde.fr/en/international/article/2025/01/10/venezuela-closes-colombia-border-ahead-of-maduro-s-swearing-in_6736907_4.html)
* [Denmark–United States relations](/wiki/Denmark%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Denmark–United States relations"), [Proposals for the United States to purchase Greenland](/wiki/Proposals_for_the_United_States_to_purchase_Greenland "Proposals for the United States to purchase Greenland")
  + The [Prime Minister of Greenland](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Greenland "Prime Minister of Greenland"), [Mute Bourup Egede](/wiki/Mute_Bourup_Egede "Mute Bourup Egede"), says that his country "has a desire for independence" and he, in particular, is ready to speak with [US President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States")-elect [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump"). [(Bloomberg)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/10/americas/greenland-trump-denmark-press-conference-intl-latam/index.html)
* [International sanctions during the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/International_sanctions_during_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "International sanctions during the Russian invasion of Ukraine"), [Russia–United States relations](/wiki/Russia%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Russia–United States relations")
  + The [United States government](/wiki/United_States_government "United States government") imposes a new series of sanctions targeting [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia")'s [energy](/wiki/Energy_in_Russia "Energy in Russia") sector, including the [Gazprom Neft](/wiki/Gazprom_Neft "Gazprom Neft") and [Surgutneftegas](/wiki/Surgutneftegas "Surgutneftegas") oil companies. [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/10/politics/biden-admin-russia-energy-sanctions-ukraine/index.html)
* [Italy–Syria relations](/wiki/Italy%E2%80%93Syria_relations "Italy–Syria relations")
  + The [Italian Foreign Minister](/wiki/Foreign_Minister_of_Italy "Foreign Minister of Italy"), [Antonio Tajani](/wiki/Antonio_Tajani "Antonio Tajani"), meets in [Damascus](/wiki/Damascus "Damascus") with [Ahmed al-Sharaa](/wiki/Ahmed_al-Sharaa "Ahmed al-Sharaa"), de facto leader of [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria"). [(Euronews)](https://es.euronews.com/2025/01/10/tajani-se-reune-con-al-sharaa-en-damasco-italia-sera-el-puente-entre-la-nueva-siria-y-la-u)

**Law and crime**

* [Indictments against Donald Trump](/wiki/Indictments_against_Donald_Trump "Indictments against Donald Trump")
  + [Prosecution of Donald Trump in New York](/wiki/Prosecution_of_Donald_Trump_in_New_York "Prosecution of Donald Trump in New York")
    - [U.S. president-elect](/wiki/President-elect_of_the_United_States "President-elect of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") is sentenced for [falsifying business records](/wiki/Falsifying_business_records "Falsifying business records"), with judge [Juan Merchan](/wiki/Juan_Merchan "Juan Merchan") ordering an [unconditional discharge](/wiki/Unconditional_discharge "Unconditional discharge"), stating that imprisonment or fines could cause Trump to eventually have his convictions overturned. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/trump-hush-money-sentencing-stormy-daniels-33e070bd3c1acb609bba13f23d784a3a)
* [Death and funeral of Alexei Navalny](/wiki/Death_and_funeral_of_Alexei_Navalny "Death and funeral of Alexei Navalny")
  + [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia") financial watchdog [Rosfinmonitoring](/wiki/Rosfinmonitoring "Rosfinmonitoring") rejects requests to remove former [opposition leader](/wiki/Opposition_to_Vladimir_Putin_in_Russia "Opposition to Vladimir Putin in Russia") [Alexei Navalny](/wiki/Alexei_Navalny "Alexei Navalny") from their state sponsor of terrorism list despite his death a year ago. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/russia-wont-cancel-navalnys-terrorist-status-even-though-hes-dead-widow-says-2025-01-10/)
* [International reactions to the 2024 Venezuelan presidential election](/wiki/International_reactions_to_the_2024_Venezuelan_presidential_election "International reactions to the 2024 Venezuelan presidential election"), [United States–Venezuela relations](/wiki/United_States%E2%80%93Venezuela_relations "United States–Venezuela relations"), [Sanctions during the Venezuelan crisis](/wiki/Sanctions_during_the_Venezuelan_crisis "Sanctions during the Venezuelan crisis")
  + [U.S.](/wiki/U.S. "U.S.") authorities announce an increased $25 million reward for information leading to the arrest of [Venezuelan president](/wiki/President_of_Venezuela "President of Venezuela") [Nicolás Maduro](/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro "Nicolás Maduro"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c4g9ezyw0keo)
* [Vince McMahon sex trafficking scandal](/wiki/Vince_McMahon_sex_trafficking_scandal "Vince McMahon sex trafficking scandal")
  + The [U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission](/wiki/U.S._Securities_and_Exchange_Commission "U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission") announces that former [WWE](/wiki/WWE "WWE") CEO [Vince McMahon](/wiki/Vince_McMahon "Vince McMahon") has agreed to pay a $400,000 fine and reimburse $1.3 million to WWE as part of a settlement to drop [accounting fraud](/wiki/Accounting_fraud "Accounting fraud") charges. [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/10/business/wwe-vince-mcmahon-sec-settlement/index.html)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024 Venezuelan political crisis](/wiki/2024_Venezuelan_political_crisis "2024 Venezuelan political crisis")
  + [Third inauguration of Nicolás Maduro](/wiki/Third_inauguration_of_Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro "Third inauguration of Nicolás Maduro")
    - [Nicolás Maduro](/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro "Nicolás Maduro") is sworn in for a third six-year term as [President of Venezuela](/wiki/President_of_Venezuela "President of Venezuela") in [Caracas](/wiki/Caracas "Caracas"). The ceremony takes place under heavy security measures with the opposition boycotting and protesting the ceremony while continuing to insist that the legitimate president-elect is [Edmundo González Urrutia](/wiki/Edmundo_Gonz%C3%A1lez_Urrutia "Edmundo González Urrutia"). Many countries and international organizations also consider the [election](/wiki/2024_Venezuelan_presidential_election "2024 Venezuelan presidential election") to be fraudulent. [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/10/americas/venezuelas-nicolas-maduro-sworn-in-intl/index.html)
* [2024 Austrian legislative election](/wiki/2024_Austrian_legislative_election "2024 Austrian legislative election")
  + [Austrian president](/wiki/President_of_Austria "President of Austria") [Alexander Van der Bellen](/wiki/Alexander_Van_der_Bellen "Alexander Van der Bellen") appoints [foreign minister](/wiki/Foreign_Minister_of_Austria "Foreign Minister of Austria") [Alexander Schallenberg](/wiki/Alexander_Schallenberg "Alexander Schallenberg") as acting [chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_of_Austria "Chancellor of Austria") to succeed [Karl Nehammer](/wiki/Karl_Nehammer "Karl Nehammer"), who resigned six days ago. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/austrian-foreign-minister-schallenberg-takes-over-caretaker-chancellor-2025-01-10/)

January 11, 2025 (2025-01-11) (Saturday)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Israel–United States relations](/wiki/Israel%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Israel–United States relations"), [Calls for a ceasefire during the Gaza war](/wiki/Calls_for_a_ceasefire_during_the_Gaza_war "Calls for a ceasefire during the Gaza war")
    - Incoming [U.S.](/wiki/U.S. "U.S.") Middle East Envoy [Steve Witkoff](/wiki/Steve_Witkoff "Steve Witkoff") meets with [Israeli Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel "Prime Minister of Israel") [Benjamin Netanyahu](/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu "Benjamin Netanyahu") in an effort to secure a [ceasefire](/wiki/Ceasefire "Ceasefire") deal in [Gaza](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip") before [President-elect](/wiki/President-elect_of_the_United_States "President-elect of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump")'s [inauguration](/wiki/Second_inauguration_of_Donald_Trump "Second inauguration of Donald Trump") on January 20. [(Sky News)](https://news.sky.com/story/donald-trumps-middle-east-envoy-pushes-for-gaza-ceasefire-deal-ahead-of-us-inauguration-13287325)
    - Netanyahu sends [Mossad](/wiki/Mossad "Mossad") director [David Barnea](/wiki/David_Barnea "David Barnea") to ceasefire talks in [Doha](/wiki/Doha "Doha"), [Qatar](/wiki/Qatar "Qatar"). [(ABC News)](https://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/israels-netanyahu-sends-mossad-director-gaza-ceasefire-talks-117581245)
  + [Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip](/wiki/Israeli_bombing_of_the_Gaza_Strip "Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip")
    - An [Israeli airstrike](/wiki/Israeli_air_force "Israeli air force") on a school sheltering displaced civilians in [Jabalia](/wiki/Jabalia "Jabalia"), northern [Gaza](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip"), kills at least eight Palestinians and leaves 30 others injured. [(Middle East Monitor)](https://www.middleeastmonitor.com/20250111-israeli-strike-on-school-in-northern-gaza-kills-8-displaced-palestinians/)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Eastern Ukraine campaign](/wiki/Eastern_Ukraine_campaign "Eastern Ukraine campaign")
    - The [Russian Army](/wiki/Russian_Ground_Forces "Russian Ground Forces") says that it has gained control of the settlement of [Shevchenko](/wiki/Shevchenko%2C_Donetsk_Oblast "Shevchenko, Donetsk Oblast") in [Donetsk Oblast](/wiki/Donetsk_Oblast "Donetsk Oblast"), [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"). [(Anadolu Agency)](https://www.aa.com.tr/en/russia-ukraine-war/russia-claims-to-have-taken-control-of-another-village-in-ukraine/3447499)
  + [Kursk offensive](/wiki/2024_Kursk_offensive "2024 Kursk offensive"), [North Korean involvement in the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/North_Korean_involvement_in_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "North Korean involvement in the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
    - [Ukrainian President](/wiki/Ukrainian_President "Ukrainian President") [Volodymyr Zelenskyy](/wiki/Volodymyr_Zelenskyy "Volodymyr Zelenskyy") announces that Ukraine has captured two [North Korean](/wiki/North_Korea "North Korea") soldiers in healthy condition in [Kursk Oblast](/wiki/Kursk_Oblast "Kursk Oblast"), [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia"), for the first time since North Korea entered the war, as the two previous North Korean prisoners of war died of their injuries shortly following their capture. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/ukraine-captures-two-north-korean-soldiers-kursk-zelenskiy-says-2025-01-11/)
* [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)"), [War against the Islamic State](/wiki/War_against_the_Islamic_State "War against the Islamic State")
  + [Islamic State insurgency in Puntland](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland")
    - The [Puntland Security Force](/wiki/Puntland_Security_Force "Puntland Security Force") discover a cave used to store food by [ISIL](/wiki/Islamic_State "Islamic State") in the [Cal Miskaad](/wiki/Cal_Miskaad "Cal Miskaad") mountains, while killing and capturing insurgent fighters and destroying [improvised explosive devices](/wiki/Improvised_explosive_devices "Improvised explosive devices") and hideouts. The security force also took down three [drones](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") armed with explosives as they continue their offensive into [Bari region](/wiki/Bari%2C_Somalia "Bari, Somalia"), [Puntland](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland"). [(Garowe Online)](https://www.garoweonline.com/en/news/puntland/somalia-puntland-troops-make-gains-in-large-scale-offensive-against-isis) [(The Somali Digest)](https://thesomalidigest.com/puntland-advances-against-is-somalia-claims-fgs-is-compromised/) [(VOA)](https://www.voasomali.com/a/7933272.html)
* [Sudanese civil war](/wiki/Sudanese_civil_war_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Sudanese civil war (2023–present)")
  + [Battle of Wad Madani](/wiki/Battle_of_Wad_Madani "Battle of Wad Madani")
    - The [Sudanese Armed Forces](/wiki/Sudanese_Armed_Forces "Sudanese Armed Forces") say that they liberated [Wad Madani](/wiki/Wad_Madani "Wad Madani"), the capital of [Gezira State](/wiki/Gezira_State "Gezira State"), [Sudan](/wiki/Sudan "Sudan"), from the [Rapid Support Forces](/wiki/Rapid_Support_Forces "Rapid Support Forces"). [(Al Arabiya)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/middle-east/2025/01/11/sudan-government-spokesman-says-army-liberated-key-city-from-rsf-)
* [Myanmar civil war](/wiki/Myanmar_civil_war_%282021%E2%80%93present%29 "Myanmar civil war (2021–present)")
  + At least fifteen civilians are killed and 10 others are wounded in a [Tatmadaw](/wiki/Tatmadaw "Tatmadaw") airstrike on a market, targeting [Kachin Independence Army](/wiki/Kachin_Independence_Army "Kachin Independence Army") fighters, in [Tanai Township](/wiki/Tanai_Township "Tanai Township"), [Kachin State](/wiki/Kachin_State "Kachin State"), [Myanmar](/wiki/Myanmar "Myanmar"). [(*The Defense Post*)](https://thedefensepost.com/2025/01/12/myanmar-junta-air-strike-2/) [(*Daily Post*)](https://dailypost.ng/2025/01/12/myanmar-junta-air-strike-kills-15-civilians/)
* [Nigerian bandit conflict](/wiki/Nigerian_bandit_conflict "Nigerian bandit conflict")
  + Twenty-one [government-backed fighters](/wiki/Vigilante_Group_of_Nigeria "Vigilante Group of Nigeria") are killed during an [ambush](/wiki/Ambush "Ambush") against a convoy in [Baure](/wiki/Baure%2C_Nigeria "Baure, Nigeria"), [Katsina State](/wiki/Katsina_State "Katsina State"), [Nigeria](/wiki/Nigeria "Nigeria"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/11/bandits-in-nigeria-ambush-and-kill-21-government-backed-fighters)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - At least 939 [CDCR](/wiki/California_Department_of_Corrections_and_Rehabilitation "California Department of Corrections and Rehabilitation") inmates are deployed to fight the ongoing [wildfires](/wiki/Wildfire "Wildfire") in [Los Angeles County](/wiki/Los_Angeles_County "Los Angeles County"), [California](/wiki/California "California"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c3rwdjwglx2o)
    - The number of deaths in the California wildfires rises to 16. [(NBC)](https://www.nbcnews.com/news/us-news/california-wildfires-victims-rcna186989)
* [2024–25 South-West Indian Ocean cyclone season](/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_South-West_Indian_Ocean_cyclone_season "2024–25 South-West Indian Ocean cyclone season")
  + [France](/wiki/France "France") places the [Indian Ocean](/wiki/Indian_Ocean "Indian Ocean") island of [Mayotte](/wiki/Mayotte "Mayotte") on red alert due to approaching [Tropical Cyclone Dikeledi](/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_South-West_Indian_Ocean_cyclone_season#Tropical_Cyclone_Dikeledi "2024–25 South-West Indian Ocean cyclone season"), roughly one month after the [French overseas department](/wiki/French_overseas_department "French overseas department") was devastated by [Cyclone Chido](/wiki/Cyclone_Chido "Cyclone Chido"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/cyclone-battered-mayotte-be-put-red-alert-2025-01-11/)
* [Al-Bayda gas station explosion](/wiki/Al-Bayda_gas_station_explosion "Al-Bayda gas station explosion")
  + At least fifteen people are killed and 67 others are injured, including 40 critically, in an explosion at a gas station in [Al Bayda Governorate](/wiki/Al_Bayda_Governorate "Al Bayda Governorate"), [Yemen](/wiki/Yemen "Yemen"). [(CTV News)](https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/15-killed-in-an-explosion-and-fire-at-a-gas-station-in-central-yemen-1.7172825)
* [Most restaurant explosion](/wiki/Most_restaurant_explosion "Most restaurant explosion")
  + Six people are killed and eleven injured when a [propane-butane cylinder](/wiki/Bottled_gas "Bottled gas") explodes in a restaurant in [Most](/wiki/Most_%28city%29 "Most (city)"), [Czech Republic](/wiki/Czech_Republic "Czech Republic"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/six-killed-explosion-czech-restaurant-2025-01-12/) [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/czech-restaurant-explosion-leaves-several-dead/a-71276478)
* Two people are killed and eleven others are injured when a bus flips on its side on a highway near [Prenzlau](/wiki/Prenzlau "Prenzlau"), [Brandenburg](/wiki/Brandenburg "Brandenburg"), [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany"). [(CTV News)](https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/a-bus-accident-on-a-highway-in-northeastern-germany-leaves-two-dead-1.7172611)
* At least 50 people are injured when two [trams](/wiki/Tram "Tram") collide in a tunnel in [Strasbourg](/wiki/Strasbourg "Strasbourg"), [France](/wiki/France "France"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/france-two-trams-collide-in-strasbourg/a-71274743)

**International relations**

* [Ethiopia–Somalia relations](/wiki/Ethiopia%E2%80%93Somalia_relations "Ethiopia–Somalia relations")
  + [Ethiopian](/wiki/Ethiopia "Ethiopia") [prime minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Ethiopia "Prime Minister of Ethiopia") [Abiy Ahmed](/wiki/Abiy_Ahmed "Abiy Ahmed") and [Somali president](/wiki/President_of_Somalia "President of Somalia") [Hassan Sheikh Mohamud](/wiki/Hassan_Sheikh_Mohamud "Hassan Sheikh Mohamud") meet in [Addis Ababa](/wiki/Addis_Ababa "Addis Ababa"), Ethiopia, as part of a [Turkey](/wiki/Turkey "Turkey")-brokered [rapprochement](/wiki/Rapprochement "Rapprochement") to restore bilateral relations after a yearlong dispute due to the [2024 Ethiopia–Somaliland memorandum of understanding](/wiki/2024_Ethiopia%E2%80%93Somaliland_memorandum_of_understanding "2024 Ethiopia–Somaliland memorandum of understanding"). [(Bloomberg News)](https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2025-01-11/ethiopia-somalia-leaders-meet-agree-to-restore-relations)
* [Lebanon–Syria relations](/wiki/Lebanon%E2%80%93Syria_relations "Lebanon–Syria relations")
  + [Lebanese](/wiki/Lebanon "Lebanon") [prime minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Lebanon "Prime Minister of Lebanon") [Najib Mikati](/wiki/Najib_Mikati "Najib Mikati") and [Syrian](/wiki/Syria "Syria") [de facto leader](/wiki/First_Syrian_transitional_government "First Syrian transitional government") [Ahmed al-Sharaa](/wiki/Ahmed_al-Sharaa "Ahmed al-Sharaa") hold a meeting in [Damascus](/wiki/Damascus "Damascus"), Syria, the first time that the two countries have met since the [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war") began in 2011. [(24 Digital)](https://24newshd.tv/11-Jan-2025/lebanon-pm-visits-damascus-on-first-such-trip-since-before-syria-war) [(MTV)](https://www.mtv.com.lb/en/News/Local/1538189/photos--the-meeting-between-mikati-and-sharaa-in-damascus-has-just-kicked-off)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024 South Korean martial law crisis](/wiki/2024_South_Korean_martial_law_crisis "2024 South Korean martial law crisis")
  + Thousands of people demonstrate in [Seoul](/wiki/Seoul "Seoul"), [South Korea](/wiki/South_Korea "South Korea"), to protest against [President](/wiki/President_of_South_Korea "President of South Korea") [Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Yoon Suk Yeol") as he defies an [arrest warrant](/wiki/Arrest_warrant "Arrest warrant") from his attempt to institute [martial law](/wiki/Martial_law "Martial law") in December 2024. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/11/thousands-protest-in-south-korea-as-yoon-continues-to-resist-arrest) [(TRT World)](https://www.trtworld.com/asia/rival-protests-erupt-in-south-korea-as-arrest-looms-for-suspended-president-18252604)
* At least 12,000 people gather in [Riesa](/wiki/Riesa "Riesa"), [Saxony](/wiki/Saxony "Saxony"), [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany"), to protest an [Alternative for Germany](/wiki/Alternative_for_Germany "Alternative for Germany") convention as well as the party's [far-right](/wiki/Far-right_politics_in_Germany_%281945%E2%80%93present%29 "Far-right politics in Germany (1945–present)") views. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/11/german-protesters-attempt-to-block-far-right-afd-congress)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Gaza war hostage crisis](/wiki/Gaza_war_hostage_crisis "Gaza war hostage crisis")
    - An [Israeli](/wiki/Israel "Israel") security delegation arrives in [Qatar](/wiki/Qatar "Qatar") for talks regarding a [ceasefire](/wiki/Ceasefire "Ceasefire") deal and the release of Israeli hostages in [Gaza](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/top-israeli-security-delegation-doha-gaza-talks-2025-01-12/)
  + [Israel–United States relations](/wiki/Israel%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Israel–United States relations"), [Calls for a ceasefire during the Gaza war](/wiki/Calls_for_a_ceasefire_during_the_Gaza_war "Calls for a ceasefire during the Gaza war")
    - [Israeli Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel "Prime Minister of Israel") [Benjamin Netanyahu](/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu "Benjamin Netanyahu") and [U.S. President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Joe Biden](/wiki/Joe_Biden "Joe Biden") discuss efforts to reach a deal to solve the [hostage crisis](/wiki/Israel%E2%80%93Hamas_war_hostage_crisis "Israel–Hamas war hostage crisis") as well as a [ceasefire](/wiki/Ceasefire "Ceasefire") to end the war. [(*USA Today*)](https://www.usatoday.com/story/news/world/israel-hamas/2025/01/12/biden-netanyahu-israel-hamas-hostage-cease-fire/77655633007/)
  + [Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip](/wiki/Israeli_bombing_of_the_Gaza_Strip "Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip")
    - At least eight [Palestinians](/wiki/Palestinians "Palestinians") are killed in [Israeli airstrikes](/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force "Israeli Air Force") on areas of the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip"). [(Xinhua)](https://english.news.cn/20250113/007ceff485b8479eb2a6bcb634f2f354/c.html)
* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [M23 offensive](/wiki/M23_offensive_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "M23 offensive (2022–present)")
    - The [Army of the Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Armed Forces of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") says that over the days it has recaptured several towns that fell to [M23 rebels](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") and other armed groups in [North Kivu](/wiki/North_Kivu "North Kivu") and [South Kivu](/wiki/South_Kivu "South Kivu") provinces.[(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/congo-rebels-northkivu-goma-44d802cead4adde2b9aea5515bb83172)
* [Nigerian bandit conflict](/wiki/Nigerian_bandit_conflict "Nigerian bandit conflict")
  + At least 40 people are killed during an attack by [Boko Haram](/wiki/Boko_Haram "Boko Haram") gunmen in Dumba, [Borno State](/wiki/Borno_State "Borno State"), [Nigeria](/wiki/Nigeria "Nigeria"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/nigeria-massacre-boho-haram-3579523f5f1b978ea7d32b4374c8e036)
  + At least 16 civilians are killed in an [airstrike](/wiki/Airstrike "Airstrike") conducted by the [Nigerian Air Force](/wiki/Nigerian_Air_Force "Nigerian Air Force") in [Zamfara State](/wiki/Zamfara_State "Zamfara State"), apparently after being mistaken for criminal gangs. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cn0y30766kjo)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - [California Governor](/wiki/Governor_of_California "Governor of California") [Gavin Newsom](/wiki/Gavin_Newsom "Gavin Newsom") states that the ongoing [wildfires](/wiki/Wildfire "Wildfire") impacting [Los Angeles County](/wiki/Los_Angeles_County%2C_California "Los Angeles County, California") could become the worst [natural disaster](/wiki/Natural_disaster "Natural disaster") in [American](/wiki/United_States "United States") history "in terms of the scale and scope", amid current estimated damages of more than [US$](/wiki/United_States_dollar "United States dollar")135 billion. [(*The Independent*)](https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/americas/fires-los-angeles-california-palisades-map-victim-latest-updates-b2677814.html) [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/meet-the-press/video/gov-newsom-says-l-a-wildfires-could-be-worst-natural-disaster-in-u-s-history-full-interview-229078085843)
    - The death toll from the wildfires increases to 24. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/ckgy0pyvglpo)
    - Officials say that the [Kenneth Fire](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires#Kenneth_Fire "January 2025 Southern California wildfires") has been contained. [(KCAL-TV)](https://www.cbsnews.com/losangeles/news/kenneth-fire-evacuations-in-west-hills-area/)
* A bus crashed on a highway in [Al-Loud](/w/index.php?title=Al-Loud&action=edit&redlink=1 "Al-Loud (page does not exist)"), [Libya](/wiki/Libya "Libya"), killing 23 and injuring five. [(Xinhua News Agency)](https://english.news.cn/20250113/ab96976fd65b4bf4b25ab9da5f04f002/c.html)
* Ten people are killed and several others are injured after large floods engulf the city of [Ipatinga](/wiki/Ipatinga "Ipatinga") in [Minas Gerais](/wiki/Minas_Gerais "Minas Gerais"), [Brazil](/wiki/Brazil "Brazil"). [(BBC)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cvglwd34l81o.amp)
* A bus fell down a 100-meter gorge in [Pauri Garhwal district](/wiki/Pauri_Garhwal_district "Pauri Garhwal district"), [Uttarakhand](/wiki/Uttarakhand "Uttarakhand"), [India](/wiki/India "India"), killing six and injuring 22. [(The Tribune)](https://www.tribuneindia.com/news/india/5-die-17-injured-as-bus-falls-into-gorge-in-uttarakhands-pauri/)
* Three people are killed and two others are injured in an [avalanche](/wiki/Avalanche "Avalanche") in [Trasquera](/wiki/Trasquera "Trasquera"), [Province of Verbano-Cusio-Ossola](/wiki/Province_of_Verbano-Cusio-Ossola "Province of Verbano-Cusio-Ossola"), [Italy](/wiki/Italy "Italy"). [(Rai News)](https://www.rainews.it/articoli/2025/01/valanga-travolge-scialpinisti-in-piemonte-3-morti-e-2-feriti-trasquera-verbano-cusio-ossola-0186dba0-f920-4286-95de-4f72db97dbd4.html)
* At least 17 miners are trapped in a gold mine in [La Libertad Department](/wiki/Department_of_La_Libertad "Department of La Libertad"), [Peru](/wiki/Peru "Peru"), after a group of illegal miners attacked the mine. [(Xinhua)](https://english.news.cn/20250114/c17952037b594df4bdc2e8f0b23c8099/c.html)

  + The [Bangladeshi](/wiki/Bangladesh "Bangladesh") [IEDCR](/wiki/Institute_of_Epidemiology%2C_Disease_Control_and_Research "Institute of Epidemiology, Disease Control and Research") reports the country's first case of [HMPV](/wiki/Human_metapneumovirus "Human metapneumovirus") in [Bhairab](/wiki/Bhairab "Bhairab"), [Dhaka Division](/wiki/Dhaka_Division "Dhaka Division"), Bangladesh.   + [German Foreign Minister](/wiki/Minister_for_Foreign_Affairs_%28Germany%29 "Minister for Foreign Affairs (Germany)") [Annalena Baerbock](/wiki/Annalena_Baerbock "Annalena Baerbock") pledges [€](/wiki/Euro "Euro")50 million in food, emergency shelters, and medical care to [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria") following talks with the [Syrian transitional government](/wiki/First_Syrian_transitional_government "First Syrian transitional government") in [Riyadh](/wiki/Riyadh "Riyadh"), [Saudi Arabia](/wiki/Saudi_Arabia "Saudi Arabia"). * [2024–25 Croatian presidential election](/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_Croatian_presidential_election "2024–25 Croatian presidential election")
  + [Croatians](/wiki/Croatians "Croatians") vote in the second round to elect the [president](/wiki/President_of_Croatia "President of Croatia") between incumbent [Zoran Milanović](/wiki/Zoran_Milanovi%C4%87 "Zoran Milanović") and former [science and education minister](/wiki/Ministry_of_Science_and_Education_%28Croatia%29 "Ministry of Science and Education (Croatia)") [Dragan Primorac](/wiki/Dragan_Primorac "Dragan Primorac"). [(*The Dubrovnik Times*)](https://www.thedubrovniktimes.com/news/croatia/item/17378-croatia-votes-presidential-election-enters-decisive-second-round) [(*Sarajevo Times*)](https://sarajevotimes.com/croatia-set-to-elect-president-in-pivotal-second-round-of-elections-2/)
* [2025 Comorian parliamentary election](/wiki/2025_Comorian_parliamentary_election "2025 Comorian parliamentary election")
  + Voters in [Comoros](/wiki/Comoros "Comoros") elect the 33 members of the [Assembly of the Union](/wiki/Assembly_of_the_Union_of_the_Comoros "Assembly of the Union of the Comoros"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/voters-comoros-head-polls-elect-33-seat-parliament-2025-01-12/)
* [Ilza Amado Vaz](/wiki/Ilza_Amado_Vaz "Ilza Amado Vaz") unexpectedly resigns as [Prime Minister of São Tomé and Príncipe](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "Prime Minister of São Tomé and Príncipe") three days after being appointed Prime Minister by [President](/wiki/President_of_S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "President of São Tomé and Príncipe") [Carlos Vila Nova](/wiki/Carlos_Vila_Nova "Carlos Vila Nova"). The ruling [Independent Democratic Action](/wiki/Independent_Democratic_Action "Independent Democratic Action") party then proposes Adelino Pereira to replace Vaz, but Vila Nova appoints [Américo d'Oliveira dos Ramos](/wiki/Am%C3%A9rico_Ramos "Américo Ramos"). [(Xinhua 1)](https://english.news.cn/20250113/2fd3f6c7f9e148fbb544e1e0c52e0a10/c.html), [(Xinhua 2)](https://english.news.cn/africa/20250113/bb2a5df8aecd44b58c904f3a522c43d3/c.html)

January 13, 2025 (2025-01-13) (Monday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_13&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_13&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_13&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)")
  + [War against the Islamic State](/wiki/War_against_the_Islamic_State "War against the Islamic State")
    - [Islamic State insurgency in Puntland](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland")
      * Twenty-six [Islamic State](/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_Somalia_Province "Islamic State – Somalia Province") militants are allegedly killed, including a female combatant and two soldiers, and several others are injured when [Puntland forces](/wiki/Puntland_Security_Force "Puntland Security Force") capture eight Islamic State bases during [ongoing offensive military operations](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland#Clashes "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland") in [Bari](/wiki/Bari%2C_Somalia "Bari, Somalia"), [Puntland](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland"), [Somalia](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia"). [(Idil News)](https://www.idilnews.com/puntland-forces-kill-26-isis-militants-in-major-offensive-in-bari-region/) [(AFP)](https://www.barrons.com/news/several-is-fighters-killed-in-somalia-s-puntland-state-9950d700)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Gaza war hostage crisis](/wiki/Gaza_war_hostage_crisis "Gaza war hostage crisis"), [Calls for a ceasefire during the Gaza war](/wiki/Calls_for_a_ceasefire_during_the_Gaza_war "Calls for a ceasefire during the Gaza war")
    - According to two [Israeli](/wiki/Israel "Israel") officials, [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") is expected to release 33 hostages during the first phase of an [emerging ceasefire agreement](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire") being finalized by negotiators in [Doha](/wiki/Doha "Doha"), [Qatar](/wiki/Qatar "Qatar"). [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/01/13/middleeast/hamas-33-hostages-israel-ceasefire-talks-intl-latam)
* [Israeli invasion of Lebanon](/wiki/Israeli_invasion_of_Lebanon_%282024%E2%80%93present%29 "Israeli invasion of Lebanon (2024–present)")
  + [2024 Israel–Lebanon ceasefire agreement](/wiki/2024_Israel%E2%80%93Lebanon_ceasefire_agreement "2024 Israel–Lebanon ceasefire agreement")
    - The [Israel Defense Forces](/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces "Israel Defense Forces") strike several [Hezbollah](/wiki/Hezbollah "Hezbollah") sites in [Lebanon](/wiki/Lebanon "Lebanon"), alleging that the targets violated the terms of the ceasefire agreement. [(*The Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/idf-says-it-hit-hezbollah-sites-after-ceasefire-monitors-failed-to-address-threats/)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Attacks in Russia during the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Attacks_in_Russia_during_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Attacks in Russia during the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
    - [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia") accuses [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine") of targeting the Russkaya compressor station in the [Krasnodar Krai](/wiki/Krasnodar_Krai "Krasnodar Krai"), which feeds gas for the [TurkStream pipeline](/wiki/TurkStream "TurkStream"), in a failed drone attack two days ago. [(S&P Global)](https://www.spglobal.com/commodity-insights/en/news-research/latest-news/natural-gas/011325-gas-market-on-alert-after-russia-claims-ukrainian-attack-on-turkstream-station)
* [Sudanese Civil War](/wiki/Sudanese_civil_war_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Sudanese civil war (2023–present)")
  + [Battle of Khartoum](/wiki/Battle_of_Khartoum_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Battle of Khartoum (2023–present)")
    - The [shelling](/wiki/Shell_%28projectile%29 "Shell (projectile)") of an area of [Omdurman](/wiki/Omdurman "Omdurman"), [Khartoum State](/wiki/Khartoum_State "Khartoum State"), [Sudan](/wiki/Sudan "Sudan"), results in the death of at least 120 civilians, according to volunteer rescuers. [(Al Arabiya News)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/middle-east/2025/01/14/sudan-rescuers-say-more-than-120-killed-by-shelling-near-capital)

**Business and economy**

* A [general strike](/wiki/General_strikes_in_Belgium "General strikes in Belgium") by [Belgian](/wiki/Belgium "Belgium") unions to protest against government plans for [pension](/wiki/Pension "Pension") reform occurs, with the work stoppages severely disrupting public transport in [Brussels](/wiki/Brussels "Brussels") as well as [rail](/wiki/Rail_transport_in_Belgium "Rail transport in Belgium") and [air travel](/wiki/List_of_airports_in_Belgium "List of airports in Belgium") throughout the country. [(Politico)](https://www.politico.eu/article/belgian-transport-faces-severe-disruption-monday-by-national-strike/)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - [AccuWeather](/wiki/AccuWeather "AccuWeather") releases a preliminary estimate of the total physical and economic losses caused by the ongoing [wildfires](/wiki/Wildfire "Wildfire") in [Southern California](/wiki/Southern_California "Southern California") of between [$](/wiki/United_States_dollar "United States dollar")250–275 billion, a figure attributed to exceptionally high property values in and near [Santa Monica](/wiki/Santa_Monica "Santa Monica"), which would surpass their estimates of the costs of the entire [2020 United States wildfire season](/wiki/2020_Western_United_States_wildfire_season "2020 Western United States wildfire season") as well as [Hurricane Helene](/wiki/Hurricane_Helene "Hurricane Helene") in 2024. [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/weather/wildfires/live-blog/california-wildfires-live-updates-santa-ana-winds-continue-rcna187351)
* Twelve people are killed and many others are missing in a [landslide](/wiki/Landslide "Landslide") in [Hpakant](/wiki/Hpakant "Hpakant"), [Kachin State](/wiki/Kachin_State "Kachin State"), [Myanmar](/wiki/Myanmar "Myanmar"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/myanmar-jade-mine-landslide-e39761fcf484acf3ecc53576d3810692)

**Law and crime**

* [Venezuelan](/wiki/Venezuela "Venezuela") attorney general [Tarek Saab](/wiki/Tarek_Saab "Tarek Saab") asks for an [arrest warrant](/wiki/Arrest_warrant "Arrest warrant") and a [red notice](/wiki/Red_notice "Red notice") from [Interpol](/wiki/Interpol "Interpol") against opposition figure [Leopoldo López](/wiki/Leopoldo_L%C3%B3pez "Leopoldo López"), who is currently in exile. Venezuela accuses López of instigating the use of arms against the state and [treason](/wiki/Treason "Treason"), among other charges. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/venezuela-ag-requests-warrant-interpol-notice-against-opposition-figure-living-2025-01-13/)
* A judge in [Peru](/wiki/Peru "Peru") dismisses charges of [money laundering](/wiki/Money_laundering "Money laundering") against [Popular Force](/wiki/Popular_Force "Popular Force") leader and former presidential candidate [Keiko Fujimori](/wiki/Keiko_Fujimori "Keiko Fujimori"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/peru-judge-throws-out-keiko-fujimoris-money-laundering-trial-2025-01-13/)

**Politics and elections**

* [Impeachment of Sara Duterte](/wiki/Impeachment_of_Sara_Duterte "Impeachment of Sara Duterte")
  + Members of the [Iglesia ni Cristo](/wiki/Iglesia_ni_Cristo "Iglesia ni Cristo") hold a nationwide [National Rally for Peace](/wiki/National_Rally_for_Peace "National Rally for Peace") in the [Philippines](/wiki/Philippines "Philippines") to express their disapproval of impeachment efforts against [Vice President](/wiki/Vice_President_of_the_Philippines "Vice President of the Philippines") [Sara Duterte](/wiki/Sara_Duterte "Sara Duterte"). [(Rappler)](https://www.rappler.com/philippines/photos-iglesia-ni-cristo-national-rally-peace-january-13-2025/)
* [International Court of Justice](/wiki/International_Court_of_Justice "International Court of Justice") President [Nawaf Salam](/wiki/Nawaf_Salam "Nawaf Salam") becomes the [prime minister-designate](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Lebanon "Prime Minister of Lebanon") of [Lebanon](/wiki/Lebanon "Lebanon") after winning an absolute majority of votes from [parliament](/wiki/Parliament_of_Lebanon "Parliament of Lebanon"), while stepping down from the ICJ. [(TVN24)](https://tvn24.pl/swiat/liban-prezes-mts-nawaf-salam-otrzymal-misje-tworzenia-rzadu-st8259027)[(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/13/middleeast/icj-judge-nawaf-salam-lebanon-prime-minister-intl/index.html)

January 14, 2025 (2025-01-14) (Tuesday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_14&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_14&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_14&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Gaza war hostage crisis](/wiki/Gaza_war_hostage_crisis "Gaza war hostage crisis"), [Calls for a ceasefire during the Gaza war](/wiki/Calls_for_a_ceasefire_during_the_Gaza_war "Calls for a ceasefire during the Gaza war")
    - [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") officials say that they have accepted a [draft agreement for a potential ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire") as well as the release of [hostages](/wiki/Gaza_war_hostage_crisis "Gaza war hostage crisis"). Mediators in the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") and [Qatar](/wiki/Qatar "Qatar") also state that this is the closest that both sides have been to a ceasefire agreement so far. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-war-news-01-14-2025-a1495c0f4f13102903ce31a862c49baa)
  + [Israeli incursions in the West Bank](/wiki/Israeli_incursions_in_the_West_Bank_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Israeli incursions in the West Bank (2023–present)")
    - Four [Al-Qassam Brigades](/wiki/Al-Qassam_Brigades "Al-Qassam Brigades") militants and two civilians are killed during an Israeli [airstrike](/wiki/Airstrike "Airstrike") in [Jenin](/wiki/Jenin "Jenin"), in the occupied [West Bank](/wiki/West_Bank "West Bank"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2025/1/15/live-israel-launches-fierce-strikes-on-gaza-as-ceasefire-deal-moves-closer?update=3442835)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Attacks in Russia during the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Attacks_in_Russia_during_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Attacks in Russia during the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
    - [Ukraine](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_Ukraine "Armed Forces of Ukraine") strikes targets in the [Republic of Tatarstan](/wiki/Republic_of_Tatarstan "Republic of Tatarstan") and [Bryansk](/wiki/Bryansk_Oblast "Bryansk Oblast"), [Saratov](/wiki/Saratov_Oblast "Saratov Oblast"), and [Tula](/wiki/Tula_Oblast "Tula Oblast") oblasts, [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia"), with more than 200 drones and five [ATACMS](/wiki/ATACMS "ATACMS") ballistic missiles, hitting ammunition depots, industrial plants and a [refinery](/wiki/Refinery "Refinery"), in what [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine") says is its "most massive" and "deepest" attack inside Russia so far. [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/14/europe/ukraine-russia-drone-missile-attack-intl-hnk/index.html) [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cwypg2z780go)
* [North Korean missile tests](/wiki/List_of_North_Korean_missile_tests "List of North Korean missile tests")
  + [North Korea](/wiki/Korean_People%27s_Army "Korean People's Army") launches multiple [short-range ballistic missiles](/wiki/Short-range_ballistic_missile "Short-range ballistic missile") into the [Sea of Japan](/wiki/Sea_of_Japan "Sea of Japan"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/north-korea-fires-missile-off-east-coast-says-south-korea-military-2025-01-14/)
* [Red Sea crisis](/wiki/Red_Sea_crisis "Red Sea crisis")
  + [Yemen](/wiki/Yemen "Yemen")'s [Houthi](/wiki/Houthi "Houthi") forces fire a missile at [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel"), triggering [sirens](/wiki/Civil_defense_siren "Civil defense siren") in several areas, including [Tel Aviv](/wiki/Tel_Aviv "Tel Aviv") and some Israeli settlements in the occupied [West Bank](/wiki/West_Bank "West Bank"). According to the [Israeli military](/wiki/Israeli_Defense_Forces "Israeli Defense Forces"), the missile was "likely intercepted" with no injuries reported. [(Xinhua)](https://english.news.cn/20250114/7d596dc7d5e6418683867e53dbecb391/c.html)

**Disasters and accidents**

* At least 43 vehicles figured in a pileup caused by icy conditions along the [Seoul](/wiki/Seoul "Seoul")-[Munsan](/wiki/Munsan "Munsan") Expressway near [Goyang](/wiki/Goyang "Goyang"), injuring nine. [(Yonhap News Agency)](https://en.yna.co.kr/view/AEN20250114002500315)

**Health and environment**

* The [World Health Organization](/wiki/World_Health_Organization "World Health Organization") reports a suspected [Marburg virus](/wiki/Marburg_virus_disease "Marburg virus disease") outbreak in [Kagera](/wiki/Kagera_Region "Kagera Region"), [Tanzania](/wiki/Tanzania "Tanzania"), with nine cases and eight deaths. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/suspected-outbreak-marburg-virus-kills-eight-tanzania-who-says-2025-01-15/)

**International relations**

* [2024 Baltic Sea submarine cable disruptions](/wiki/2024_Baltic_Sea_submarine_cable_disruptions "2024 Baltic Sea submarine cable disruptions"), [NATO operations](/wiki/List_of_NATO_operations "List of NATO operations")
  + At the Summit of Baltic Sea Allies in [Helsinki](/wiki/Helsinki "Helsinki"), [Finland](/wiki/Finland "Finland"), [NATO Secretary General](/wiki/Secretary_General_of_NATO "Secretary General of NATO") [Mark Rutte](/wiki/Mark_Rutte "Mark Rutte") announces the establishment of the *Baltic Sentry* military mission, which will strengthen the protection of critical infrastructure in the region, such as [energy](/wiki/Submarine_power_cable "Submarine power cable") and [communication cables](/wiki/Submarine_communications_cable "Submarine communications cable"), from "destabilizing acts". [(NATO News)](https://www.nato.int/cps/cz/natohq/news_232122.htm?selectedLocale=en)
* [Armenia–United States relations](/wiki/Armenia%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Armenia–United States relations")
  + The [Armenian Foreign Minister](/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_%28Armenia%29 "Ministry of Foreign Affairs (Armenia)"), [Ararat Mirzoyan](/wiki/Ararat_Mirzoyan "Ararat Mirzoyan"), and the [U.S. Secretary of State](/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_State "United States Secretary of State"), [Antony Blinken](/wiki/Antony_Blinken "Antony Blinken"), sign in [Washington, DC](/wiki/Washington%2C_DC "Washington, DC") a Strategic Partnership Charter between [Armenia](/wiki/Armenia "Armenia") and the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"). [(The Defense Post)](https://thedefensepost.com/2025/01/14/armenia-signs-us-pact/)
* [Cuba–United States relations](/wiki/Cuba%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Cuba–United States relations")
  + [U.S. President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Joe Biden](/wiki/Joe_Biden "Joe Biden") announces that the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") will remove [Cuba](/wiki/Cuba "Cuba") from its [state sponsors of terrorism list](/wiki/State_Sponsors_of_Terrorism_%28U.S._list%29 "State Sponsors of Terrorism (U.S. list)") as part of a prisoner release deal. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c17e0k92g41o)

**Law and crime**

* [2024 South Korean martial law crisis](/wiki/2024_South_Korean_martial_law_crisis "2024 South Korean martial law crisis")
  + [Arrest of Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Arrest_of_Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Arrest of Yoon Suk Yeol")
    - A military unit assigned to guard the presidential residence of [impeached](/wiki/Impeachment_of_Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Impeachment of Yoon Suk Yeol") [South Korean President](/wiki/President_of_South_Korea "President of South Korea") [Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Yoon Suk Yeol") approves the entry of [anti-corruption officials](/wiki/Corruption_Investigation_Office_for_High-ranking_Officials "Corruption Investigation Office for High-ranking Officials") and police, which is contested by the [Presidential Security Service](/wiki/Presidential_Security_Service_%28South_Korea%29 "Presidential Security Service (South Korea)"). [(Yonhap)](https://en.yna.co.kr/view/AEN20250114011453320?section=national/politics)
  + The [Constitutional Court of South Korea](/wiki/Constitutional_Court_of_South_Korea "Constitutional Court of South Korea") adjourns the opening session of Yoon Suk Yeol's impeachment trial after Yoon failed to attend the session due to alleged safety concerns. [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/news/world/impeachment-trial-south-koreas-yoon-adjourned-not-attend-rcna187549) [(Xinhua)](https://english.news.cn/20250112/45dfd6352df4438ea412380d3f2df56e/c.html)
* [Moldova](/wiki/Moldova "Moldova") detains former [Kyrgyzstan](/wiki/Kyrgyzstan "Kyrgyzstan") presidential advisor Aidar Khalikov, who has accused [Kyrgyz President](/wiki/President_of_Kyrgyzstan "President of Kyrgyzstan") [Sadyr Japarov](/wiki/Sadyr_Japarov "Sadyr Japarov") of corruption and [election rigging](/wiki/Electoral_fraud "Electoral fraud"). [(OCCRP)](https://www.occrp.org/en/news/moldova-detains-ex-kyrgyz-advisor-who-accused-president-japarov-of-graft)

**Politics and elections**

* [British](/wiki/United_Kingdom "United Kingdom") [Treasury](/wiki/HM_Treasury "HM Treasury") [Economic Secretary](/wiki/Economic_Secretary_to_the_Treasury "Economic Secretary to the Treasury") [Tulip Siddiq](/wiki/Tulip_Siddiq "Tulip Siddiq") resigns amid an [anti-corruption](/wiki/Anti-corruption "Anti-corruption") investigation in [Bangladesh](/wiki/Bangladesh "Bangladesh") involving [her family](/wiki/Tungipara_Sheikh_family "Tungipara Sheikh family"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/live/crmnjjm9j12t)
* The new [Government](/wiki/Government_of_S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "Government of São Tomé and Príncipe") of [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "Prime Minister of São Tomé and Príncipe") [Américo Ramos](/wiki/Am%C3%A9rico_Ramos "Américo Ramos") is sworn in [São Tomé and Príncipe](/wiki/S%C3%A3o_Tom%C3%A9_and_Pr%C3%ADncipe "São Tomé and Príncipe"). [(Xinhua)](https://english.news.cn/20250115/62c12ba528404f3b923b3a6f6853de7f/c.html)

**Science and technology**

* The [government](/wiki/Government_of_Venezuela "Government of Venezuela") of [Venezuela](/wiki/Venezuela "Venezuela") lifts its ban on the [social media](/wiki/Social_media "Social media") and [instant messaging](/wiki/Instant_messaging "Instant messaging") app [Telegram](/wiki/Telegram_%28software%29 "Telegram (software)"). [(TechRadar)](https://www.techradar.com/vpn/vpn-privacy-security/venezuela-lifts-telegram-ban-but-the-internet-remains-restricted)

January 15, 2025 (2025-01-15) (Wednesday)
