**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Allied Democratic Forces insurgency](/wiki/Allied_Democratic_Forces_insurgency "Allied Democratic Forces insurgency")
  + [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
    - [Allied Democratic Forces](/wiki/Allied_Democratic_Forces "Allied Democratic Forces") militants kill ten people in an attack on a village in [North Kivu](/wiki/North_Kivu "North Kivu"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/congo-islamic-rebel-attack-adf-kivu-makoko-faae44fe327d54ca619acd7c3fb30104)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [2025 Gaza war ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire")
    - [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel") and [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") reach a diplomatic agreement mediated by [Egypt](/wiki/Egypt "Egypt"), [Qatar](/wiki/Qatar "Qatar"), and the [U.S.](/wiki/U.S. "U.S.") to initiate a [ceasefire](/wiki/Ceasefire "Ceasefire") and an end to military operations in the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip"), as well as to facilitate the exchange of [hostages](/wiki/Gaza_war_hostage_crisis "Gaza war hostage crisis") and [prisoners](/wiki/Palestinians_in_Israeli_custody "Palestinians in Israeli custody"), marking the first major cessation of hostilities since [November 2023](/wiki/2023_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2023 Gaza war ceasefire"). [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/world/live-news/israel-hamas-gaza-ceasefire-hostages-01-15-24/index.html)
* [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war")
  + [Israeli invasion of Syria](/wiki/Israeli_invasion_of_Syria_%282024%E2%80%93present%29 "Israeli invasion of Syria (2024–present)")
    - The [Israeli Air Force](/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force "Israeli Air Force") strikes a [Hay'at Tahrir al-Sham](/wiki/Hay%27at_Tahrir_al-Sham "Hay'at Tahrir al-Sham") (HTS) vehicle convoy in [Quneitra Governorate](/wiki/Quneitra_Governorate "Quneitra Governorate"), [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria"), killing two HTS personnel and the mayor of a local village. It is the first time that Israel has targeted HTS forces since the [fall of the Assad regime](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Assad_regime "Fall of the Assad regime"). [(Al Arabiya)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/middle-east/2025/01/15/first-israel-strike-on-new-syria-security-forces-kills-3-medical-source-monitor)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Russian strikes against Ukrainian infrastructure](/wiki/Russian_strikes_against_Ukrainian_infrastructure_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "Russian strikes against Ukrainian infrastructure (2022–present)")
    - [Russia](/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces "Russian Armed Forces") launches a major ballistic and [cruise missile](/wiki/Cruise_missile "Cruise missile") attack on regions across [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"), targeting energy production and compelling authorities to shut down the power grid. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/russia-ukraine-war-massive-attack-power-cuts-2dc7a30e36c9eca3e874476374c21eba)
* [Red Sea crisis](/wiki/Red_Sea_crisis "Red Sea crisis")
  + [Yemen](/wiki/Yemen "Yemen")'s [Houthi movement](/wiki/Houthi_movement "Houthi movement") claims that it launched a missile attack targeting the [USS *Harry S. Truman*](/wiki/USS_Harry_S._Truman "USS Harry S. Truman") [aircraft carrier](/wiki/Aircraft_carrier "Aircraft carrier") and accompanying warships of the [United States Navy](/wiki/United_States_Navy "United States Navy") in the [Red Sea](/wiki/Red_Sea "Red Sea"). [(Anadolu Agency)](https://www.aa.com.tr/en/middle-east/yemen-s-houthis-claim-missile-drone-attack-on-us-aircraft-carrier-in-red-sea/3451441)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 Istanbul alcohol poisonings](/wiki/2025_Istanbul_alcohol_poisonings "2025 Istanbul alcohol poisonings")
  + [Bootleg alcohol](/wiki/Moonshine "Moonshine") kills 37 people and leaves 80 others hospitalized over the last 48 hours in [Istanbul](/wiki/Istanbul "Istanbul"), [Turkey](/wiki/Turkey "Turkey"). Turkish health officials say many of those in hospital are in [intensive care](/wiki/Intensive_care_medicine "Intensive care medicine"). [(ABC News)](https://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/bootleg-alcohol-claims-lives-30-people-istanbul-dozens-117746365)
* [Stilfontein mine deaths](/wiki/Stilfontein_mine_deaths "Stilfontein mine deaths")
  + Seventy-eight bodies of workers are retrieved from a closed [illegal](/wiki/Illegal_mining "Illegal mining") [gold mine](/wiki/Gold_mine "Gold mine") in [Stilfontein](/wiki/Stilfontein "Stilfontein"), [North West Province](/wiki/North_West_%28South_African_province%29 "North West (South African province)"), [South Africa](/wiki/South_Africa "South Africa") following a months-long siege by [police](/wiki/South_African_Police_Service "South African Police Service"). Over 200 survivors are arrested as they exit the mine. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/body-count-south-african-mine-rescue-operation-rises-60-2025-01-15/)

**Health and environment**

* The [U.S.](/wiki/U.S. "U.S.") [Food and Drug Administration](/wiki/Food_and_Drug_Administration "Food and Drug Administration") bans the usage of [Red No. 3](/wiki/Red_No._3 "Red No. 3") artificial [food coloring](/wiki/Food_coloring "Food coloring"), due to research showing that the food coloring is [carcinogenic](/wiki/Carcinogen "Carcinogen"). [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/health/health-news/fda-bans-red-no-3-artificial-coloring-beverages-candy-rcna185479)

**International relations**

* [Poland–Russia relations](/wiki/Poland%E2%80%93Russia_relations "Poland–Russia relations")
  + [Polish](/wiki/Poland "Poland") [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Poland "Prime Minister of Poland") [Donald Tusk](/wiki/Donald_Tusk "Donald Tusk") accuses [Russian](/wiki/Russia "Russia") [President](/wiki/President_of_Russia "President of Russia") [Vladimir Putin](/wiki/Vladimir_Putin "Vladimir Putin") and his country of [plotting terror attacks](/wiki/State-sponsored_terrorism "State-sponsored terrorism") on [airliners](/wiki/Airliner "Airliner") around the world. [(*The Independent*)](https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/ukraine-russia-war-live-putin-storm-shadow-missiles-b2679782.html)

**Law and crime**

* [2024 South Korean martial law crisis](/wiki/2024_South_Korean_martial_law_crisis "2024 South Korean martial law crisis")
  + [Arrest of Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Arrest_of_Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Arrest of Yoon Suk Yeol")
    - [Anti-corruption officials](/wiki/Corruption_Investigation_Office_for_High-ranking_Officials "Corruption Investigation Office for High-ranking Officials") and police attempt to breach the [residence](/wiki/Office_of_the_President_of_South_Korea "Office of the President of South Korea") of [impeached](/wiki/Impeachment_of_Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Impeachment of Yoon Suk Yeol") [South Korean president](/wiki/President_of_South_Korea "President of South Korea") [Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Yoon Suk Yeol") for a second time in order to execute an [arrest warrant](/wiki/Arrest_warrant "Arrest warrant"), while facing resistance from the [Presidential Security Service](/wiki/Presidential_Security_Service_%28South_Korea%29 "Presidential Security Service (South Korea)"), [People Power Party](/wiki/People_Power_Party_%28South_Korea%29 "People Power Party (South Korea)") lawmakers, and pro-Yoon protesters. Following a five-hour standoff, Yoon is arrested, becoming [South Korea](/wiki/South_Korea "South Korea")'s first sitting president to be arrested. [(Yonhap)](https://www.yna.co.kr/view/AKR20250115005200004?rec_id=1736900123005&site=recommendation_view) [(Yonhap 2)](https://www.yna.co.kr/view/AKR20250115069851001) [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/south-korea-yoon-martial-law-detain-8dd7f03661be39729741de9a3b5d1714)
* [2024 drone sightings](/wiki/2024_drone_sightings "2024 drone sightings")
  + The [German government](/wiki/Federal_Government_of_Germany "Federal Government of Germany") authorises the [Bundeswehr](/wiki/Bundeswehr "Bundeswehr") to shoot down suspicious drones seen near military sites or other critical infrastructure with [Interior Minister](/wiki/Federal_Ministry_of_the_Interior_%28Germany%29 "Federal Ministry of the Interior (Germany)") [Nancy Faeser](/wiki/Nancy_Faeser "Nancy Faeser") stating that [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia") is suspected of being behind the drone activity. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/ce3l2v01y4wo)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024–2025 Georgian protests](/wiki/2024%E2%80%932025_Georgian_protests "2024–2025 Georgian protests")
  + A [general strike](/wiki/General_strike "General strike") takes place in [Georgia](/wiki/Georgia_%28country%29 "Georgia (country)") with hundreds of Georgian firms urging [the government](/wiki/Government_of_Georgia_%28country%29 "Government of Georgia (country)") to release all [political prisoners](/wiki/Political_prisoner "Political prisoner") and hold new elections amid nationwide protests. Former [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Georgia "Prime Minister of Georgia") and opposition leader [Giorgi Gakharia](/wiki/Giorgi_Gakharia "Giorgi Gakharia") is hospitalized after being assaulted, allegedly by members of the ruling [Georgian Dream](/wiki/Georgian_Dream "Georgian Dream") party. [(Civil Georgia)](https://civil.ge/archives/652251) [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cpql9v1r57vo)
* [2024–2025 Mozambican protests](/wiki/2024%E2%80%932025_Mozambican_protests "2024–2025 Mozambican protests")
  + [Daniel Chapo](/wiki/Daniel_Chapo "Daniel Chapo") is sworn in as [President of Mozambique](/wiki/President_of_Mozambique "President of Mozambique"), succeeding [Filipe Nyusi](/wiki/Filipe_Nyusi "Filipe Nyusi"). The inauguration takes place amid ongoing political unrest in [Mozambique](/wiki/Mozambique "Mozambique"), with opposition leader [Venâncio Mondlane](/wiki/Ven%C3%A2ncio_Mondlane "Venâncio Mondlane") continuing to insist that the [October 2024 election](/wiki/2024_Mozambican_general_election "2024 Mozambican general election") was rigged. Since then, over 300 people have died in clashes with Police. [(France 24)](https://www.france24.com/en/africa/20250115-mozambique-inaugurates-president-elect-daniel-chapo-amid-deadly-unrest) [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/mozambique-president-sworn-post-election-protest-deaths-rise-2025-01-15/)
  + [Maria Benvinda Levy](/wiki/Maria_Benvinda_Levy "Maria Benvinda Levy") is appointed [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Mozambique "Prime Minister of Mozambique").[(*Club of Mozambique*)](https://clubofmozambique.com/news/mozambique-president-names-former-justice-minister-as-prime-minister-274141/)
* [Rosen Zhelyazkov](/wiki/Rosen_Zhelyazkov "Rosen Zhelyazkov") of the [GERB–SDS](/wiki/GERB%E2%80%93SDS "GERB–SDS") coalition is tasked by [Bulgarian President](/wiki/President_of_Bulgaria "President of Bulgaria") [Rumen Radev](/wiki/Rumen_Radev "Rumen Radev") with forming the new [government](/wiki/Government_of_Bulgaria "Government of Bulgaria"), following the [parliamentary election](/wiki/October_2024_Bulgarian_parliamentary_election "October 2024 Bulgarian parliamentary election") in October 2024. [(Fakti.bg)](https://fakti.bg/en/bulgaria/941822-prezidentat-vrachi-parvia-mandat-na-gerb-sds)

**Science and technology**

* [Exploration of the Moon](/wiki/Exploration_of_the_Moon "Exploration of the Moon"), [Commercial Lunar Payload Services](/wiki/Commercial_Lunar_Payload_Services "Commercial Lunar Payload Services")
  + A [SpaceX](/wiki/SpaceX "SpaceX") [Falcon 9](/wiki/Falcon_9 "Falcon 9") rocket lifts off from the [Kennedy Space Center](/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center "Kennedy Space Center") in [Florida](/wiki/Florida "Florida"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), carrying the American [Blue Ghost M1](/wiki/Blue_Ghost_M1 "Blue Ghost M1") [moon lander](/wiki/Moon_landing "Moon landing") from [Firefly Aerospace](/wiki/Firefly_Aerospace "Firefly Aerospace") and the [Japanese](/wiki/Japan "Japan") [Hakuto-R Mission 2](/wiki/Hakuto-R_Mission_2 "Hakuto-R Mission 2") moon lander from [ispace](/wiki/Ispace_Inc. "Ispace Inc."). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cn8x5gm4k1xo)

January 16, 2025 (2025-01-16) (Thursday)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip](/wiki/Israeli_bombing_of_the_Gaza_Strip "Israeli bombing of the Gaza Strip")
    - [Israeli](/wiki/Israeli_Air_Force "Israeli Air Force") [airstrikes](/wiki/Airstrike "Airstrike") kill at least 82 people across the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip"), including 30 in [Gaza City](/wiki/Gaza_City "Gaza City"), hours after the announcement of a [ceasefire agreement](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/16/israeli-attacks-kill-30-palestinians-in-gaza-after-ceasefire-deal-announced)
  + [2025 Gaza war ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire")
    - The [Israeli](/wiki/Israel "Israel") and [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") negotiating teams sign the hostage release and ceasefire deal in [Doha](/wiki/Doha "Doha"), [Qatar](/wiki/Qatar "Qatar"). [(*The Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/israel-and-hamas-sign-hostage-ceasefire-deal-after-mediators-iron-out-final-kinks/)
* [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)"), [War against the Islamic State](/wiki/War_against_the_Islamic_State "War against the Islamic State")
  + [Islamic State insurgency in Puntland](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland")
    - The [Puntland Security Force](/wiki/Puntland_Security_Force "Puntland Security Force") claims to have captured a training facility used by [ISIL](/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_Somalia_Province "Islamic State – Somalia Province") militants, with over forty ISIL fighters killed following heavy fighting. [(*The Eastleigh Voice*)](https://eastleighvoice.co.ke/somalia/105485/puntland-forces-record-major-victories-against-isis-in-somalia)
    - Thousands of families are displaced as the military campaign intensifies, forcing locals to flee their homes in [Bari region](/wiki/Bari%2C_Somalia "Bari, Somalia") of [Puntland](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland"), [Somalia](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia"). [(Idil News)](https://www.idilnews.com/puntland-urging-international-community-while-forces-crack-down-toward-isis-discover-foreign-passports-and-bank-cards/) [(*Horn Observer*)](https://hornobserver.com/articles/3126/Puntland-Appeals-for-Urgent-Aid-Amid-Military-Operations-Against-ISIS)
* [Red Sea crisis](/wiki/Red_Sea_crisis "Red Sea crisis")
  + The leader of the [Houthis](/wiki/Houthis "Houthis") [Abdul-Malik al-Houthi](/wiki/Abdul-Malik_al-Houthi "Abdul-Malik al-Houthi") announces that the group will monitor the implementation of the [Israel–Hamas ceasefire agreement](/wiki/Three-phase_Israel%E2%80%93Hamas_war_ceasefire_proposal "Three-phase Israel–Hamas war ceasefire proposal") and continue its attacks on vessels and on [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel") if the ceasefire is breached. [(*Middle East Monitor*)](https://www.middleeastmonitor.com/20250116-yemens-houthis-to-continue-attacks-if-gaza-ceasefire-breached/)
* [Sudanese civil war](/wiki/Sudanese_civil_war_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Sudanese civil war (2023–present)")
  + The [U.S. Treasury Department](/wiki/United_States_Department_of_the_Treasury "United States Department of the Treasury") sanctions the head of the [Sudanese Armed Forces](/wiki/Sudanese_Armed_Forces "Sudanese Armed Forces") [Abdel Fattah al-Burhan](/wiki/Abdel_Fattah_al-Burhan "Abdel Fattah al-Burhan") for "destabilizing [Sudan](/wiki/Sudan "Sudan") and undermining the goal of a democratic transition" to a civilian-led government. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/cn8x5nkj8pyo)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - It is reported that the [Eaton Fire](/wiki/Eaton_Fire "Eaton Fire"), which has burned over 14,000 acres and has killed 17 people, is 65% contained. [(CBS News)](https://www.cbsnews.com/losangeles/news/eaton-fire-containment-altadena-strong-winds/)
* [Stilfontein mine deaths](/wiki/Stilfontein_mine_deaths "Stilfontein mine deaths")
  + The bodies of nine [illegal miners](/wiki/Illegal_mining "Illegal mining") trapped inside a [gold mine](/wiki/Gold_mine "Gold mine") in [Stilfontein](/wiki/Stilfontein "Stilfontein"), [South Africa](/wiki/South_Africa "South Africa"), are recovered by [police](/wiki/South_African_Police_Service "South African Police Service"). [(CTV News)](https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/article/standoff-in-south-africa-ends-with-87-miners-dead-and-anger-over-polices-smoke-them-out-tactics/)
* Two [deminers](/wiki/Demining "Demining") are killed in an explosion while attempting to remove a [Cambodian Civil War](/wiki/Cambodian_Civil_War "Cambodian Civil War")-era [anti-tank mine](/wiki/Anti-tank_mine "Anti-tank mine") from a rice field in [Oddar Meanchey province](/wiki/Oddar_Meanchey_province "Oddar Meanchey province"), [Cambodia](/wiki/Cambodia "Cambodia"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/landmine-cambodia-killed-cmac-khmer-rouge-c4468881e8805a3106c56f8a2e664d34)

**International relations**

* [Ukraine–United Kingdom relations](/wiki/Ukraine%E2%80%93United_Kingdom_relations "Ukraine–United Kingdom relations")
  + [British Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom "Prime Minister of the United Kingdom") [Keir Starmer](/wiki/Keir_Starmer "Keir Starmer") [visits](/wiki/List_of_international_prime_ministerial_trips_made_by_Keir_Starmer "List of international prime ministerial trips made by Keir Starmer") [Kyiv](/wiki/Kyiv "Kyiv"), [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"), to sign a 100-year agreement with Ukraine that will formalize [British](/wiki/UK "UK") economic and military support for Ukraine. [(Sky News)](https://news.sky.com/story/sir-keir-starmer-to-sign-100-year-friendship-deal-with-ukraine-in-first-kyiv-visit-since-becoming-pm-13289508) [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/cvgem31jekvo)

**Law and crime**

* [Capital punishment in Taiwan](/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_Taiwan "Capital punishment in Taiwan")
  + [Taiwan](/wiki/Taiwan "Taiwan") carries out its first execution in five years on a man who was convicted of the 2013 murder of his former girlfriend and her mother. [(Yahoo! News)](https://uk.news.yahoo.com/taiwan-carries-first-execution-five-003203347.html)
* [Spišská Stará Ves school stabbing](/wiki/Spi%C5%A1sk%C3%A1_Star%C3%A1_Ves_school_stabbing "Spišská Stará Ves school stabbing")
  + Two women are killed and a third is injured in a [mass stabbing](/wiki/Mass_stabbing "Mass stabbing") at a school in [Spišská Stará Ves](/wiki/Spi%C5%A1sk%C3%A1_Star%C3%A1_Ves "Spišská Stará Ves"), [Slovakia](/wiki/Slovakia "Slovakia"). The perpetrator is arrested. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cx2kvz9d9rvo) [(Devdiscourse)](https://www.devdiscourse.com/article/law-order/3227238-tragic-school-stabbing-in-slovakia-two-dead)
* Two [homeless people](/wiki/Homelessness "Homelessness") are killed and two others are injured in a [mass stabbing](/wiki/Mass_stabbing "Mass stabbing") attack in [Miami](/wiki/Miami "Miami"), [Florida](/wiki/Florida "Florida"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"). A 30-year-old suspect is arrested. [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcmiami.com/news/local/police-investigate-death-in-downtown-miami-detain-suspect-armed-with-stick/3517156/)
* The [Government of Cuba](/wiki/Government_of_Cuba "Government of Cuba") releases dissident and human rights activist [José Daniel Ferrer](/wiki/Jos%C3%A9_Daniel_Ferrer "José Daniel Ferrer") from jail. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/cuba-releases-jailed-dissident-rights-activist-jose-daniel-ferrer-2025-01-16/)

**Politics and elections**

* [2021–present Bulgarian political crisis](/wiki/2021%E2%80%93present_Bulgarian_political_crisis "2021–present Bulgarian political crisis")
  + The [Parliament of Bulgaria](/wiki/Parliament_of_Bulgaria "Parliament of Bulgaria") approves a [coalition government](/wiki/Zhelyazkov_Government "Zhelyazkov Government") consisting of the [GERB-SDS](/wiki/GERB-SDS "GERB-SDS"), [BSP – United Left](/wiki/BSP_%E2%80%93_United_Left "BSP – United Left"), and [There is Such a People](/wiki/There_is_Such_a_People "There is Such a People") parties, with GERB's [Rosen Zhelyazkov](/wiki/Rosen_Zhelyazkov "Rosen Zhelyazkov") becoming [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Bulgaria "Prime Minister of Bulgaria"). [(Euronews)](https://www.euronews.com/2025/01/16/bulgarian-parliament-approves-centre-right-coalition-government)
* [2024 French political crisis](/wiki/2024_French_political_crisis "2024 French political crisis")
  + The [government](/wiki/Bayrou_government "Bayrou government") of [French Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_France "Prime Minister of France") [François Bayrou](/wiki/Fran%C3%A7ois_Bayrou "François Bayrou") survives a [no-confidence motion](/wiki/Motion_of_no_confidence "Motion of no confidence") by the opposition [New Popular Front](/wiki/New_Popular_Front "New Popular Front") electoral alliance. [(Euronews)](https://www.euronews.com/my-europe/2025/01/16/new-french-prime-minister-francois-bayrou-survives-no-confidence-vote)
* [2025 Vanuatuan general election](/wiki/2025_Vanuatuan_general_election "2025 Vanuatuan general election")
  + Citizens of [Vanuatu](/wiki/Vanuatu "Vanuatu") vote for the 52 members of [Parliament](/wiki/Parliament_of_Vanuatu "Parliament of Vanuatu"). [(RNZ)](https://www.rnz.co.nz/international/pacific-news/539119/polling-underway-in-vanuatu)

**Science and technology**

* [2025 in spaceflight](/wiki/2025_in_spaceflight "2025 in spaceflight")
  + [Blue Origin](/wiki/Blue_Origin "Blue Origin") launches its [New Glenn](/wiki/New_Glenn "New Glenn") rocket for the first time from [Cape Canaveral Space Force Station](/wiki/Cape_Canaveral_Space_Force_Station "Cape Canaveral Space Force Station") in [Florida](/wiki/Florida "Florida"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"). The rocket's [second stage](/wiki/Multistage_rocket "Multistage rocket"), carrying a prototype [Blue Ring](/wiki/Blue_Ring "Blue Ring") spacecraft, successfully reaches a [geocentric orbit](/wiki/Geocentric_orbit "Geocentric orbit"), but its [reusable](/wiki/Reusable_launch_vehicle "Reusable launch vehicle") first stage is lost during landing. [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/01/16/science/new-glenn-launch-blue-origin/index.html)
  + The twin satellites SDX01 and SDX02 of the [SpaDeX](/wiki/SpaDeX "SpaDeX") mission, launched in December by the [Indian Space Research Organisation](/wiki/Indian_Space_Research_Organisation "Indian Space Research Organisation"), successfully conduct [India](/wiki/India "India")'s first [spacecraft docking](/wiki/Docking_and_berthing_of_spacecraft "Docking and berthing of spacecraft"), with India becoming the fourth country to successfully dock a spacecraft after the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia"), and [China](/wiki/China "China"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c8j89k02py0o)
  + [SpaceX](/wiki/SpaceX "SpaceX") launches its [seventh test flight](/wiki/Starship_flight_test_7 "Starship flight test 7") of the [Starship launch vehicle](/wiki/SpaceX_Starship "SpaceX Starship"), with an improved [second stage](/wiki/SpaceX_Starship_%28spacecraft%29 "SpaceX Starship (spacecraft)"), at [Starbase](/wiki/SpaceX_Starbase "SpaceX Starbase") in [Texas](/wiki/Texas "Texas"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"). The [first stage](/wiki/SpaceX_Super_Heavy "SpaceX Super Heavy") is successfully caught by the launch tower but the second stage breaks up shortly before engine shutdown. [(CNBC)](https://www.cnbc.com/2025/01/16/spacex-launch-starship-flight-seven-starlink-satellite-test.html)
* [Nintendo](/wiki/Nintendo "Nintendo") officially reveals the [Nintendo Switch 2](/wiki/Nintendo_Switch_2 "Nintendo Switch 2") [video game console](/wiki/Video_game_console "Video game console"), the successor to the [Nintendo Switch](/wiki/Nintendo_Switch "Nintendo Switch"). [(Nintendo)](https://www.nintendo.com/us/whatsnew/nintendo-switch-2-to-be-released-in-2025/)

**Sports**

* [2025 in sumo](/wiki/2025_in_sumo "2025 in sumo")
  + Shortly after withdrawing from the January 2025 [Grand Sumo Tournament](/wiki/Honbasho "Honbasho") due to injuries, the 73rd *[yokozuna](/wiki/Yokozuna "Yokozuna")* [Terunofuji Haruo](/wiki/Terunofuji_Haruo "Terunofuji Haruo") announces his retirement. If no other wrestler is promoted this tournament, his retirement leaves [sumo](/wiki/Sumo "Sumo") without a *yokozuna* for the first time since [1993](/wiki/1993_in_sumo "1993 in sumo"). Terunofuji also announced his intention to remain in the [Japan Sumo Association](/wiki/Japan_Sumo_Association "Japan Sumo Association") as an *[oyakata](/wiki/Toshiyori "Toshiyori")*. [(*Kyodo News*)](https://english.kyodonews.net/news/2025/01/14bd63c63a6b-sumo-lone-yokozuna-terunofuji-pulls-out-of-new-year-meet.html) [(*Nikkan Sports*)](https://www.nikkansports.com/battle/sumo/news/202501160000520.html)

January 17, 2025 (2025-01-17) (Friday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_17&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_17&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_17&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + The [Security Cabinet of Israel](/wiki/Security_Cabinet_of_Israel "Security Cabinet of Israel") approves the proposed [Gaza ceasefire agreement](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire"), which is expected to take effect on Sunday. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/jan/17/israel-security-cabinet-approves-gaza-ceasefire-agreement)
* [Naxalite–Maoist insurgency](/wiki/Naxalite%E2%80%93Maoist_insurgency "Naxalite–Maoist insurgency")
  + Twelve [Naxalites](/wiki/Communist_Party_of_India_%28Maoist%29 "Communist Party of India (Maoist)") are killed in a [police](/wiki/State_Armed_Police_Forces "State Armed Police Forces") raid in [Bijapur](/wiki/Bijapur_district%2C_Chhattisgarh "Bijapur district, Chhattisgarh"), [Chhattisgarh](/wiki/Chhattisgarh "Chhattisgarh"), [India](/wiki/India "India"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/17/at-least-12-maoist-rebels-killed-by-indias-security-forces)
* [Colombian conflict](/wiki/Colombian_conflict "Colombian conflict")
  + Nine people are killed during a [shootout](/wiki/Shootout "Shootout") between [Gulf Cartel](/wiki/Gulf_Cartel "Gulf Cartel") gunmen and the [National Liberation Army](/wiki/National_Liberation_Army_%28Colombia%29 "National Liberation Army (Colombia)") (ELN) in [Montelibano](/wiki/Montelibano "Montelibano"), [Córdoba Department](/wiki/C%C3%B3rdoba_Department "Córdoba Department"), [Colombia](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia"). [(Barron's)](https://www.barrons.com/news/nine-dead-in-new-fighting-with-colombia-s-eln-rebels-official-2be8a3d0)
* Three people are killed and seven others are injured in clashes with security forces in [Juba](/wiki/Juba "Juba") and [Aweil](/wiki/Aweil%2C_South_Sudan "Aweil, South Sudan"), [South Sudan](/wiki/South_Sudan "South Sudan"), with three [Sudanese](/wiki/Sudan "Sudan")-owned houses set on fire in Aweil. This comes after videos emerged allegedly showing [Sudanese soldiers](/wiki/Sudanese_Armed_Forces "Sudanese Armed Forces") killing South Sudanese civilians in [Wad Madani](/wiki/Wad_Madani "Wad Madani"), Sudan. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c9d55x6q7d3o)

**Business and economy**

* [British](/wiki/United_Kingdom "United Kingdom") [oil and gas](/wiki/Petroleum_industry "Petroleum industry") company [BP](/wiki/BP "BP") announces that it will [lay off](/wiki/Layoff "Layoff") 4,700 employees and 3,000 contractors globally to reduce costs. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/bp-job-cuts-oil-b96729fc515a1495ca2fae320f62fefc)

**Disasters and accidents**

* A minivan rammed into a stationary bus near [Narayangaon](/wiki/Narayangaon "Narayangaon"), [India](/wiki/India "India"), killing nine. [(INDIA TODAY)](https://www.indiatoday.in/india/story/maharashtra-road-accident-on-pune-nashik-highway-dead-injured-2666217)

**Health and environment**

* The [Zimbabwean](/wiki/Zimbabwe "Zimbabwe") [Ministry of Health](/wiki/Ministry_of_Health_and_Child_Care_%28Zimbabwe%29 "Ministry of Health and Child Care (Zimbabwe)") reports that a new [cholera](/wiki/Cholera "Cholera") outbreak that started in December 2024 has reached eight [districts](/wiki/Districts_of_Zimbabwe "Districts of Zimbabwe") and infected nearly 300 people, causing one death. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/zimbabwe-cholera-outbreak-in-al-least-eight-districts/a-71333093)

**International relations**

* [2024 United States telecommunications hack](/wiki/2024_United_States_telecommunications_hack "2024 United States telecommunications hack")
  + The [U.S. Treasury Department](/wiki/U.S._Treasury_Department "U.S. Treasury Department") sanctions a cybersecurity company and hacker, both with ties to [China](/wiki/China "China")'s [Ministry of State Security](/wiki/Ministry_of_State_Security_%28China%29 "Ministry of State Security (China)"), for their alleged roles in hacking [American](/wiki/U.S. "U.S.") telecommunications companies. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/technology/cybersecurity/us-treasury-dept-issues-sanctions-related-salt-typhoon-hack-2025-01-17/)
* [Iran–Russia relations](/wiki/Iran%E2%80%93Russia_relations "Iran–Russia relations")
  + [Iranian president](/wiki/President_of_Iran "President of Iran") [Masoud Pezeshkian](/wiki/Masoud_Pezeshkian "Masoud Pezeshkian") and [Russian president](/wiki/President_of_Russia "President of Russia") [Vladimir Putin](/wiki/Vladimir_Putin "Vladimir Putin") sign the [Iranian–Russian Treaty on Comprehensive Strategic Partnership](/wiki/Iranian%E2%80%93Russian_Treaty_on_Comprehensive_Strategic_Partnership "Iranian–Russian Treaty on Comprehensive Strategic Partnership"). The 20-year deal will see cooperation between the two countries in multiple areas, including [nuclear energy](/wiki/Nuclear_program_of_Iran "Nuclear program of Iran"), [counterterrorism](/wiki/Counterterrorism "Counterterrorism"), and environmental issues. [(Middle East Eye)](https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/iran-russia-inside-strategic-partnership-treaty)

**Law and crime**

* *[TikTok v. Garland](/wiki/TikTok_v._Garland "TikTok v. Garland")*
  + The [United States Supreme Court](/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_the_United_States "Supreme Court of the United States") upholds [a law](/wiki/Protecting_Americans_from_Foreign_Adversary_Controlled_Applications_Act "Protecting Americans from Foreign Adversary Controlled Applications Act") that could ban [TikTok](/wiki/TikTok "TikTok") in the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") on January 19 unless the social media platform is sold by its [Chinese](/wiki/China "China") parent company [ByteDance](/wiki/ByteDance "ByteDance"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/supreme-court-tiktok-china-security-speech-166f7c794ee587d3385190f893e52777)
* A judge in [Bolivia](/wiki/Bolivia "Bolivia") orders the arrest of former [Bolivian President](/wiki/Bolivian_President "Bolivian President") [Evo Morales](/wiki/Evo_Morales "Evo Morales") on [statutory rape](/wiki/Statutory_rape "Statutory rape") charges. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/jan/17/evo-morales-arrest-sex-abuse)
* [Brazilian police](/wiki/Federal_Police_of_Brazil "Federal Police of Brazil") raid a ranch in [Ponta Grossa](/wiki/Ponta_Grossa "Ponta Grossa"), [South Region, Brazil](/wiki/South_Region%2C_Brazil "South Region, Brazil"), in an operation to dismantle a gang planning large-scale [bank heists](/wiki/Bank_robbery "Bank robbery"), killing six suspects and seizing weapons, including a [.50-caliber machine gun](/wiki/M2_Browning "M2 Browning") and explosives. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/brazil-parana-bank-robbery-gangs-police-53d75f51e0bc35b3036f91a10a8ab97a)

**Politics and elections**

* [Colombian conflict](/wiki/Colombian_conflict "Colombian conflict")
  + [Colombian President](/wiki/Colombian_President "Colombian President") [Gustavo Petro](/wiki/Gustavo_Petro "Gustavo Petro") suspends dialogue with the [National Liberation Army](/wiki/National_Liberation_Army_%28Colombia%29 "National Liberation Army (Colombia)") following accusations of [war crimes](/wiki/War_crimes "War crimes") against the group. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/colombias-president-suspends-peace-talks-with-eln-rebels-2025-01-17/)
* [Second inauguration of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_inauguration_of_Donald_Trump "Second inauguration of Donald Trump")
  + [U.S. President-elect](/wiki/President-elect_of_the_United_States "President-elect of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") announces that his upcoming second inauguration will be held indoors at the [United States Capitol](/wiki/United_States_Capitol "United States Capitol") [rotunda](/wiki/United_States_Capitol_rotunda "United States Capitol rotunda") due to cold temperatures forecasts. Trump also announces that the [inaugural parade](/wiki/Inaugural_parade "Inaugural parade") will be held indoors at [Capital One Arena](/wiki/Capital_One_Arena "Capital One Arena") in [Washington D.C.](/wiki/Washington_D.C. "Washington D.C.") [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/trump-inauguration-be-moved-indoors-due-cold-temperatures-cnn-reports-2025-01-17/)
* [Didier Guillaume](/wiki/Didier_Guillaume "Didier Guillaume"), the [head of government of Monaco](/wiki/Minister_of_State_%28Monaco%29 "Minister of State (Monaco)"), dies suddenly at the age of 65. [Isabelle Berro-Lefèvre](/wiki/Isabelle_Berro-Lef%C3%A8vre "Isabelle Berro-Lefèvre") is appointed acting Minister of State by [Prince](/wiki/Monarchy_of_Monaco "Monarchy of Monaco") [Albert II](/wiki/Albert_II%2C_Prince_of_Monaco "Albert II, Prince of Monaco"). [(Monaco Tribune)](https://www.monaco-tribune.com/en/2025/01/monacos-minister-of-state-didier-guillaume-dies-aged-65/)

**Science and technology**

* [Censorship of TikTok](/wiki/Censorship_of_TikTok "Censorship of TikTok")
  + [TikTok](/wiki/TikTok "TikTok") warns that it could "go dark" on Sunday without assistance from outgoing [U.S. President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Joe Biden](/wiki/Joe_Biden "Joe Biden") and [his administration](/wiki/Presidency_of_Joe_Biden "Presidency of Joe Biden"). [(Politico)](https://www.politico.com/news/2025/01/17/tiktok-pressures-biden-last-minute-00199145)

January 18, 2025 (2025-01-18) (Saturday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_18&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_18&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_18&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Kryvyi Rih strikes](/wiki/Kryvyi_Rih_strikes_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "Kryvyi Rih strikes (2022–present)")
    - Four people are killed and 14 others are injured in a [Russian](/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces "Russian Armed Forces") [ballistic missile](/wiki/Ballistic_missile "Ballistic missile") strike on [Kryvyi Rih](/wiki/Kryvyi_Rih "Kryvyi Rih"), [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"), according to the [Governor of Dnipropetrovsk Oblast](/wiki/Governor_of_Dnipropetrovsk_Oblast "Governor of Dnipropetrovsk Oblast") [Serhiy Lysak](/wiki/Serhiy_Lysak "Serhiy Lysak"). [(Euronews)](https://www.euronews.com/my-europe/2025/01/18/four-killed-in-russian-air-strike-on-kryvyi-rih-as-zelenskyy-bemoans-lack-of-air-defences)
  + [Russian strikes against Ukrainian infrastructure](/wiki/Russian_strikes_against_Ukrainian_infrastructure_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "Russian strikes against Ukrainian infrastructure (2022–present)")
    - At least four people are killed in Russian missile and [drone attacks](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") on [Kyiv](/wiki/Kyiv "Kyiv"), Ukraine. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/18/russian-attacks-on-centre-of-kyiv-leave-four-dead)
* [Israeli–Palestinian conflict](/wiki/Israeli%E2%80%93Palestinian_conflict "Israeli–Palestinian conflict")
  + [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
    - The [Government of Israel](/wiki/Government_of_Israel "Government of Israel") approves the proposed [Gaza ceasefire agreement](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire"), which had previously been approved by the [Security Cabinet of Israel](/wiki/Security_Cabinet_of_Israel "Security Cabinet of Israel"). [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/18/middleeast/israel-approves-ceasefire-hostage-deal-intl-hnk/index.html?iid=cnn_buildContentRecirc_end_recirc)
  + A [Palestinian](/wiki/Palestinian "Palestinian") man from [Tulkarm](/wiki/Tulkarm "Tulkarm") in the [West Bank](/wiki/West_Bank "West Bank") stabs and seriously injures a man in central [Tel Aviv](/wiki/Tel_Aviv "Tel Aviv") after illegally entering [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel"). An armed civilian subsequently shoots and kills the perpetrator. [(*The Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/man-seriously-hurt-in-tel-aviv-stabbing-palestinian-terrorist-shot-dead/)
* [2025 assassination of Iranian Supreme Court judges](/wiki/2025_assassination_of_Iranian_Supreme_Court_judges "2025 assassination of Iranian Supreme Court judges")
  + Two judges are killed and a third judge and a bodyguard are injured in a mass shooting at the [Supreme Court of Iran](/wiki/Supreme_Court_of_Iran "Supreme Court of Iran") in [Tehran](/wiki/Tehran "Tehran"), [Iran](/wiki/Iran "Iran"). The perpetrator subsequently [kills himself](/wiki/Murder%E2%80%93suicide "Murder–suicide"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/iran-two-judges-shot-dead-outside-supreme-court-in-tehran/a-71335185)
* [Ghanian soldiers](/wiki/Ghana_Army "Ghana Army") open fire on [illegal miners](/wiki/Illegal_mining "Illegal mining") at a [gold mine](/wiki/Gold_mining "Gold mining") in [Ashanti Region](/wiki/Ashanti_Region "Ashanti Region"), killing seven people. [Ghanian president](/wiki/President_of_Ghana "President of Ghana") [John Mahama](/wiki/John_Mahama "John Mahama") calls for an investigation into the incident. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/ghana-illegal-gold-mining-soldiers-anglogold-ashanti-abd602d2574d19281550244dc8a622cd)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 Suleja fuel tanker explosion](/wiki/2025_Suleja_fuel_tanker_explosion "2025 Suleja fuel tanker explosion")
  + At least 86 people are killed and several others are injured when a [fuel tanker](/wiki/Tank_truck "Tank truck") overturns on a highway in [Suleja](/wiki/Suleja "Suleja"), [Niger State](/wiki/Niger_%28state%29 "Niger (state)"), [Nigeria](/wiki/Nigeria "Nigeria"), and later explodes when people gather to collect the spilled fuel. [(Vanguard)](https://www.vanguardngr.com/2025/01/death-toll-in-niger-petrol-tanker-explosion-now-70/) [(The Straits Times)](https://www.straitstimes.com/world/fuel-tanker-truck-blast-kills-at-least-60-in-nigeria)
* Ten people are injured, including two seriously, when a [chairlift](/wiki/Chairlift "Chairlift") collapses at the [Astún](/wiki/Ast%C3%BAn "Astún") [ski resort](/wiki/Ski_resort "Ski resort") in [Aragon](/wiki/Aragon "Aragon"), [Spain](/wiki/Spain "Spain"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/ckgydwvkv1do)

**Health and environment**

* [2023–2024 mpox epidemic](/wiki/2023%E2%80%932024_mpox_epidemic "2023–2024 mpox epidemic")
  + [Azerbaijan](/wiki/Azerbaijan "Azerbaijan")'s [Ministry of Healthcare](/wiki/Ministry_of_Healthcare_%28Azerbaijan%29 "Ministry of Healthcare (Azerbaijan)") reports the country's first case of [mpox](/wiki/Mpox "Mpox") in a 22-year-old patient who had recently travelled abroad. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/business/healthcare-pharmaceuticals/first-mpox-case-detected-azerbaijan-interfax-reports-2025-01-18/)

**Law and crime**

* [Internet censorship in the United States](/wiki/Internet_censorship_in_the_United_States "Internet censorship in the United States")
  + [Apple](/wiki/Apple_Inc. "Apple Inc.") and [Google](/wiki/Google "Google") remove apps by the [Chinese](/wiki/China "China") company [ByteDance](/wiki/ByteDance "ByteDance"), including [TikTok](/wiki/TikTok "TikTok"), [Lemon8](/wiki/Lemon8 "Lemon8"), and [CapCut](/wiki/CapCut "CapCut"), from their app stores in the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") to comply with the [Protecting Americans from Foreign Adversary Controlled Applications Act](/wiki/Protecting_Americans_from_Foreign_Adversary_Controlled_Applications_Act "Protecting Americans from Foreign Adversary Controlled Applications Act"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/technology/tiktok-faces-us-ban-deadline-users-brace-fallout-2025-01-18/) [(CNBC)](https://www.cnbc.com/2025/01/18/apple-google-remove-tiktok-from-stores-as-app-halts-service-in-us.html)

**Politics and elections**

* [Gaza war protests](/wiki/Gaza_war_protests "Gaza war protests")
  + [Gaza war protests in the United Kingdom](/wiki/Gaza_war_protests_in_the_United_Kingdom "Gaza war protests in the United Kingdom")
    - More than 70 people are arrested at a [pro-Palestine](/wiki/Palestinian_nationalism "Palestinian nationalism") protest in [London](/wiki/London "London"), [England](/wiki/England "England"), [United Kingdom](/wiki/United_Kingdom "United Kingdom") for violating protest regulations. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cz0l34kpv51o)
* [Protests against Donald Trump](/wiki/Protests_against_Donald_Trump "Protests against Donald Trump")
  + In [Washington, D.C.](/wiki/Washington%2C_D.C. "Washington, D.C."), the [Women's March](/wiki/2017_Women%27s_March "2017 Women's March") holds a [protest](/wiki/Protests_against_the_second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Protests against the second presidency of Donald Trump") rebranded as the [People's March](/wiki/People%27s_March "People's March") against [U.S. President-elect](/wiki/President-elect_of_the_United_States "President-elect of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") ahead of his [inauguration](/wiki/Second_inauguration_of_Donald_Trump "Second inauguration of Donald Trump") on Monday. Women's March protests are also held in several cities in the [United Kingdom](/wiki/United_Kingdom "United Kingdom"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/thousands-gather-washington-protest-trump-inauguration-2025-01-18/) [(WRC-TV)](https://www.nbcwashington.com/news/local/live-coverage-crowds-expected-for-the-peoples-march-in-dc-saturday/3817450/) [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cq8kyv7yxlgo)

January 19, 2025 (2025-01-19) (Sunday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_19&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_19&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_19&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Colombian conflict](/wiki/Colombian_conflict "Colombian conflict")
  + [Catatumbo campaign](/wiki/Catatumbo_campaign "Catatumbo campaign")
    - [2025 Catatumbo attacks](/wiki/2025_Catatumbo_attacks "2025 Catatumbo attacks")
      * The [National Liberation Army](/wiki/National_Liberation_Army_%28Colombia%29 "National Liberation Army (Colombia)") (ELN) and [FARC dissidents](/wiki/FARC_dissidents "FARC dissidents") exchange heavy fire across the [Catatumbo region](/wiki/Catatumbo_region "Catatumbo region"), [Colombia](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia"), killing at least 80 people and injuring hundreds of others, with an unknown number of people also reportedly being kidnapped, after the ELN accused the FARC dissidents of killing civilians in the area. Thousands of people have fled their homes due to the fighting. The [Colombian Army](/wiki/National_Army_of_Colombia "National Army of Colombia") says that it has rescued dozens of people, while [the government](/wiki/Government_of_Colombia "Government of Colombia") calls on the ELN to cease their attacks immediately. [(CBS News)](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/kidnapped-colombia-peace-talks-fail-rebel-national-liberation-army/)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Gaza war hostage crisis](/wiki/Gaza_war_hostage_crisis "Gaza war hostage crisis")
    - The [Gaza ceasefire agreement](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire") formally goes into effect, with the first hostages and prisoners freed as part of the deal. [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/world/live-news/israel-hamas-ceasefire-war-palestine-01-19-25/index.html)
  + [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel") announces that [its troops](/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces "Israel Defense Forces") have recovered the body of [staff sergeant](/wiki/Staff_sergeant "Staff sergeant") [Oron Shaul](/wiki/Deaths_and_ransoming_of_Oron_Shaul_and_Hadar_Goldin#Oron_Shaul "Deaths and ransoming of Oron Shaul and Hadar Goldin"), who was captured and killed by [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") in 2014. [(*The Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/body-of-oron-shaul-killed-and-captured-by-hamas-in-2014-recovered-from-gaza/)

**Disasters and accidents**

* The *[Washington Post](/wiki/Washington_Post "Washington Post")* reports that there is an "emerging consensus" among U.S. and European intelligence officials that maritime accidents, rather than Russian sabotage, was the cause of damage to Baltic seabed energy and communications lines. [(Washington Post)](https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2025/01/19/russia-baltic-undersea-cables-accidents-sabotage/)
* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - [Cal Fire](/wiki/California_Department_of_Forestry_and_Fire_Protection "California Department of Forestry and Fire Protection") reports that the [Palisades Fire](/wiki/Palisades_Fire "Palisades Fire") is more than 50% contained, while the [Eaton Fire](/wiki/Eaton_Fire "Eaton Fire") is more than 80% contained. [(*Forbes*)](https://www.forbes.com/sites/antoniopequenoiv/2025/01/19/california-wildfire-updates-palisades-fire-finally-over-50-contained/)
* A bus crashed into a concrete centre barrier in [Eastern Cape](/wiki/Eastern_Cape "Eastern Cape"), killing five and injuring six. [(news365)](https://news365.co.za/head-on-collision-25/)

**Law and crime**

* [2024 South Korean martial law crisis](/wiki/2024_South_Korean_martial_law_crisis "2024 South Korean martial law crisis")
  + [Arrest of Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Arrest_of_Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Arrest of Yoon Suk Yeol")
    - [Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Yoon Suk Yeol") becomes the first sitting [president of South Korea](/wiki/President_of_South_Korea "President of South Korea") to be formally arrested, following his [declaration of martial law](/wiki/2024_South_Korean_martial_law_crisis "2024 South Korean martial law crisis") in December. [(Yonhap)](https://www.yna.co.kr/view/AKR20250118038600004?section=society/all)
    - Following Yoon's arrest, pro-Yoon protesters raid the [Seoul](/wiki/Seoul "Seoul") [Western District Court](/wiki/Judiciary_of_South_Korea "Judiciary of South Korea"), resulting in 41 injuries and property damage. [(Yonhap)](https://www.yna.co.kr/view/AKR20250119008151004)
* [Capital punishment in Iran](/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_Iran "Capital punishment in Iran"), [Islam and blasphemy](/wiki/Islam_and_blasphemy "Islam and blasphemy")
  + An [Iranian](/wiki/Iran "Iran") court sentences singer [Amir Tataloo](/wiki/Amir_Tataloo "Amir Tataloo") to death on appeal after Tataloo was convicted of [insulting](/wiki/Criticism_of_Muhammad "Criticism of Muhammad") the [prophet Muhammad](/wiki/Prophet_Muhammad "Prophet Muhammad"). [(Al Arabiya)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/middle-east/2025/01/19/iran-court-sentences-pop-singer-tataloo-to-death)

**Politics and elections**

* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + Three ministers of the [Government of Israel](/wiki/Government_of_Israel "Government of Israel") belonging to the [Otzma Yehudit](/wiki/Otzma_Yehudit "Otzma Yehudit") party resign in protest of the approved [Gaza ceasefire agreement](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire"). [(*The Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/otzma-yehudit-exits-coalition-over-gaza-deal-blasting-it-as-victory-for-terrorism/)

**Science and technology**

* [Restrictions on TikTok in the United States](/wiki/Restrictions_on_TikTok_in_the_United_States "Restrictions on TikTok in the United States")
  + [Social media](/wiki/Social_media "Social media") platform [TikTok](/wiki/TikTok "TikTok") temporarily suspends most of its services in the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") as the [Protecting Americans from Foreign Adversary Controlled Applications Act](/wiki/Protecting_Americans_from_Foreign_Adversary_Controlled_Applications_Act "Protecting Americans from Foreign Adversary Controlled Applications Act") goes into effect. TikTok restores these services, but its app remains unavailable in U.S. markets on the [App Store](/wiki/App_Store_%28Apple%29 "App Store (Apple)") and [Google Play](/wiki/Google_Play "Google Play"). [(*People*)](https://people.com/tiktok-working-to-restore-service-in-us-less-than-24-hours-after-ban-8777120) [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/tiktok-ban-trump-biden-china-bdc79b7ce741a81761f67ea56d410103)

January 20, 2025 (2025-01-20) (Monday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_20&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_20&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_20&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Colombian conflict](/wiki/Colombian_conflict "Colombian conflict")
  + [Catatumbo campaign](/wiki/Catatumbo_campaign "Catatumbo campaign")
    - [2025 Catatumbo attacks](/wiki/2025_Catatumbo_attacks "2025 Catatumbo attacks")
      * [Colombian president](/wiki/President_of_Colombia "President of Colombia") [Gustavo Petro](/wiki/Gustavo_Petro "Gustavo Petro") declares a [state of emergency](/wiki/State_of_emergency "State of emergency") in response to [rebel](/wiki/National_Liberation_Army_%28Colombia%29 "National Liberation Army (Colombia)") attacks in the [Catatumbo region](/wiki/Catatumbo_region "Catatumbo region"). [(MSN)](https://www.msn.com/en-gb/news/world/colombia-to-declare-state-of-emergency-as-violence-in-northern-regions-spikes/ar-AA1xy0fj)
      * The death toll from fighting in the [Catatumbo region](/wiki/Catatumbo_region "Catatumbo region"), [Colombia](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia"), increases to more than 100 as the [National Liberation Army](/wiki/National_Liberation_Army_%28Colombia%29 "National Liberation Army (Colombia)") (ELN) launches more attacks. The [Colombian government](/wiki/Government_of_Colombia "Government of Colombia") vows "war" against the ELN with [Colombian president](/wiki/President_of_Colombia "President of Colombia") [Gustavo Petro](/wiki/Gustavo_Petro "Gustavo Petro") saying that the group has "chosen the path of war, and a war they will have". [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/world/2025/jan/20/colombia-guerrilla-violence-deaths)
      * More than 11,000 people flee to the city of [Cúcuta](/wiki/C%C3%BAcuta "Cúcuta") as ELN rebels clash with the 33rd Front of the [FARC dissidents](/wiki/FARC_dissidents "FARC dissidents"). Authorities say more than 20,000 people have now been [internally displaced](/wiki/Internally_displaced_person "Internally displaced person") due to recent fighting. [(France 24)](https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20250120-colombia-troops-try-to-contain-guerrilla-violence-that-has-killed-100)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Attacks in Russia during the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Attacks_in_Russia_during_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Attacks in Russia during the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
    - [Ukrainian](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_Ukraine "Armed Forces of Ukraine") [drones attack](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") industrial facilities in [Tatarstan](/wiki/Tatarstan "Tatarstan"), [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia"), prompting the Russian [Federal Air Transport Agency](/wiki/Federal_Air_Transport_Agency "Federal Air Transport Agency") to temporarily suspend flights at [Kazan International Airport](/wiki/Kazan_International_Airport "Kazan International Airport") in [Kazan](/wiki/Kazan "Kazan") and [Begishevo Airport](/wiki/Begishevo_Airport "Begishevo Airport") in [Nizhnekamsk](/wiki/Nizhnekamsk "Nizhnekamsk"). [(ABC News)](https://abcnews.go.com/International/drones-attack-russian-military-industrial-hub-600-miles/story?id=117876447)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + An [IDF](/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces "Israel Defense Forces") reservist is killed and four others are injured, including a senior officer in critical condition, after their [MDT David](/wiki/MDT_David "MDT David") light armored vehicle hits a roadside bomb during a patrol in [Tammun](/wiki/Tammun "Tammun") in the [West Bank](/wiki/West_Bank "West Bank"). [(*Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/idf-reservist-killed-two-others-wounded-by-roadside-bomb-in-west-bank-overnight/)
  + The [Palestinian Civil Defence](/wiki/Palestinian_Civil_Defence "Palestinian Civil Defence") (PCD) states that the remains of 137 people have been recovered from [Rafah](/wiki/Rafah "Rafah") in the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip") since the start of the [ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire"). The PCD estimates that there are 10,000 bodies buried under rubble left to be recovered. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2025/1/20/live-palestinian-prisoners-freed-by-israel-after-captives-released-in-gaza?update=3454862)

**Business and economy**

* [Kingdom Holding](/wiki/Kingdom_Holding_Company "Kingdom Holding Company") announces the resumption of construction on the 1,000 metres (3,300 ft)-tall [Jeddah Tower](/wiki/Jeddah_Tower "Jeddah Tower") in [Saudi Arabia](/wiki/Saudi_Arabia "Saudi Arabia"), which is expected to be the [world's tallest building](/wiki/List_of_tallest_buildings "List of tallest buildings"). [(Al Arabiya)](https://www.alarabiya.net/aswaq/realestate/2025/01/20/-%D8%A7%D9%84%D9%85%D9%85%D9%84%D9%83%D8%A9-%D8%A7%D9%84%D9%82%D8%A7%D8%A8%D8%B6%D8%A9-%D8%AA%D8%B9%D9%84%D9%86-%D8%A7%D8%B3%D8%AA%D8%A6%D9%86%D8%A7%D9%81-%D8%A3%D8%B9%D9%85%D8%A7%D9%84-%D8%A8%D9%86%D8%A7%D8%A1-%D8%A8%D8%B1%D8%AC-%D8%AC%D8%AF%D8%A9-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%A3%D8%B7%D9%88%D9%84-%D9%81%D9%8A-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%B9%D8%A7%D9%84%D9%85)

**Law and crime**

* [January 6 United States Capitol attack](/wiki/January_6_United_States_Capitol_attack "January 6 United States Capitol attack")
  + [Pardon of January 6 United States Capitol attack defendants](/wiki/Pardon_of_January_6_United_States_Capitol_attack_defendants "Pardon of January 6 United States Capitol attack defendants")
    - [United States President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") formally [pardons](/wiki/Pardon "Pardon") around 1,500 defendants who had been criminally charged with involvement in the [January 6 United States Capitol attack](/wiki/January_6_United_States_Capitol_attack "January 6 United States Capitol attack"). Fourteen convicted individuals have their sentences [commuted](/wiki/Commutation_%28law%29 "Commutation (law)") to time served. [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/justice-department/trump-set-pardon-defendants-stormed-capitol-jan-6-2021-rcna187735)
* [2024 Kolkata rape and murder](/wiki/2024_Kolkata_rape_and_murder "2024 Kolkata rape and murder")
  + A court in [Kolkata](/wiki/Kolkata "Kolkata"), [India](/wiki/India "India"), [sentences](/wiki/Sentence_%28law%29 "Sentence (law)") a 33-year-old [police](/wiki/Kolkata_Police "Kolkata Police") volunteer to [life in prison](/wiki/Life_in_prison "Life in prison") for [raping](/wiki/Rape_in_India "Rape in India") and [murdering](/wiki/Murder_in_Indian_law "Murder in Indian law") a medical trainee in August 2024. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/india-man-jailed-for-life-in-doctor-rape-murder-case/a-71346298)
* [2024 Southport stabbing](/wiki/2024_Southport_stabbing "2024 Southport stabbing")
  + [Axel Rudakubana](/wiki/Axel_Rudakubana "Axel Rudakubana") pleads guilty to all 16 [charges](/wiki/Criminal_charge "Criminal charge"), including three charges of [murder](/wiki/Murder_in_English_law "Murder in English law") in relation to a [mass stabbing](/wiki/Mass_stabbing "Mass stabbing") in [Southport](/wiki/Southport "Southport"), [Merseyside](/wiki/Merseyside "Merseyside"), [England](/wiki/England "England"), in July 2024. Rudakubana is expected to be sentenced on Thursday. [(ITV News)](https://www.itv.com/news/granada/2025-01-20/rudakubana-changes-pleas-to-guilty-on-first-day-of-trial-for-southport-attack)
* [Capital punishment in China](/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_China "Capital punishment in China")
  + [China](/wiki/China "China") [executes](/wiki/Capital_punishment "Capital punishment") the perpetrators of the [2024 Zhuhai car attack](/wiki/2024_Zhuhai_car_attack "2024 Zhuhai car attack") and the [2024 Wuxi stabbing attack](/wiki/2024_Wuxi_stabbing_attack "2024 Wuxi stabbing attack"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/20/china-executes-two-men-for-committing-deadly-revenge-on-society-crimes)
* [China–Philippines relations](/wiki/China%E2%80%93Philippines_relations "China–Philippines relations")
  + [Philippine police](/wiki/Philippine_National_Police "Philippine National Police") arrest a [student](/wiki/Academic_institutions_of_the_armed_forces_of_China "Academic institutions of the armed forces of China") of the [People's Liberation Army](/wiki/People%27s_Liberation_Army "People's Liberation Army") for allegedly attempting to [spy](/wiki/Chinese_intelligence_activity_abroad "Chinese intelligence activity abroad") on several [military](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_the_Philippines "Armed Forces of the Philippines") facilities, including [U.S.-accessible bases](/wiki/United_States_bases_in_the_Philippines "United States bases in the Philippines") under the [Enhanced Defense Cooperation Agreement](/wiki/Enhanced_Defense_Cooperation_Agreement "Enhanced Defense Cooperation Agreement"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/philippines-arrests-chinese-national-suspicion-espionage-2025-01-20/)
* [Presidency of Joe Biden](/wiki/Presidency_of_Joe_Biden "Presidency of Joe Biden")
  + Outgoing U.S. President [Joe Biden](/wiki/Joe_Biden "Joe Biden") issues pre-emptive [pardons](/wiki/Federal_pardons_in_the_United_States "Federal pardons in the United States") for [his siblings](/wiki/Family_of_Joe_Biden "Family of Joe Biden"), former [Chief Medical Advisor](/wiki/Chief_Medical_Advisor_to_the_President "Chief Medical Advisor to the President") [Anthony Fauci](/wiki/Anthony_Fauci "Anthony Fauci"), former [Chairman of the Joint Chiefs of Staff](/wiki/Chairman_of_the_Joint_Chiefs_of_Staff "Chairman of the Joint Chiefs of Staff") [Mark Milley](/wiki/Mark_Milley "Mark Milley") and members of the [House Select Committee on the January 6 Attack](/wiki/United_States_House_Select_Committee_on_the_January_6_Attack "United States House Select Committee on the January 6 Attack") prior to [President-elect](/wiki/President-elect_of_the_United_States "President-elect of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump")'s [inauguration](/wiki/Second_inauguration_of_Donald_Trump "Second inauguration of Donald Trump"). Biden also [commutes](/wiki/Commutation_%28law%29 "Commutation (law)") the sentence of Indigenous activist and convicted murderer [Leonard Peltier](/wiki/Leonard_Peltier "Leonard Peltier"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/c8r5g5dezk4o) [(*HuffPost*)](https://www.huffpost.com/entry/joe-biden-leonard-peltier-clemency_n_67608b04e4b0d06419ec6367)
* Eight people are killed and seven others are injured in an [arson](/wiki/Arson "Arson") attack at a [nursing home](/wiki/Nursing_home "Nursing home") in [Barajevo](/wiki/Barajevo "Barajevo"), [Belgrade](/wiki/Belgrade "Belgrade"), [Serbia](/wiki/Serbia "Serbia"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/eight-die-seven-injured-serbian-retirement-home-fire-2025-01-20/)

**Politics and elections**

* [Second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump")
  + [Second inauguration of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_inauguration_of_Donald_Trump "Second inauguration of Donald Trump")
    - [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") and [JD Vance](/wiki/JD_Vance "JD Vance") are [inaugurated](/wiki/Inauguration "Inauguration") as the [47th](/wiki/List_of_presidents_of_the_United_States "List of presidents of the United States") [president](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") and [50th](/wiki/List_of_vice_presidents_of_the_United_States "List of vice presidents of the United States") [vice president of the United States](/wiki/Vice_President_of_the_United_States "Vice President of the United States") in [Washington, D.C.](/wiki/Washington%2C_D.C. "Washington, D.C."), with Trump becoming the first president since [Grover Cleveland](/wiki/Grover_Cleveland "Grover Cleveland") to serve non-consecutive terms. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/live/trump-inauguration-updates)
    - The inauguration is held indoors in the [United States Capitol](/wiki/United_States_Capitol "United States Capitol") [rotunda](/wiki/United_States_Capitol_rotunda "United States Capitol rotunda") due to extreme cold temperatures, making it the first inauguration since [1985](/wiki/Second_inauguration_of_Ronald_Reagan "Second inauguration of Ronald Reagan") to be held indoors. [(Today.com)](https://www.today.com/news/politics/donald-trump-2025-indoor-inauguration-weather-rcna188400)
    - During celebrations of the inauguration, businessman [Elon Musk](/wiki/Elon_Musk "Elon Musk") makes [two gestures](/wiki/Elon_Musk_salute_controversy "Elon Musk salute controversy") to a crowd at the [Capital One Arena](/wiki/Capital_One_Arena "Capital One Arena") that some on social media liken to [Nazi salutes](/wiki/Nazi_salute "Nazi salute"). The gestures were made as Musk thanked the crowd, stating "My heart goes out to you." Musk denied any meaning behind the gestures. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cy48v1x4dv4o) [(*The Independent*)](https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/americas/us-politics/elon-musk-salute-trump-inauguration-b2683095.html) [(AJ)](https://www.aljazeera.com/economy/2025/1/21/musk-accused-of-giving-nazi-salute-during-trump-inauguration-celebrations)
  + [Executive orders in the second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/List_of_executive_orders_in_the_second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "List of executive orders in the second presidency of Donald Trump")
    - On his first day of his second term, Trump signs his first executive orders on [gender](/wiki/LGBTQ_rights_in_the_United_States "LGBTQ rights in the United States") and [immigration](/wiki/Immigration_to_the_United_States "Immigration to the United States"), and also signs an order ending usage of the [CBP One](/wiki/CBP_One "CBP One") app. [(*Boston Globe*)](https://www.bostonglobe.com/2025/01/20/nation/donald-trump-executive-orders/)
    - Trump signs the [Putting America First In International Environmental Agreements](/wiki/Putting_America_First_In_International_Environmental_Agreements "Putting America First In International Environmental Agreements") executive order directing the [U.S. to withdraw from the Paris Agreement](/wiki/United_States_withdrawal_from_the_Paris_Agreement "United States withdrawal from the Paris Agreement"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/trump-paris-agreement-climate-change-788907bb89fe307a964be757313cdfb0)
    - Trump signs an executive order directing the [U.S. to withdraw from the World Health Organization](/wiki/United_States_withdrawal_from_the_World_Health_Organization "United States withdrawal from the World Health Organization"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/trump-signs-executive-withdrawing-world-health-organization-2025-01-21/)
    - Trump signs executive orders calling for the renaming the [Gulf of Mexico](/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico "Gulf of Mexico") to the "Gulf of America" and for [Denali](/wiki/Denali "Denali") to [return to its former name](/wiki/Denali%E2%80%93Mount_McKinley_naming_dispute "Denali–Mount McKinley naming dispute") "Mount McKinley". The rename would apply to all references from the [federal government](/wiki/Federal_government_of_the_United_States "Federal government of the United States"). [(CBS News)](https://www.cbsnews.com/news/trump-rename-gulf-of-mexico-denali/)
    - Trump declares [illegal immigration](/wiki/Illegal_immigration_to_the_United_States "Illegal immigration to the United States") a [national emergency](/wiki/List_of_national_emergencies_in_the_United_States "List of national emergencies in the United States") under the [National Emergencies Act](/wiki/National_Emergencies_Act "National Emergencies Act"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/trump-declare-national-emergency-border-trump-official-says-2025-01-20/)
    - Trump officially creates the [Department of Government Efficiency](/wiki/Department_of_Government_Efficiency "Department of Government Efficiency") (DOGE) led by [Elon Musk](/wiki/Elon_Musk "Elon Musk") aimed at cutting spending of the U.S. government. DOGE is a temporary organization under the [United States DOGE Service](/wiki/United_States_DOGE_Service "United States DOGE Service"), not a [federal executive department](/wiki/United_States_federal_executive_departments "United States federal executive departments"). Within minutes of the announcement, government employee unions, watchdog groups, and public interest organizations sued over this executive order. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/trump-use-one-his-first-executive-orders-create-doge-semafor-reports-2025-01-20/)
    - Trump signs an executive order to delay enforcement of the [law](/wiki/Protecting_Americans_from_Foreign_Adversary_Controlled_Applications_Act "Protecting Americans from Foreign Adversary Controlled Applications Act") [banning](/wiki/Restrictions_on_TikTok_in_the_United_States "Restrictions on TikTok in the United States") [TikTok](/wiki/TikTok "TikTok") in the United States for 75 days. [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/01/20/tech/tiktok-future-donald-trump-ban-sale/index.html)
    - Trump revokes Biden's removal of [Cuba](/wiki/Cuba "Cuba") from the [state sponsors of terrorism list](/wiki/State_Sponsors_of_Terrorism_%28U.S._list%29 "State Sponsors of Terrorism (U.S. list)"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/trump-revokes-biden-removal-cuba-us-state-sponsors-terrorism-list-2025-01-21/)
  + [Protests against Donald Trump](/wiki/Protests_against_Donald_Trump "Protests against Donald Trump")
    - [Anti-Trump protests](/wiki/Protests_against_the_second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Protests against the second presidency of Donald Trump") are held in cities across the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), as well as in other countries, such as [Mexico](/wiki/Mexico "Mexico"), [Panama](/wiki/Panama "Panama"), and the [United Kingdom](/wiki/United_Kingdom "United Kingdom"). [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/gallery/2025/jan/20/anti-trump-protests-photos)
  + [Second cabinet of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_cabinet_of_Donald_Trump "Second cabinet of Donald Trump")
    - The [United States Senate](/wiki/United_States_Senate "United States Senate") unanimously confirms [Marco Rubio](/wiki/Marco_Rubio "Marco Rubio") as [Secretary of State](/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_State "United States Secretary of State"), making him the first Cabinet official of Trump's second term to be confirmed by the Senate. Rubio also becomes the first [Latino American](/wiki/Hispanic_and_Latino_Americans "Hispanic and Latino Americans") to serve as Secretary of State. [(*The Hill*)](https://thehill.com/policy/international/5096622-senate-confirms-marco-rubio-secretary/)

**Sports**

* [2025 College Football Playoff National Championship](/wiki/2025_College_Football_Playoff_National_Championship "2025 College Football Playoff National Championship")
  + In [American football](/wiki/American_football "American football"), the [Ohio State Buckeyes](/wiki/Ohio_State_Buckeyes_football "Ohio State Buckeyes football") win their 9th [college football](/wiki/College_football "College football") championship, [defeating](/wiki/2024_Notre_Dame_Fighting_Irish_football_team "2024 Notre Dame Fighting Irish football team") the [Notre Dame Fighting Irish](/wiki/Notre_Dame_Fighting_Irish_football_team "Notre Dame Fighting Irish football team"). [(Fox Sports)](https://www.foxsports.com/live-blog/college-football/ohio-state-vs-notre-dame-live-updates-cfp-national-championship-highlights)

January 21, 2025 (2025-01-21) (Tuesday)
