**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Colombian conflict](/wiki/Colombian_conflict "Colombian conflict")
  + [Catatumbo campaign](/wiki/Catatumbo_campaign "Catatumbo campaign")
    - [2025 Catatumbo attacks](/wiki/2025_Catatumbo_attacks "2025 Catatumbo attacks")
      * Fourteen members of the 33rd Front of [FARC dissidents](/wiki/FARC_dissidents "FARC dissidents"), including one minor, surrender to personnel from the [National Army of Colombia](/wiki/National_Army_of_Colombia "National Army of Colombia") to avoid combat with the [ELN](/wiki/National_Liberation_Army_%28Colombia%29 "National Liberation Army (Colombia)"). [(*Blu Radio*)](https://www.bluradio.com/nacion/14-disidentes-de-las-farc-se-entregaron-en-medio-de-guerra-contra-eln-en-catatumbo-rg10)
      * The [Office of the Inspector General of Colombia](/wiki/Office_of_the_Inspector_General_of_Colombia "Office of the Inspector General of Colombia") warns that about 46,000 schoolchildren have not been able to start the [academic year](/wiki/Academic_year "Academic year") due to the ongoing conflict in the region and asserted that about 35% of the affected displaced population are individuals under the age of 18. [(*El Espectador*)](https://www.elespectador.com/judicial/alrededor-de-46000-ninos-se-quedaron-sin-ir-a-clase-en-el-catatumbo/)
* [Israeli incursions in the West Bank](/wiki/Israeli_incursions_in_the_West_Bank_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Israeli incursions in the West Bank (2023–present)")
  + [2025 Israeli raid on Jenin](/wiki/2025_Israeli_raid_on_Jenin "2025 Israeli raid on Jenin")
    - [Israeli forces](/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces "Israel Defense Forces") launch [a large-scale raid](/wiki/2025_Israeli_raid_on_Jenin "2025 Israeli raid on Jenin") in the [Jenin refugee camp](/wiki/Jenin_refugee_camp "Jenin refugee camp"), in the [Israeli-occupied](/wiki/Israeli-occupied_territories "Israeli-occupied territories") [West Bank](/wiki/West_Bank "West Bank"), killing at least ten people and injuring more than 35 others. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/21/israeli-army-launches-deadly-attack-on-jenin-refugee-camp-in-west-bank)
* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [M23 offensive](/wiki/M23_offensive_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "M23 offensive (2022–present)")
    - [M23](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") rebels seize the town of [Minova](/wiki/Minova "Minova") in [Kalehe Territory](/wiki/Kalehe_Territory "Kalehe Territory"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"), cutting off a major supply route to the strategic city of [Goma](/wiki/Goma "Goma"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/congos-m23-rebels-seize-eastern-town-minova-2025-01-21/)
* [Mexican drug war](/wiki/Mexican_drug_war "Mexican drug war")
  + Former regional prosecutor of [Cuautitlán](/wiki/Cuautitl%C3%A1n "Cuautitlán") Elohim Díaz Jiménez and coffee businessman Cristian Muñoz are shot dead inside a restaurant in [Metepec](/wiki/Metepec "Metepec"), [State of Mexico](/wiki/State_of_Mexico "State of Mexico"), by gunmen disguised as food delivery workers. [(El Universal)](https://www.eluniversal.com.mx/metropoli/exfiscal-regional-de-cuautitlan-es-asesinado-en-metepec/)
* [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war")
  + Six people are killed in [Homs Governorate](/wiki/Homs_Governorate "Homs Governorate"), [Syria](/wiki/Syria "Syria"), as [security forces](/wiki/Syrian_Armed_Forces "Syrian Armed Forces") conduct an operation against militias supporting ousted [president](/wiki/President_of_Syria "President of Syria") [Bashar al-Assad](/wiki/Bashar_al-Assad "Bashar al-Assad"). [(Al Arabiya)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/middle-east/2025/01/21/six-killed-as-syria-security-forces-launch-sweep-in-homs-province)
* Four people are injured, one seriously, in a [stabbing attack](/wiki/Mass_stabbing "Mass stabbing") in [Tel Aviv](/wiki/Tel_Aviv "Tel Aviv"), [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel"). The [Shin Bet](/wiki/Shin_Bet "Shin Bet") confirm that the attacker was a 28-year-old from [Morocco](/wiki/Morocco "Morocco"), and had [permanent residency](/wiki/Permanent_residency "Permanent residency") in the [United States](/wiki/Green_card "Green card"). [(BBC)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cp8qv8gz1m3o) [(*The Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/one-seriously-wounded-in-suspected-tel-aviv-stabbing-attack-medics/) [(Xinhua)](https://english.news.cn/20250122/ba124e01edd14f35a96912817adf637a/c.html)

**Business and economy**

* [Infrastructure policy of Donald Trump](/wiki/Infrastructure_policy_of_Donald_Trump "Infrastructure policy of Donald Trump")
  + [The Stargate Project](/wiki/Stargate_LLC "Stargate LLC")
    - [U.S. President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") unveils a [joint venture](/wiki/Joint_venture "Joint venture") between [OpenAI](/wiki/OpenAI "OpenAI"), [Oracle](/wiki/Oracle_Corporation "Oracle Corporation"), and [SoftBank](/wiki/SoftBank_Group "SoftBank Group"), called Stargate. With planned funding of up to $500 billion in the next four years, the project aims to build [data centers](/wiki/Data_center "Data center") and [computing infrastructure](/wiki/Computing_infrastructure "Computing infrastructure") across the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") to power AI development and create over 100,000 jobs. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/technology/2025/jan/22/trump-ai-investment-tech-ceos)
  + President Trump announces a pause in $300 billion of funding for [green infrastructure](/wiki/Green_infrastructure "Green infrastructure") previously allocated in the [Inflation Reduction Act](/wiki/Inflation_Reduction_Act "Inflation Reduction Act") and [Infrastructure Investment and Jobs Act](/wiki/Infrastructure_Investment_and_Jobs_Act "Infrastructure Investment and Jobs Act"). [(*Financial Times*)](https://www.ft.com/content/fcaf50dc-6779-44d2-a7fa-264df798a4c1)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - Multiple [brush fires](/wiki/Wildfire "Wildfire") spread by [hurricane-force winds](/wiki/Hurricane_force_wind_warning "Hurricane force wind warning") erupt in [San Diego County](/wiki/San_Diego_County%2C_California "San Diego County, California"), [California](/wiki/California "California"), U.S., prompting evacuation orders. [(USA Today)](https://www.usatoday.com/story/news/nation/2025/01/21/california-wildfires-san-diego-los-angeles/77844651007/)
* [2024–2025 floods in Southeast Asia and South Asia](/wiki/2024%E2%80%932025_floods_in_Southeast_Asia_and_South_Asia "2024–2025 floods in Southeast Asia and South Asia")
  + Sixteen people are killed in [floods](/wiki/Flood "Flood") and [landslides](/wiki/Landslide "Landslide") in [Central Java Province](/wiki/Central_Java_Province "Central Java Province"), [Indonesia](/wiki/Indonesia "Indonesia"). [(ABC)](https://abcnews.go.com/International/wireStory/landslides-flash-floods-indonesias-java-island-leave-16-117929532)
* [2025 Kartalkaya hotel fire](/wiki/2025_Kartalkaya_hotel_fire "2025 Kartalkaya hotel fire")
  + At least 76 people are killed and another 51 injured in a fire at the Grand Kartal hotel in [Kartalkaya](/wiki/Kartalkaya "Kartalkaya"), [Bolu Province](/wiki/Bolu_Province "Bolu Province"), [Turkey](/wiki/Turkey "Turkey"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/six-dead-31-injured-ski-resort-hotel-fire-turkey-state-broadcaster-says-2025-01-21/)
* Seventeen people are killed and 23 more injured after a collision between a bus and a truck in Ponan-Ouinlo, [Ivory Coast](/wiki/Ivory_Coast "Ivory Coast"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/ivory-coast-crash-ponan-ouinlo-f357f4bff556a9802c21834f005e5363)
* Much of [Canada](/wiki/Canada "Canada") and the contiguous [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") are impacted by a [cold wave](/wiki/Cold_wave "Cold wave"), killing one person near [Milwaukee](/wiki/Milwaukee "Milwaukee"), [Wisconsin](/wiki/Wisconsin "Wisconsin"). Historic snowfall is expected in the [US South](/wiki/Southern_United_States "Southern United States"), and historic [blizzard](/wiki/Blizzard "Blizzard") and [whiteout conditions](/wiki/Whiteout_%28weather%29 "Whiteout (weather)") are expected on the [Gulf Coast](/wiki/Gulf_Coast_of_the_United_States "Gulf Coast of the United States"). [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/01/21/weather/winter-storm-south-tuesday-hnk/index.html)
* One person is killed and another is injured in an explosion at the [Port of Barcelona](/wiki/Port_of_Barcelona "Port of Barcelona") in [Barcelona](/wiki/Barcelona "Barcelona"), [Spain](/wiki/Spain "Spain"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/blast-spains-barcelona-port-kills-one-person-emergency-services-say-2025-01-21/)
* Twenty [Ethiopian](/wiki/Ethiopians "Ethiopians") migrants are killed when their boat capsizes off [Yemen](/wiki/Yemen "Yemen") after departing from [Djibouti](/wiki/Djibouti "Djibouti"), according to the [International Organization for Migration](/wiki/International_Organization_for_Migration "International Organization for Migration"). [(Al Arabiya)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/middle-east/2025/01/21/boat-capsized-off-yemen-killing-20-ethiopian-migrants-iom-says)

**International relations**

* [Afghanistan–United States relations](/wiki/Afghanistan%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Afghanistan–United States relations")
  + Two [Americans](/wiki/Americans "Americans") held in [Afghanistan](/wiki/Afghanistan "Afghanistan") are [freed in exchange](/wiki/Prisoner_swap "Prisoner swap") for a [Taliban](/wiki/Taliban "Taliban") fighter in the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"). The deal is brokered by [Qatar](/wiki/Qatar "Qatar") and finalized during the final hours of the outgoing [Biden administration](/wiki/Biden_administration "Biden administration"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/taliban-say-2-americans-released-in-prisoner-swap/a-71357642)

**Politics and elections**

* [Pope Francis](/wiki/Pope_Francis "Pope Francis") announces that nun [Raffaella Petrini](/wiki/Raffaella_Petrini "Raffaella Petrini") will be appointed [President of the Governorate](/wiki/Pontifical_Commission_for_Vatican_City_State "Pontifical Commission for Vatican City State"), becoming the first woman head of government of Vatican City. She will assume the office on March 2025. [(*Catholic News Agency*)](https://www.catholicnewsagency.com/news/261691/italian-nun-raffaella-petrini-to-head-vatican-governorate)

**Law and crime**

* [U.S. President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") pardons [Ross Ulbricht](/wiki/Ross_Ulbricht "Ross Ulbricht"), the creator of the [Silk Road](/wiki/Silk_Road_%28marketplace%29 "Silk Road (marketplace)"). Ulbricht was serving a [life sentence](/wiki/Life_sentence "Life sentence") for charges including conspiracy to commit [money laundering](/wiki/Money_laundering "Money laundering"), [hacking](/wiki/Security_hacker "Security hacker"), and [drug trafficking](/wiki/Drug_trafficking "Drug trafficking"). [(Axios)](https://www.axios.com/2025/01/22/trump-ross-ulbricht-silk-road)

January 22, 2025 (2025-01-22) (Wednesday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_22&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_22&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_22&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Colombian conflict](/wiki/Colombian_conflict "Colombian conflict")
  + A [car bomb](/wiki/Car_bomb "Car bomb") explosion inside a house in [San Juan de Arama](/wiki/San_Juan_de_Arama "San Juan de Arama"), [Meta Department](/wiki/Meta_Department "Meta Department"), [Colombia](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia"), kills one person. Authorities confirm that the car was going to be used in an attack and the perpetrator was a member of the [Estado Mayor Central](/wiki/Revolutionary_Armed_Forces_of_Colombia "Revolutionary Armed Forces of Colombia"). [(*El Tiempo*)](https://www.eltiempo.com/colombia/otras-ciudades/alerta-en-meta-por-explosion-de-carro-bomba-que-se-activo-cuando-terrorista-lo-manipulaba-quien-esta-detras-3420193)
* [Moro conflict](/wiki/Moro_conflict "Moro conflict")
  + Militants from an offshoot branch of the [Moro Islamic Liberation Front](/wiki/Moro_Islamic_Liberation_Front "Moro Islamic Liberation Front") open fire against a [United Nations](/wiki/United_Nations "United Nations") [livelihood project](/wiki/UNDP "UNDP") in [Sumisip](/wiki/Sumisip "Sumisip"), [Basilan](/wiki/Basilan "Basilan"), [Philippines](/wiki/Philippines "Philippines"), killing two [soldiers](/wiki/Philippine_Army "Philippine Army") and wounding 12 others. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/philippines-attack-moro-rebels-peace-deal-undp-7037a64c90095cdda20cccfb3986b59c)
* [Red Sea crisis](/wiki/Red_Sea_crisis "Red Sea crisis")
  + The [Houthis](/wiki/Houthi "Houthi") report that 25 crew members of the [Japanese](/wiki/Japan "Japan")-operated [roll-on/roll-off](/wiki/Roll-on/roll-off "Roll-on/roll-off") ship *[Galaxy Leader](/wiki/Galaxy_Leader "Galaxy Leader")*, including many foreign nationals, are released to [Oman](/wiki/Oman "Oman"), with the Houthis citing support for the [2025 Israel–Hamas war ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Israel%E2%80%93Hamas_war_ceasefire "2025 Israel–Hamas war ceasefire") as the reason for release. [(BBC)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c9d5q0jn067o)

**Business and economy**

* [Constitutional crisis in Somalia](/wiki/Constitutional_crisis_in_Somalia "Constitutional crisis in Somalia"), [Transport in Somalia](/wiki/Transport_in_Somalia "Transport in Somalia")
  + The Somali Airlines Operators Association, representing at least 20 airlines, suspends all flights beginning on January 22, 2025, in protest against increased government-imposed fees after disputes with the [Ministry of Aviation](/wiki/Ministry_of_Aviation_%28Somalia%29 "Ministry of Aviation (Somalia)") and the [Somali Civil Aviation Authority](/wiki/Somali_Civil_Aviation_Authority "Somali Civil Aviation Authority"). [(Shabelle Media)](https://shabellemedia.com/somali-airlines-ground-flights-over-government-dispute/) [(Hiiraan Online)](https://www.hiiraan.com/news4/2025/Jan/199914/somali_airlines_halt_flights_nationwide_in_protest_against_fee_increases.aspx)
* The [Society of Professional Engineering Employees in Aerospace](/wiki/Society_of_Professional_Engineering_Employees_in_Aerospace "Society of Professional Engineering Employees in Aerospace") of the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") issues a report alleging that aerospace manufacturer [Boeing](/wiki/Boeing "Boeing"), long associated with the [Seattle](/wiki/Seattle "Seattle"), [Washington](/wiki/Washington_%28state%29 "Washington (state)") area, has been relocating much of its engineering work to non-[unionized](/wiki/Labor_unions_in_the_United_States "Labor unions in the United States") sites both in the US and abroad. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/business/aerospace-defense/union-investigates-claims-that-boeing-is-sending-work-non-union-locations-2025-01-23/)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - [Hughes Fire](/wiki/Hughes_Fire "Hughes Fire")
      * The [Hughes Fire](/wiki/Hughes_Fire "Hughes Fire") ignites and spreads to over 5,000 acres in less than four hours, triggering mandatory evacuation orders in settlements around [Castaic Lake](/wiki/Castaic_Lake "Castaic Lake") in [Los Angeles County](/wiki/Los_Angeles_County%2C_California "Los Angeles County, California"), [California](/wiki/California "California"), United States. [(*Los Angeles Times*)](https://www.latimes.com/california/story/2025-01-22/hughes-fire-evacuations-road-closures-shelters) [(KTLA)](https://ktla.com/news/california/wildfires/photos-hughes-fire-ignites-expands-rapidly-across-southern-california-mountainside/)
* [January 20–22, 2025 Gulf Coast blizzard](/wiki/January_20%E2%80%9322%2C_2025_Gulf_Coast_blizzard "January 20–22, 2025 Gulf Coast blizzard")
  + The death toll of a historic [winter storm](/wiki/Winter_storm "Winter storm") event on the [Gulf Coast of the United States](/wiki/Gulf_Coast_of_the_United_States "Gulf Coast of the United States") rises to nine people. 8 in (20 cm) of [snowfall](/wiki/Snowfall "Snowfall") is measured at [Louis Armstrong New Orleans International Airport](/wiki/Louis_Armstrong_New_Orleans_International_Airport "Louis Armstrong New Orleans International Airport") in [Louisiana](/wiki/Louisiana "Louisiana"). The statewide snowfall record in [Florida](/wiki/Florida "Florida") is broken as over 5.5 in (14 cm) falls in [Molino](/wiki/Molino%2C_Florida "Molino, Florida"). [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/01/21/weather/winter-storm-south-tuesday-hnk/index.html)
* At least thirteen people are killed in a railway accident in [Jalgaon](/wiki/Jalgaon "Jalgaon"), [Maharashtra](/wiki/Maharashtra "Maharashtra"), [India](/wiki/India "India"). The victims had initially fled from their train following an alleged [fire alarm](/wiki/Fire_alarm "Fire alarm") and were subsequently struck and killed by a passing train on the adjacent tracks. [(BBC)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cly9zrpvjm0o)
* A truck overturned and fell into a ravine along [National Highway 63](/wiki/National_Highway_63_%28India%29 "National Highway 63 (India)") in [Yellapur](/wiki/Yellapur "Yellapur"), killing 10 and injuring 15. [(The Indian Express)](https://indianexpress.com/article/india/eight-killed-ten-injured-when-truck-fell-into-valley-9792483/)

**International relations**

* [Red Sea crisis](/wiki/Red_Sea_crisis "Red Sea crisis"), [Yemeni civil war](/wiki/Yemeni_civil_war_%282014%E2%80%93present%29 "Yemeni civil war (2014–present)")
  + [U.S. President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") re-designates the [Yemeni](/wiki/Yemen "Yemen") [Houthi movement](/wiki/Houthi_movement "Houthi movement") as a [foreign terrorist organization](/wiki/United_States_Department_of_State_list_of_Foreign_Terrorist_Organizations "United States Department of State list of Foreign Terrorist Organizations"). [(*The Hill*)](https://thehill.com/policy/international/5101521-trump-houthis-yemen-terrorist-designation/)

**Law and crime**

* [Aftermath of the January 6 United States Capitol attack](/wiki/Aftermath_of_the_January_6_United_States_Capitol_attack "Aftermath of the January 6 United States Capitol attack")
  + [Pardon of January 6 United States Capitol attack defendants](/wiki/Pardon_of_January_6_United_States_Capitol_attack_defendants "Pardon of January 6 United States Capitol attack defendants")
    - Daniel Ball, a rioter who took part in the [riot](/wiki/January_6_United_States_Capitol_attack "January 6 United States Capitol attack") at the [United States Capitol](/wiki/United_States_Capitol "United States Capitol") in 2021, is [arrested](/wiki/Criminal_proceedings_in_the_January_6_United_States_Capitol_attack "Criminal proceedings in the January 6 United States Capitol attack") again despite being [pardoned](/wiki/Criminal_pardon "Criminal pardon") by Trump, making him the first rioter to get into additional legal trouble after the pardon. [(*The Hill*)](https://thehill.com/regulation/court-battles/5100384-daniel-ball-arrest-gun-charges-jan-6-pardon/amp/)
* [2025 Aschaffenburg stabbing](/wiki/2025_Aschaffenburg_stabbing "2025 Aschaffenburg stabbing")
  + Two people are killed, including a two-year-old boy, and three others are injured in a [mass stabbing](/wiki/Mass_stabbing "Mass stabbing") at a park in [Aschaffenburg](/wiki/Aschaffenburg "Aschaffenburg"), [Bavaria](/wiki/Bavaria "Bavaria"), [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany"). The perpetrator is arrested. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/suspect-arrested-after-two-killed-knife-attack-german-park-2025-01-22/)
* [Antioch High School shooting](/wiki/Antioch_High_School_shooting "Antioch High School shooting")
  + A student is killed and two others are wounded in a [school shooting](/wiki/School_shooting "School shooting") at [Antioch High School](/wiki/Antioch_High_School_%28Tennessee%29 "Antioch High School (Tennessee)") in [Nashville](/wiki/Nashville%2C_Tennessee "Nashville, Tennessee"), [Tennessee](/wiki/Tennessee "Tennessee"), United States. The perpetrator kills himself. [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/01/22/us/antioch-high-school-shooting-nashville/index.html)
* [Illegal immigration in the United States](/wiki/Illegal_immigration_in_the_United_States "Illegal immigration in the United States"), [Murder of Laken Riley](/wiki/Murder_of_Laken_Riley "Murder of Laken Riley")
  + The [U.S. Congress](/wiki/United_States_Congress "United States Congress") passes the [Laken Riley Act](/wiki/Laken_Riley_Act "Laken Riley Act") following a 263–156 vote in the [House of Representatives](/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives "United States House of Representatives"), making it easier for [immigration agents](/wiki/U.S._Immigration_and_Customs_Enforcement "U.S. Immigration and Customs Enforcement") to detain and deport those without legal status who are charged with a variety of crimes ranging from [theft](/wiki/Theft "Theft") to [assault](/wiki/Assault "Assault"). It will head to President Donald Trump for his signature. [(NPR)](https://www.npr.org/2025/01/22/nx-s1-5253926/congress-laken-riley-act)
* [Hunt family murders](/wiki/Hunt_family_murders "Hunt family murders")
  + Kyle Clifford, the perpetrator of the Hunt family killings in [Bushey](/wiki/Bushey "Bushey"), [England](/wiki/England "England"), in 2024, pleads guilty to three counts of [murder](/wiki/Murder "Murder"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cy8pd7dn8v6o)
* One person is killed and two others are injured in a [mass stabbing](/wiki/Mass_stabbing "Mass stabbing") at [Nagano Station](/wiki/Nagano_Station "Nagano Station") in [Nagano](/wiki/Nagano_%28city%29 "Nagano (city)"), [Japan](/wiki/Japan "Japan"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/japan-nagano-stabbing-train-station-524044f684df1c62cbf2036bee7bfdcd)

January 23, 2025 (2025-01-23) (Thursday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_23&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)

**Disasters and accidents**

* Four people are killed and five more injured in a [stampede](/wiki/Stampede "Stampede") at [Cambodian](/wiki/Cambodia "Cambodia") businessman [Sok Kong](/wiki/Sok_Kong "Sok Kong")'s home in [Phnom Penh](/wiki/Phnom_Penh "Phnom Penh") as he was giving away food and money amid [Lunar New Year](/wiki/Lunar_New_Year "Lunar New Year") celebrations. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/cambodia-crowd-crush-killed-sok-kong-facdf0652f008fa1695283aae9f49078)
* Nineteen vehicles figured in a pileup along the [Yekaterinburg](/wiki/Yekaterinburg "Yekaterinburg")-[Almaty](/wiki/Almaty "Almaty") highway near [Aksu-Ayuly](/wiki/Aksu-Ayuly "Aksu-Ayuly"), [Kazakhstan](/wiki/Kazakhstan "Kazakhstan"), [Karaganda Region](/wiki/Karaganda_Region "Karaganda Region"), injuring six. [(Kazinform)](https://en.inform.kz/news/several-injured-in-massive-19-car-pile-up-in-karaganda-region-8ed368/)

**Law and crime**

* [2024 Southport stabbing](/wiki/2024_Southport_stabbing "2024 Southport stabbing")
  + A court in [Liverpool](/wiki/Liverpool "Liverpool"), [England](/wiki/England "England"), sentences the man who was found guilty of killing three children and injuring 10 others in a [mass stabbing](/wiki/Mass_stabbing "Mass stabbing") in [Southport](/wiki/Southport "Southport"), [Merseyside](/wiki/Merseyside "Merseyside"), to [life imprisonment](/wiki/Life_imprisonment "Life imprisonment") with a minimum of 52 years in prison. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/uk-court-jails-southport-girls-murderer-to-52-years/a-71382959)
* [LGBTQ rights in Thailand](/wiki/LGBTQ_rights_in_Thailand "LGBTQ rights in Thailand")
  + [Thailand](/wiki/Thailand "Thailand") becomes the 38th country and the first in [Southeast Asia](/wiki/Southeast_Asia "Southeast Asia") to legalize [same-sex marriage](/wiki/Same-sex_marriage_in_Thailand "Same-sex marriage in Thailand"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/thailands-same-sex-marriage-law-2025-01-23/)
* The [International Criminal Court](/wiki/International_Criminal_Court "International Criminal Court") prosecutor requests [arrest warrants](/wiki/Arrest_warrant "Arrest warrant") against Afghanistan's [Taliban](/wiki/Taliban "Taliban") [supreme leader](/wiki/Supreme_Leader_of_Afghanistan "Supreme Leader of Afghanistan") [Hibatullah Akhundzada](/wiki/Hibatullah_Akhundzada "Hibatullah Akhundzada") and Taliban [chief justice](/wiki/Chief_Justice_of_Afghanistan "Chief Justice of Afghanistan") [Abdul Hakim Haqqani](/wiki/Abdul_Hakim_Haqqani "Abdul Hakim Haqqani"), accusing them of [crimes against humanity](/wiki/Crimes_against_humanity "Crimes against humanity"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/icc-prosecutor-seeks-arrest-warrants-against-taliban-leaders-2025-01-23/)
* [United States federal law enforcement](/wiki/Federal_law_enforcement_in_the_United_States "Federal law enforcement in the United States") and [ICE](/wiki/U.S._Immigration_and_Customs_Enforcement "U.S. Immigration and Customs Enforcement") agents arrest nearly 500 [undocumented migrants](/wiki/Illegal_immigration_to_the_United_States "Illegal immigration to the United States") with arrest warrants in [sanctuary cities](/wiki/Sanctuary_cities "Sanctuary cities"), including in [New Jersey](/wiki/New_Jersey "New Jersey") and [New York](/wiki/New_York_%28state%29 "New York (state)"). [(CTV News)](https://www.ctvnews.ca/world/article/ice-agents-arrest-hundreds-of-migrants-in-sanctuary-cities-including-new-york-city/)

**Politics and elections**

* [Second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump")
  + [Executive actions by Donald Trump](/wiki/List_of_executive_actions_by_Donald_Trump "List of executive actions by Donald Trump")
    - [Declassification of Records Concerning the Assassinations of President John F. Kennedy, Senator Robert F. Kennedy, and the Reverend Dr. Martin Luther King, Jr.](/wiki/Declassification_of_Records_Concerning_the_Assassinations_of_President_John_F._Kennedy%2C_Senator_Robert_F._Kennedy%2C_and_the_Reverend_Dr._Martin_Luther_King%2C_Jr. "Declassification of Records Concerning the Assassinations of President John F. Kennedy, Senator Robert F. Kennedy, and the Reverend Dr. Martin Luther King, Jr.")
      * [U.S. President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") signs an [executive order](/wiki/Executive_order "Executive order") to [declassify](/wiki/Declassify "Declassify") files related to the [assassinations of John F. Kennedy](/wiki/Assassination_of_John_F._Kennedy "Assassination of John F. Kennedy"), [Robert F. Kennedy](/wiki/Assassination_of_Robert_F._Kennedy "Assassination of Robert F. Kennedy") and [Martin Luther King Jr](/wiki/Assassination_of_Martin_Luther_King_Jr. "Assassination of Martin Luther King Jr."). [(Axios)](https://www.axios.com/2025/01/23/trump-classified-files-jfk-mlk-assassinations-executive-order)
  + [State of Washington v. Trump (2025)](/wiki/State_of_Washington_v._Trump_%282025%29 "State of Washington v. Trump (2025)")
    - [U.S. District Judge](/wiki/United_States_federal_judge "United States federal judge") for [Washington](/wiki/United_States_District_Court_for_the_Western_District_of_Washington "United States District Court for the Western District of Washington") [John C. Coughenour](/wiki/John_C._Coughenour "John C. Coughenour") temporarily blocks President Trump's [executive order](/wiki/Executive_Order_14156 "Executive Order 14156") attempting to end [birthright citizenship](/wiki/Birthright_citizenship_in_the_United_States "Birthright citizenship in the United States"), calling it "blatantly [unconstitutional](/wiki/Constitution_of_the_United_States "Constitution of the United States")". [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/us-judge-hear-states-bid-block-trump-birthright-citizenship-order-2025-01-23/) [(*The New York Times*)](https://www.nytimes.com/2025/01/23/us/politics/judge-blocks-birthright-citizenship.html)
  + The [U.S. Department of State](/wiki/United_States_Department_of_State "United States Department of State") bans [consular posts](/wiki/List_of_diplomatic_missions_of_the_United_States "List of diplomatic missions of the United States") from flying any flags other than the [U.S. flag](/wiki/Flag_of_the_United_States "Flag of the United States") as part of the [Trump administration](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump") targeting several instances during the [Biden administration](/wiki/Presidency_of_Joe_Biden "Presidency of Joe Biden") when [LGBTQ pride](/wiki/Rainbow_flag_%28LGBTQ%29 "Rainbow flag (LGBTQ)") and [Black Lives Matter flags](/wiki/Black_Lives_Matter "Black Lives Matter") were flown at embassies abroad. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2025/jan/23/trump-administration-bans-non-us-flags-from-being-flown-at-embassies)
* [2024 Irish general election](/wiki/2024_Irish_general_election "2024 Irish general election"), [Government of the 34th Dáil](/wiki/Government_of_the_34th_D%C3%A1il "Government of the 34th Dáil")
  + [Fianna Fáil](/wiki/Fianna_F%C3%A1il "Fianna Fáil") and [Fine Gael](/wiki/Fine_Gael "Fine Gael") form a [coalition government](/wiki/Coalition_government "Coalition government") with the backing of several [independent TDs](/wiki/Independent_politician_%28Ireland%29 "Independent politician (Ireland)"). Fianna Fáil leader [Micheál Martin](/wiki/Miche%C3%A1l_Martin "Micheál Martin") is elected as [Taoiseach](/wiki/Taoiseach "Taoiseach"), with Fine Gael leader [Simon Harris](/wiki/Simon_Harris "Simon Harris") as [Tánaiste](/wiki/T%C3%A1naiste "Tánaiste"). [(Politico)](https://www.politico.eu/article/dublin-detente-micheal-martin-elected-prime-minister-after-opposition-showdown/)

**Sports**

* [2025 Australian Open](/wiki/2025_Australian_Open "2025 Australian Open")
  + In [tennis](/wiki/Tennis "Tennis"), [John Peers](/wiki/John_Peers "John Peers") and [Olivia Gadecki](/wiki/Olivia_Gadecki "Olivia Gadecki"), both from [Australia](/wiki/Australia "Australia"), defeats [Kimberly Birrell](/wiki/Kimberly_Birrell "Kimberly Birrell") and [John-Patrick Smith](/wiki/John-Patrick_Smith "John-Patrick Smith") 3-6, 6-4, 10-6, in the [mixed doubles final](/wiki/2025_Australian_Open_%E2%80%93_Mixed_doubles "2025 Australian Open – Mixed doubles") to win their first [Australian Open](/wiki/Australian_Open "Australian Open") title. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/sport/2025/jan/24/local-heroes-olivia-gadecki-and-john-peers-clinch-australian-open-mixed-doubles-title)

January 24, 2025 (2025-01-24) (Friday)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Colombian conflict](/wiki/Colombian_conflict "Colombian conflict")
  + [Catatumbo campaign](/wiki/Catatumbo_campaign "Catatumbo campaign")
    - [2025 Catatumbo clashes](/wiki/2025_Catatumbo_clashes "2025 Catatumbo clashes")
      * The [Colombian](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia") [National Army](/wiki/National_Army_of_Colombia "National Army of Colombia") and [National Police](/wiki/National_Police_of_Colombia "National Police of Colombia") begin [offensive](/wiki/Offensive_%28military%29 "Offensive (military)") operations across eleven [*municipios*](/wiki/Municipio "Municipio") of the [Catatumbo region](/wiki/Catatumbo_region "Catatumbo region"). [(*El Tiempo*)](https://www.eltiempo.com/justicia/conflicto-y-narcotrafico/arrancan-las-operaciones-ofensivas-en-catatumbo-mindefensa-y-cupula-de-la-fuerza-publica-pasan-revista-3420649)
* [War against the Islamic State](/wiki/War_against_the_Islamic_State "War against the Islamic State")
  + [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)")
    - [Islamic State insurgency in Puntland](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland")
      * At least thirteen [Islamic State](/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_Somalia_Province "Islamic State – Somalia Province") militants are allegedly killed in heavy fighting as [Puntland forces](/wiki/Puntland_Dervish_Force "Puntland Dervish Force") claim they successfully took over the towns of Turmasaale and Janno-Jiifta in the [Bari region](/wiki/Bari%2C_Somalia "Bari, Somalia"), [Puntland](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland"), [Somalia](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia"). [(*The Somali Digest*)](https://thesomalidigest.com/puntland-troops-seize-strategic-mountain-village-deal-blow-to-isis/) [(Idil News)](https://www.idilnews.com/puntland-forces-seize-key-towns-from-isis-gain-strategic-advantage-in-bari-region/)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Attacks in Russia during the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Attacks_in_Russia_during_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Attacks in Russia during the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
    - A [Ukrainian](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_Ukraine "Armed Forces of Ukraine") [drone strike](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") targets an [oil refinery](/wiki/Oil_refinery "Oil refinery") in [Ryazan Oblast](/wiki/Ryazan_Oblast "Ryazan Oblast"), [Russia](/wiki/Russia "Russia"), in one of the largest [Ukrainian](/wiki/Ukrainia "Ukrainia") drone attacks inside Russia of the conflict to date. The [Russian military](/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces "Russian Armed Forces") says it shot down at least 121 drones over 13 regions overnight. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/cvg84r5g8d0o)
  + [Kyiv strikes](/wiki/Kyiv_strikes_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "Kyiv strikes (2022–present)")
    - A Russian drone strikes a ten-storey [apartment building](/wiki/Apartment_building "Apartment building") in [Fastiv](/wiki/Fastiv "Fastiv"), [Kyiv Oblast](/wiki/Kyiv_Oblast "Kyiv Oblast"), Ukraine, killing at least three people. [(Euronews)](https://www.euronews.com/2025/01/24/at-least-three-killed-in-overnight-russian-drone-attack-on-kyiv)
  + [Mobilization in Ukraine](/wiki/Mobilization_in_Ukraine "Mobilization in Ukraine")
    - [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine") finalizes military reforms aimed at recruiting 18- to 25-year-olds to the [armed forces](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_Ukraine "Armed Forces of Ukraine"), penalizing [draft dodgers](/wiki/Draft_evasion "Draft evasion"), and lowering the minimum [compulsory military service](/wiki/Conscription "Conscription") age to 25 from 27. [(*The Kyiv Independent*)](https://kyivindependent.com/ukraine-finalizes-draft-reform-to-attract-18-to-25-year-olds-media-reports/)
  + The Ukrainian [Coordination Headquarters for the Treatment of Prisoners of War](/wiki/Coordination_Headquarters_for_the_Treatment_of_Prisoners_of_War "Coordination Headquarters for the Treatment of Prisoners of War") announces that, with assistance from the [International Committee of the Red Cross](/wiki/International_Committee_of_the_Red_Cross "International Committee of the Red Cross"), the bodies of 757 Ukrainian soldiers have been returned to Ukraine. [(*The Kyiv Independent*)](https://kyivindependent.com/ukraine-repatriates-757-bodies/)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") confirms that an [Israeli](/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces "Israel Defense Forces") airstrike last summer killed [Rawhi Mushtaha](/wiki/Rawhi_Mushtaha "Rawhi Mushtaha"), who according to Israel was the "head of the [Hamas government](/wiki/Gaza_Strip_under_Hamas "Gaza Strip under Hamas") in the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip")", along with Sameh al-Siraj, who held the security portfolio in Hamas's [political bureau](/wiki/List_of_leaders_of_Hamas "List of leaders of Hamas"), and Sami Odeh, the head of Hamas's "general security mechanism". [(*Asharq Al-Awsat*)](https://aawsat.com/%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%B9%D8%A7%D9%84%D9%85-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%B9%D8%B1%D8%A8%D9%8A/%D8%A7%D9%84%D9%85%D8%B4%D8%B1%D9%82-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%B9%D8%B1%D8%A8%D9%8A/5104053-%D8%AD%D9%85%D8%A7%D8%B3-%D8%AA%D8%A8%D9%84%D8%BA-%D8%B9%D8%A7%D8%A6%D9%84%D8%A7%D8%AA-%D9%84%D9%82%D9%8A%D8%A7%D8%AF%D9%8A%D9%8A%D9%87%D8%A7-%D8%A8%D9%85%D9%82%D8%AA%D9%84%D9%87%D9%85-%D9%81%D9%85%D9%86-%D9%87%D9%85%D8%9F)

**Arts and culture**

* [97th Academy Awards](/wiki/97th_Academy_Awards "97th Academy Awards")
  + *[I'm Still Here](/wiki/I%27m_Still_Here_%282024_film%29 "I'm Still Here (2024 film)")* becomes the first [Brazilian](/wiki/Cinema_of_Brazil "Cinema of Brazil") film to be nominated for [Best Picture](/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Picture "Academy Award for Best Picture"), while [Karla Sofía Gascón](/wiki/Karla_Sof%C3%ADa_Gasc%C3%B3n "Karla Sofía Gascón") becomes the first openly transgender actress to be nominated for [Best Actress](/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Actress "Academy Award for Best Actress"). [(*The Washington Post*)](https://www.washingtonpost.com/entertainment/movies/2025/01/23/oscar-nominations-where-watch-stream/) [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/lifestyle/brazilians-jubilant-im-still-here-historic-oscar-nomination-best-picture-2025-01-23/) [(AP)](https://www.ap.org/news-highlights/spotlights/2025/emilia-perez-tops-oscar-nominations-with-13-wicked-and-the-brutalist-land-10-apiece/)

**Business and economy**

* [Canadian economic crisis](/w/index.php?title=Canadian_economic_crisis_(2022%E2%80%93present)&action=edit&redlink=1 "Canadian economic crisis (2022–present) (page does not exist)")
  + The [Canadian](/wiki/Canada "Canada") [Immigration, Refugees and Citizenship department](/wiki/Immigration%2C_Refugees_and_Citizenship_Canada "Immigration, Refugees and Citizenship Canada") announces a limit of 437,000 [study permits](/wiki/International_students_in_Canada "International students in Canada") for 2025, a 10% reduction from 2024, as part of efforts to address [pressures on housing](/wiki/Canadian_property_bubble "Canadian property bubble"), [healthcare](/wiki/Healthcare_in_Canada "Healthcare in Canada"), and other [public services](/wiki/Public_services_in_Canada "Public services in Canada") caused by the country's [rapid population growth](/wiki/Population_of_Canada "Population of Canada"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/canada-reduces-international-student-permits-second-year-2025-01-24/)
* [Saudi Arabia–United States relations](/wiki/Saudi_Arabia%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Saudi Arabia–United States relations")
  + [Saudi Arabia](/wiki/Saudi_Arabia "Saudi Arabia") announces that it will invest US$600 billion in the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") economy. [(Al Arabiya)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/saudi-arabia/2025/01/24/saudi-economy-minister-says-600-bln-package-with-us-includes-investments-procurement)
* [Spirit Airlines](/wiki/Spirit_Airlines "Spirit Airlines") announces a ban on passengers who wear "lewd" clothing or have "offensive" [tattoos](/wiki/Tattoo "Tattoo"). [(*The Hill*)](https://thehill.com/policy/transportation/5105837-spirit-airlines-rules-clothing-tattoos/)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2024–25 European windstorm season](/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_European_windstorm_season "2024–25 European windstorm season")
  + [Storm Éowyn](/wiki/Storm_%C3%89owyn "Storm Éowyn")
    - A [wind gust](/wiki/Wind_gust "Wind gust") provisionally measured at 183 km/h (114 mph) was recorded in [Connemara](/wiki/Connemara "Connemara") in [County Galway](/wiki/County_Galway "County Galway"), [Ireland](/wiki/Ireland "Ireland"), and a mean [wind speed](/wiki/Wind_speed "Wind speed") measured at 135 km/h (84 mph), would surpass Ireland's previous records. [(*The Irish Times*)](https://www.irishtimes.com/environment/2025/01/24/storm-eowyn-live-updates-status-red-warning-ireland-met-eireann-power-outages-transport/)
    - A man is killed in [County Donegal](/wiki/County_Donegal "County Donegal"), Ireland, after high winds cause a tree to fall on his car. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c78x4503neyo)
* [Environmental issues in Somalia](/wiki/Environmental_issues_in_Somalia "Environmental issues in Somalia")
  + At least 140 [dolphins](/wiki/Dolphins "Dolphins") are found stranded on the shores of [Mareero Beach](/wiki/Mareero "Mareero") near [Bosaso](/wiki/Bosaso "Bosaso"), [Puntland](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland"), [Somalia](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia"), with 60 confirmed dead and 30 returned to the sea. [(Idil News)](https://www.idilnews.com/puntland-mass-dolphin-stranding-prompts-environmental-investigation-in-bosaso-of-bari-region/) [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/more-than-100-dead-dolphins-found-somali-coast-cause-mystery-2025-01-24/) [(*Horn Observer*)](https://hornobserver.com/articles/3144/Over-100-dolphins-were-washed-ashore-in-Somalias-northeastern-region-of-Puntland)

**International relations**

* [Mexico–United States border crisis](/wiki/Mexico%E2%80%93United_States_border_crisis "Mexico–United States border crisis")
  + [Mass deportation of illegal immigrants in the second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/Mass_deportation_of_illegal_immigrants_in_the_second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Mass deportation of illegal immigrants in the second presidency of Donald Trump")
    - [Mexico](/wiki/Mexico "Mexico") denies a request from the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") to allow a [military](/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces "United States Armed Forces") aircraft [deporting](/wiki/Deportation_and_removal_from_the_United_States "Deportation and removal from the United States") [migrants](/wiki/Immigration_to_the_United_States "Immigration to the United States") from the U.S. to land in Mexico. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/mexico-refuses-us-military-flight-deporting-migrants-sources-say-2025-01-25/)
* The [U.S. State Department](/wiki/U.S._State_Department "U.S. State Department") freezes nearly all [foreign aid](/wiki/United_States_foreign_aid "United States foreign aid") except military aid to [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel") and [Egypt](/wiki/Egypt "Egypt"), as well as emergency food programs. [(Global News)](https://globalnews.ca/news/10976873/us-foreign-assistance-new-funding-frozen/)

**Law and crime**

* The [Cabinet of Hun Manet](/wiki/Cabinet_of_Hun_Manet "Cabinet of Hun Manet") approves a bill that strengthens penalties for [Cambodian genocide denial](/wiki/Cambodian_genocide_denial "Cambodian genocide denial"), proposing prison terms of one to five years and fines of US$2,500 to $125,000. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/law-genocide-denialism-politics-history-b85cd51c0657eb73b33850add280737e)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024–2025 Serbian anti-corruption protests](/wiki/2024%E2%80%932025_Serbian_anti-corruption_protests "2024–2025 Serbian anti-corruption protests")
  + Mass protests and a [general strike](/wiki/General_strike "General strike") are held across [Serbia](/wiki/Serbia "Serbia") in an escalation of months of anti-government protests. [(France24)](https://www.france24.com/en/live-news/20250124-serbians-strike-in-protest-over-fatal-roof-collapse)
* [2025 Slovak protests](/wiki/2025_Slovak_protests "2025 Slovak protests")
  + Over 60,000 people demonstrate across [Slovakia](/wiki/Slovakia "Slovakia") in protest of [Prime Minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Slovakia "Prime Minister of Slovakia") [Robert Fico](/wiki/Robert_Fico "Robert Fico")'s [anti-Ukrainian](/wiki/Anti-Ukrainian_sentiment "Anti-Ukrainian sentiment"), [pro-Russian](/wiki/Russophilia "Russophilia"), and [Eurosceptic](/wiki/Euroscepticism "Euroscepticism") policies. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/slovakia-anti-government-protests-russia-robert-fico-bfd1a3b2277d91fcf55b698b9c5dae55)
* [Second cabinet of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_cabinet_of_Donald_Trump "Second cabinet of Donald Trump")
  + [Pete Hegseth](/wiki/Pete_Hegseth "Pete Hegseth") is confirmed as [U.S. Secretary of Defense](/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_Defense "United States Secretary of Defense") in a 51–50 vote, with [Vice President](/wiki/Vice_President_of_the_United_States "Vice President of the United States") [JD Vance](/wiki/JD_Vance "JD Vance") casting the [tie-breaking](/wiki/List_of_tie-breaking_votes_cast_by_the_vice_president_of_the_United_States "List of tie-breaking votes cast by the vice president of the United States") vote. [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/politics/congress/senate-vote-confirm-pete-hegseth-defense-secretary-rcna189058)

January 25, 2025 (2025-01-25) (Saturday)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Colombian conflict](/wiki/Colombian_conflict "Colombian conflict")
  + [Catatumbo campaign](/wiki/Catatumbo_campaign "Catatumbo campaign")
    - [2025 Catatumbo clashes](/wiki/2025_Catatumbo_clashes "2025 Catatumbo clashes")
      * Eighty-four [National Liberation Army](/wiki/National_Liberation_Army_%28Colombia%29 "National Liberation Army (Colombia)") (ELN) combatants surrender to [Colombian](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia") [authorities](/wiki/Military_Forces_of_Colombia "Military Forces of Colombia") as offensive operations resume in the [Catatumbo region](/wiki/Catatumbo_region "Catatumbo region"). Colombian authorities also rescue 20 [child soldiers](/wiki/Child_soldiers "Child soldiers") from the ELN's 33rd Front. [(*El Colombiano*)](https://www.elcolombiano.com/colombia/primeros-resultados-operaciones-militares-en-el-catatumbo-GE26447188)
  + A [police officer](/wiki/National_Police_of_Colombia "National Police of Colombia") is shot dead by an ELN sniper in [Río Iró](/wiki/R%C3%ADo_Ir%C3%B3 "Río Iró"), [Chocó Department](/wiki/Choc%C3%B3_Department "Chocó Department"), Colombia. [(*El Tiempo*)](https://www.eltiempo.com/colombia/otras-ciudades/choco-muere-patrullero-de-la-policia-que-resulto-herido-durante-ataque-armado-del-eln-en-rio-iro-3420870)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [2025 Gaza war ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire"), [Gaza war hostage crisis](/wiki/Gaza_war_hostage_crisis "Gaza war hostage crisis")
    - [Israeli forces](/wiki/Israeli_Defense_Forces "Israeli Defense Forces") open fire on a crowd of [displaced](/wiki/Forced_displacement "Forced displacement") [Palestinians](/wiki/Palestinians "Palestinians") waiting at the [Netzarim Corridor](/wiki/Netzarim_Corridor "Netzarim Corridor"), killing two people and wounding seven others, including a child. [Israeli authorities](/wiki/Government_of_Israel "Government of Israel") allege that the shooting was due to the delayed release of Israeli hostage [Arbel Yahud](/wiki/2025_Israel%E2%80%93Hamas_ceasefire#By_Hamas "2025 Israel–Hamas ceasefire"). [(Anadolu Ajansi)](https://www.aa.com.tr/en/middle-east/2-killed-7-injured-by-israeli-army-fire-in-gaza-in-violation-of-ceasefire/3462678) [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/program/newsfeed/2025/1/25/israeli-forces-fire-on-crowds-near-gazas-netzarim-corridor)
    - [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") frees four [Israeli](/wiki/Israelis "Israelis") hostages, including [Naama Levy](/wiki/Kidnapping_of_Naama_Levy "Kidnapping of Naama Levy"), in exchange for 200 [Palestinian prisoners](/wiki/Palestinian_prisoners_in_Israel "Palestinian prisoners in Israel"), including 121 people serving [life sentences](/wiki/Life_sentence "Life sentence") after being convicted of carrying out deadly attacks against Israelis, as part of the ceasefire deal. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-war-news-ceasefire-hostages-01-25-2025-150674e17bd8b22f2c2c3aa4991cf061)
  + [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel") accuses Hamas of violating the deal by failing to release female civilians, including Arbel Yehud, before [female soldiers](/wiki/Women_in_the_Israel_Defense_Forces "Women in the Israel Defense Forces"). As a result, Israel blocks Palestinians from returning to [North Gaza](/wiki/North_Gaza_Governorate "North Gaza Governorate") through the Netzarim Corridor. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/israel-palestinians-hamas-war-news-ceasefire-hostages-01-26-2025-d0f9d113ceec2dababe462967ee8d398) [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c9qjy4lzqn3o)
* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [M23 offensive](/wiki/M23_offensive_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "M23 offensive (2022–present)")
    - Thirteen [peacekeepers](/wiki/Peacekeeping "Peacekeeping"), including nine from [South Africa](/wiki/South_Africa "South Africa"), three from [Malawi](/wiki/Malawi "Malawi") and one from [Uruguay](/wiki/Uruguay "Uruguay"), are killed as fighting intensifies in the [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo") between [government forces](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Armed Forces of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") and [M23](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") rebels, the latter backed by the [Rwandan military](/wiki/Rwanda_Defence_Force "Rwanda Defence Force"). [(*Le Monde*)](https://www.lemonde.fr/en/le-monde-africa/article/2025/01/25/13-peacekeepers-killed-as-fighting-rages-in-eastern-drc_6737423_124.html)
* [Sudanese civil war](/wiki/Sudanese_civil_war_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Sudanese civil war (2023–present)")
  + [Siege of El Fasher](/wiki/Siege_of_El_Fasher "Siege of El Fasher")
    - At least 70 people are killed in a [drone attack](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") on the Saudi Hospital, one of the last functioning hospitals in [El Fasher](/wiki/El_Fasher "El Fasher"), [Sudan](/wiki/Sudan "Sudan"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/sudan-war-hospital-attack-fasher-53f41de57ca442ed5dd3a8a1312f4052)

**Disasters and accidents**

* Eighteen people are killed and ten more injured in a [gasoline](/wiki/Gasoline "Gasoline") [tank truck](/wiki/Tank_truck "Tank truck") explosion along an [expressway](/wiki/Controlled-access_highway "Controlled-access highway") in [Enugu State](/wiki/Enugu_State "Enugu State"), [Nigeria](/wiki/Nigeria "Nigeria"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/nigeria-tanker-explosion-gasoline-f2b546036ef8a0b4b1360333aed972f3)

**International relations**

* [Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda tensions (2022–present)](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo%E2%80%93Rwanda_tensions_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda tensions (2022–present)")
  + The [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo") severs its [diplomatic relations](/wiki/Diplomatic_relations "Diplomatic relations") with [Rwanda](/wiki/Rwanda "Rwanda") as Rwandan-backed rebels advance on the city of [Goma](/wiki/Goma "Goma"), the capital of the DRC's [North Kivu](/wiki/North_Kivu "North Kivu") province. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/global-development/2025/jan/25/rwandan-army-ready-to-invade-drc-and-help-rebels-seize-city)

**Law and crime**

* [Islam and blasphemy](/wiki/Islam_and_blasphemy "Islam and blasphemy"), [Capital punishment in Pakistan](/wiki/Capital_punishment_in_Pakistan "Capital punishment in Pakistan")
  + A [Pakistani](/wiki/Pakistan "Pakistan") court sentences four people [to death](/wiki/Death_sentence "Death sentence") for [blasphemy](/wiki/Blasphemy "Blasphemy"), after they allegedly posted sacrilegious material on social media about [Islamic](/wiki/Islam "Islam") [religious figures](/wiki/Islamic_religious_leaders "Islamic religious leaders") and the [Quran](/wiki/Quran "Quran"). [(Al Arabiya)](https://english.alarabiya.net/News/world/2025/01/25/pakistan-court-sentences-4-people-to-death-for-blasphemy)
* [2025 Drents Museum heist](/wiki/2025_Drents_Museum_heist "2025 Drents Museum heist")
  + A heist at the [Drents Museum](/wiki/Drents_Museum "Drents Museum") in [Assen](/wiki/Assen "Assen"), [Netherlands](/wiki/Netherlands "Netherlands"), results in the loss of valuable [Dacian](/wiki/Dacians "Dacians") gold and silver artifacts, including the [Helmet of Coțofenești](/wiki/Helmet_of_Co%C8%9Bofene%C8%99ti "Helmet of Coțofenești"). [(Dutch News)](https://www.dutchnews.nl/2025/01/interpol-drafted-in-to-help-in-dacia-gold-heist-investigation/) [(*Romania Insider*)](https://www.romania-insider.com/romanian-dacian-treasure-robbery-dutch-museum-january-2025)

**Politics and elections**

* [2025 Greek presidential election](/wiki/2025_Greek_presidential_election "2025 Greek presidential election")
  + The [Hellenic Parliament](/wiki/Hellenic_Parliament "Hellenic Parliament") fails to elect the new [President of Greece](/wiki/President_of_Greece "President of Greece"). A second round is called between the candidates [Konstantinos Tasoulas](/wiki/Konstantinos_Tasoulas "Konstantinos Tasoulas") and [Louka Katseli](/wiki/Louka_Katseli "Louka Katseli"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/greek-lawmakers-fail-elect-new-president-first-round-voting-2025-01-25/)

**Sports**

* [2025 Australian Open](/wiki/2025_Australian_Open "2025 Australian Open")
  + In [tennis](/wiki/Tennis "Tennis"), [Madison Keys](/wiki/Madison_Keys "Madison Keys") wins her first [major](/wiki/Grand_Slam_%28tennis%29 "Grand Slam (tennis)") title after defeating the two-time defending champion [Aryna Sabalenka](/wiki/Aryna_Sabalenka "Aryna Sabalenka"), 6–3, 2–6, 7–5, to win the [women's singles](/wiki/2025_Australian_Open_%E2%80%93_Women%27s_singles "2025 Australian Open – Women's singles") title at the [Australian Open](/wiki/Australian_Open "Australian Open"). [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/25/sport/australian-open-womens-final-sabalenka-keys-spt-intl/index.html)
  + [Henry Patten](/wiki/Henry_Patten "Henry Patten") and [Harri Heliövaara](/wiki/Harri_Heli%C3%B6vaara "Harri Heliövaara") defeat [Simone Bolelli](/wiki/Simone_Bolelli "Simone Bolelli") and [Andrea Vavassori](/wiki/Andrea_Vavassori "Andrea Vavassori") 6–7 (16–18), 7–6 (7–5), 6–3, in the [men's doubles final](/wiki/2025_Australian_Open_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_doubles "2025 Australian Open – Men's doubles") to win their first Australian Open title and their second joint Grand Slam title. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/sport/tennis/articles/c9vmdkzd9k2o) [(AO)](https://ausopen.com/articles/news/mens-doubles-heliovaarapatten-win-dramatic-decider)
  + [Kateřina Siniaková](/wiki/Kate%C5%99ina_Siniakov%C3%A1 "Kateřina Siniaková") and [Taylor Townsend](/wiki/Taylor_Townsend "Taylor Townsend") defeats [Hsieh Su-wei](/wiki/Hsieh_Su-wei "Hsieh Su-wei") and [Jeļena Ostapenko](/wiki/Je%C4%BCena_Ostapenko "Jeļena Ostapenko") 6–2, 6–7 (4–7), 6–3, to win the [women's doubles final](/wiki/2025_Australian_Open_%E2%80%93_Women%27s_doubles "2025 Australian Open – Women's doubles") title.

January 26, 2025 (2025-01-26) (Sunday)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Israeli invasion of Lebanon](/wiki/Israeli_invasion_of_Lebanon_%282024%E2%80%93present%29 "Israeli invasion of Lebanon (2024–present)")
  + [2024 Israel–Lebanon ceasefire agreement](/wiki/2024_Israel%E2%80%93Lebanon_ceasefire_agreement "2024 Israel–Lebanon ceasefire agreement")
    - [January 2025 southern Lebanon attack](/wiki/January_2025_southern_Lebanon_attack "January 2025 southern Lebanon attack")
      * [Israeli soldiers](/wiki/Israeli_Defense_Forces "Israeli Defense Forces") open fire against the [Lebanese Army](/wiki/Lebanese_Army "Lebanese Army") and civilians in two villages in [southern](/wiki/Southern_Lebanon "Southern Lebanon") [Lebanon](/wiki/Lebanon "Lebanon"), killing 22 people and wounding at least 124 more. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/26/israel-kills-3-wounds-dozens-in-south-lebanon-in-breach-of-ceasefire-deal) [(*The Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/liveblog_entry/lebanese-health-ministry-raises-death-toll-to-22-from-israeli-fire-in-south-of-country/)
    - The [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") announces that the ceasefire between [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel") and [Lebanon](/wiki/Lebanon "Lebanon") will be extended to February 18. [(Axios)](https://www.axios.com/2025/01/26/israel-lebanon-ceasefire-extended-trump-white-house)
* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [M23 offensive](/wiki/M23_offensive_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "M23 offensive (2022–present)")
    - [Battle of Goma](/wiki/Battle_of_Goma_%282025%29 "Battle of Goma (2025)")
      * [March 23 Movement](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") rebels begin their advance into the city of [Goma](/wiki/Goma "Goma"), [North Kivu Province](/wiki/North_Kivu_Province "North Kivu Province"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/26/un-chief-calls-for-rwandan-forces-to-leave-drc-as-rebels-press-offensive)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Velyka Novosilka offensive](/wiki/Velyka_Novosilka_offensive "Velyka Novosilka offensive")
    - The [Russian Ministry of Defence](/wiki/Ministry_of_Defence_%28Russia%29 "Ministry of Defence (Russia)") claims that Russian forces have captured the village of [Velyka Novosilka](/wiki/Velyka_Novosilka "Velyka Novosilka"), [Donetsk Oblast](/wiki/Donetsk_Oblast "Donetsk Oblast"), [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"). [(*Mathrubhumi*)](https://english.mathrubhumi.com/amp/news/world/russia-captures-velyka-novosilka-ukraine-1.10287795)
* [Boko Haram insurgency](/wiki/Boko_Haram_insurgency "Boko Haram insurgency")
  + At least 27 [Nigerian soldiers](/wiki/Nigerian_Armed_Forces "Nigerian Armed Forces"), including the commanding officer of the 149th Battalion, are killed and dozens of others wounded in a [suicide bombing](/wiki/Suicide_attack "Suicide attack") carried out by an [Islamic State](/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_West_Africa_Province "Islamic State – West Africa Province") fighter in Malam-Fatori, [Borno State](/wiki/Borno_State "Borno State"), [Nigeria](/wiki/Nigeria "Nigeria"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/26/at-least-20-nigerian-soldiers-killed-in-attack-on-remote-army-base) [(AFP via *Inquirer*)](https://globalnation.inquirer.net/262431/jihadist-suicide-attack-kills-27-nigeria-sodiers-army)

**Business and economy**

* The [Syrian](/wiki/Syria "Syria") newspaper *[Enab Baladi](/wiki/Enab_Baladi "Enab Baladi")* announces it will return to Syria after a decade in exile following the beginning of the [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war"). [(*The New Arab*)](https://www.newarab.com/news/syrian-paper-announces-damascus-return-after-decade-exile)

**Disasters and accidents**

* A bus overturned in [Potosi Department](/wiki/Potosi_Department "Potosi Department"), [Bolivia](/wiki/Bolivia "Bolivia"), killing 19 and injuring nine. [(Barron's)](https://www.barrons.com/news/bus-crash-in-southern-bolivia-leaves-19-dead-police-ffc252c7)
* A bus traveling from [Vientiane](/wiki/Vientiane "Vientiane") to [Pakse](/wiki/Pakse "Pakse") [Laos](/wiki/Laos "Laos"), crashed into a tree after the driver fell asleep, killing five and injuring 13. [(The Times of Israel)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/13-israeli-tourists-injured-some-seriously-in-bus-crash-in-laos/)

**International relations**

* [Colombia–United States relations](/wiki/Colombia%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Colombia–United States relations"), [Mass deportation of immigrants in the second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/Mass_deportation_of_immigrants_in_the_second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Mass deportation of immigrants in the second presidency of Donald Trump")
  + [Colombian](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia") [President](/wiki/President_of_Colombia "President of Colombia") [Gustavo Petro](/wiki/Gustavo_Petro "Gustavo Petro") blocks two [U.S. military](/wiki/U.S._military "U.S. military") aircraft carrying deported [Colombians](/wiki/Colombians "Colombians") as part of [U.S. President](/wiki/U.S._President "U.S. President") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump")'s immigration crackdown from landing in his country. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/us-news/2025/jan/26/colombia-gustavo-petro-trump-deportation-flights)
  + In response to President Gustavo Petro's refusal, U.S. President Donald Trump enacts a 25% [tariff](/wiki/Tariff "Tariff") on all goods traded to the U.S. from Colombia, which will be raised to 50% in one week. Hours after Trump's announcement, President Petro orders the [commerce ministry](/wiki/Ministry_of_Commerce%2C_Industry_and_Tourism_%28Colombia%29 "Ministry of Commerce, Industry and Tourism (Colombia)") to raise tariffs on U.S. imports by 25%. [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/2025/01/26/politics/colombia-tariffs-trump-deportation-flights/index.html)
  + The dispute is settled with an agreement to use the [Colombian presidential plane](/wiki/Colombian_Air_Force_One "Colombian Air Force One") to fly the deportees from the U.S. to Colombia. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/colombia-immigration-deportation-flights-petro-trump-us-67870e41556c5d8791d22ec6767049fd) [(*The Hill*)](https://thehill.com/policy/international/5107740-colombia-presidential-plane-honduras-us-deportation-flights/)
* [Belarus–United States relations](/wiki/Belarus%E2%80%93United_States_relations "Belarus–United States relations")
  + [U.S. Secretary of State](/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_State "United States Secretary of State") [Marco Rubio](/wiki/Marco_Rubio "Marco Rubio") announces the release of [American citizen](/wiki/American_citizen "American citizen") Anastasia Nufer from a prison in [Belarus](/wiki/Belarus "Belarus"). [(RFE/RL)](https://www.rferl.org/a/us-citizen-belarus-prison-release-rubio/33289470.html)
* [Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda tensions](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo%E2%80%93Rwanda_tensions_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda tensions (2022–present)")
  + [United Nations](/wiki/United_Nations "United Nations") [Secretary-General](/wiki/Secretary-General_of_the_United_Nations "Secretary-General of the United Nations") [Antonio Guterres](/wiki/Antonio_Guterres "Antonio Guterres") urges [Rwanda](/wiki/Rwanda "Rwanda") to end its support for rebels in the [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo") and withdraw [Rwandan soldiers](/wiki/Rwanda_Defence_Force "Rwanda Defence Force") from Congolese territory. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/26/un-chief-calls-for-rwandan-forces-to-leave-drc-as-rebels-press-offensive)
  + [Congolese Foreign Minister](/wiki/Minister_of_Foreign_Affairs_%28Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo%29 "Minister of Foreign Affairs (Democratic Republic of the Congo)") [Thérèse Kayikwamba Wagner](/wiki/Th%C3%A9r%C3%A8se_Kayikwamba_Wagner "Thérèse Kayikwamba Wagner") calls Rwanda's military support for [M23](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") rebels a "[declaration of war](/wiki/Declaration_of_war "Declaration of war")". [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/dr-congo-updates-un-chief-urges-rwanda-to-pull-back-troops/live-71416951)

**Law and crime**

* [2024 South Korean martial law crisis](/wiki/2024_South_Korean_martial_law_crisis "2024 South Korean martial law crisis")
  + [South Korean President](/wiki/President_of_South_Korea "President of South Korea") [Yoon Suk Yeol](/wiki/Yoon_Suk_Yeol "Yoon Suk Yeol") is formally indicted on [insurrection](/wiki/Insurrection "Insurrection") charges over his declaration of [martial law](/wiki/Martial_law "Martial law") in December 2024. [(*The Washington Post*)](https://www.washingtonpost.com/world/2025/01/26/south-korea-president-yoon-indicted/)
* Two people, including the perpetrator, are killed and six others are injured in a [vehicle-ramming attack](/wiki/Vehicle-ramming_attack "Vehicle-ramming attack") in [Tampa](/wiki/Tampa%2C_Florida "Tampa, Florida"), [Florida](/wiki/Florida "Florida"), United States. [(NPR)](https://www.wusf.org/courts-law/2025-01-27/a-suspect-is-identified-in-a-vehicular-rampage-that-led-to-the-deaths-of-two-in-south-tampa)

**Politics and elections**

* [2025 Belarusian presidential election](/wiki/2025_Belarusian_presidential_election "2025 Belarusian presidential election")
  + A vote is held in [Belarus](/wiki/Belarus "Belarus") for [president](/wiki/President_of_Belarus "President of Belarus"), with President [Alexander Lukashenko](/wiki/Alexander_Lukashenko "Alexander Lukashenko") expected to extend his rule in an election that the [Belarusian opposition](/wiki/Belarusian_opposition "Belarusian opposition"), the [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), and the [European Parliament](/wiki/European_Parliament "European Parliament") have called a [sham election](/wiki/Sham_election "Sham election"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/amp/features/2025/1/25/lukashenko-ahead-of-2025-election-still-afraid-of-the-people)
  + A protest in [Warsaw](/wiki/Warsaw "Warsaw"), [Poland](/wiki/Poland "Poland"), is organized by Belarusian opposition leader [Sviatlana Tsikhanouskaya](/wiki/Sviatlana_Tsikhanouskaya "Sviatlana Tsikhanouskaya") after Lukashenko's rule was extended to a 7th term. [(Balkan Insight)](https://balkaninsight.com/2025/01/27/belarusians-in-poland-protest-farce-election/)

**Sports**

* [2025 ATP Tour](/wiki/2025_ATP_Tour "2025 ATP Tour")
  + [2025 Australian Open](/wiki/2025_Australian_Open "2025 Australian Open")
    - In [tennis](/wiki/Tennis "Tennis"), [Jannik Sinner](/wiki/Jannik_Sinner "Jannik Sinner") defeats [Alexander Zverev](/wiki/Alexander_Zverev "Alexander Zverev") 6–3, 7–6 (7–4), 6–3, in the [men's singles final](/wiki/2025_Australian_Open_%E2%80%93_Men%27s_singles "2025 Australian Open – Men's singles") to win his second [Australian Open](/wiki/Australian_Open "Australian Open") title and his third [Grand Slam](/wiki/Grand_Slam_%28tennis%29#Tournaments "Grand Slam (tennis)") overall. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/sport/2025/jan/26/australian-open-final-jannik-sinner-alexander-zverev-mens-singles-report) [(ATP News)](https://www.atptour.com/en/news/sinner-zverev-australian-open-2025-final)

  + [2025 24 Hours of Daytona](/wiki/2025_24_Hours_of_Daytona "2025 24 Hours of Daytona")
    - In [motor racing](/wiki/Motor_racing "Motor racing"), the [Porsche Penske Motorsport](/wiki/Team_Penske "Team Penske") team wins the 63rd [24 Hours of Daytona](/wiki/24_Hours_of_Daytona "24 Hours of Daytona") endurance race with drivers [Felipe Nasr](/wiki/Felipe_Nasr "Felipe Nasr"), [Nick Tandy](/wiki/Nick_Tandy "Nick Tandy"), and [Laurens Vanthoor](/wiki/Laurens_Vanthoor "Laurens Vanthoor"). [(*The Daytona Beach News-Journal*)](https://www.news-journalonline.com/story/sports/nascar/2025/01/26/daytona-rolex-24-winners-2025-imsa-race/77956414007/)
* [2024–25 NFL playoffs](/wiki/2024%E2%80%9325_NFL_playoffs "2024–25 NFL playoffs")
  + In [American football](/wiki/American_football "American football"), the [Philadelphia Eagles](/wiki/Philadelphia_Eagles "Philadelphia Eagles") and [Kansas City Chiefs](/wiki/Kansas_City_Chiefs "Kansas City Chiefs") win their respective conference championship games to reach [Super Bowl LIX](/wiki/Super_Bowl_LIX "Super Bowl LIX"), a rematch of [two years prior](/wiki/Super_Bowl_LVII "Super Bowl LVII"). [(FOX Sports)](https://www.foxsports.com/stories/nfl/super-bowl-lix-preview-chiefs-eagles-matchup)
* In [association football](/wiki/Association_football "Association football"), [Chelsea F.C. Women](/wiki/Chelsea_F.C._Women "Chelsea F.C. Women") sign [American](/wiki/Soccer_in_the_United_States "Soccer in the United States") defender [Naomi Girma](/wiki/Naomi_Girma "Naomi Girma") from [San Diego Wave](/wiki/San_Diego_Wave_FC "San Diego Wave FC") for a world-record fee of US$1.1 million (£881,540), making her [the most expensive woman player](/wiki/List_of_most_expensive_women%27s_association_football_transfers "List of most expensive women's association football transfers") and the first million-dollar transfer in [women's soccer](/wiki/Women%27s_soccer "Women's soccer"). [(CBS Sports)](https://www.cbssports.com/soccer/news/uswnt-star-naomi-girma-joins-chelsea-in-first-million-dollar-transfer-in-womens-soccer-history/)

January 27, 2025 (2025-01-27) (Monday)
