**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Colombian conflict](/wiki/Colombian_conflict "Colombian conflict")
  + [Catatumbo campaign](/wiki/Catatumbo_campaign "Catatumbo campaign")
    - [2025 Catatumbo clashes](/wiki/2025_Catatumbo_clashes "2025 Catatumbo clashes")
      * Local authorities of [Teorama](/wiki/Teorama "Teorama"), [Norte de Santander](/wiki/Norte_de_Santander_Department "Norte de Santander Department"), [Colombia](/wiki/Colombia "Colombia"), find the bodies of thirteen [FARC](/wiki/FARC_dissidents "FARC dissidents") combatants. [(*El Espectador*)](https://www.elespectador.com/judicial/urgente-catatumbo-hoy-encuentran-13-cuerpos-sin-vida-en-zona-rural-de-teorama-noticias-hoy/)
* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda tensions](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo%E2%80%93Rwanda_tensions_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda tensions (2022–present)")
  + [M23 offensive](/wiki/M23_offensive_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "M23 offensive (2022–present)")
    - [Battle of Goma](/wiki/Battle_of_Goma_%282025%29 "Battle of Goma (2025)")
      * [M23](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") rebels claim to have captured the city of [Goma](/wiki/Goma "Goma") in [North Kivu Province](/wiki/North_Kivu_Province "North Kivu Province"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"). The government says its troops still hold the [Goma International Airport](/wiki/Goma_International_Airport "Goma International Airport") and other key locations, and that [Rwandan](/wiki/Rwanda "Rwanda") army soldiers are present in Goma. [Congolese](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Armed Forces of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") and [Rwandan forces](/wiki/Rwanda_Defence_Force "Rwanda Defence Force") exchange fire along the [border](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo%E2%80%93Rwanda_border "Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda border"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/27/declaration-of-war-m23-rebels-claim-to-have-captured-key-dr-congo-city) [(BBC)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c0qwlkydxxko) [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/dr-congo-says-rwanda-army-in-goma/a-71422564)

**Business and economy**

* A global technology stocks selloff on the [Nasdaq Stock Market](/wiki/Nasdaq_Stock_Market "Nasdaq Stock Market"), prompted by the release of the [Chinese](/wiki/China "China") [DeepSeek](/wiki/DeepSeek "DeepSeek")-R1 model, leads to record losses in the [market capitalizations](/wiki/Market_capitalization "Market capitalization") of [AI](/wiki/Artificial_intelligence "Artificial intelligence") and [computer hardware](/wiki/Computer_hardware "Computer hardware") [companies](/wiki/List_of_computer_hardware_manufacturers "List of computer hardware manufacturers"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/technology/chinas-deepseek-sets-off-ai-market-rout-2025-01-27/)

**International relations**

* [China–India relations](/wiki/China%E2%80%93India_relations "China–India relations")
  + Following the meeting between [Indian Foreign Secretary](/wiki/Foreign_Secretary_%28India%29 "Foreign Secretary (India)") [Vikram Misri](/wiki/Vikram_Misri "Vikram Misri") and [Chinese Foreign Minister](/wiki/Foreign_Minister_of_China "Foreign Minister of China") [Wang Yi](/wiki/Wang_Yi_%28politician%29 "Wang Yi (politician)") in [Beijing](/wiki/Beijing "Beijing"), [China](/wiki/China "China") and [India](/wiki/India "India") agree to resume direct air travel between the two countries after a five-year hiatus. [(CNA)](https://www.channelnewsasia.com/asia/india-china-agree-resume-air-travel-after-five-years-4899321).

**Law and crime**

* [Interpol Terrorism Watch List](/wiki/Interpol_Terrorism_Watch_List "Interpol Terrorism Watch List")
  + A joint [INTERPOL](/wiki/INTERPOL "INTERPOL") and [AFRIPOL](/wiki/Afripol "Afripol") operation including eight [East African](/wiki/East_Africa "East Africa") nations leads to the arrest of 37 people and the seizure of [small](/wiki/Small_arms_and_light_weapons "Small arms and light weapons") and [heavy weapons](/wiki/Heavy_weapon "Heavy weapon") in [Kenya](/wiki/Kenya "Kenya"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"), [Somalia](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia"), and [Tanzania](/wiki/Tanzania "Tanzania"). [(INTERPOL)](https://www.interpol.int/en/News-and-Events/News/2025/37-terror-suspects-arrested-in-East-African-operation)

**Politics and elections**

* [Second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump")
  + [Executive Order 14186](/wiki/Executive_Order_14186 "Executive Order 14186"), [Executive Order 14183](/wiki/Executive_Order_14183 "Executive Order 14183")
    - President Trump signs an executive order eliminating "gender radicalism in the military", targeting [transgender personnel](/wiki/Transgender_personnel_in_the_United_States_military "Transgender personnel in the United States military") in the [military](/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces "United States Armed Forces"), and another executive order that mandates a process to develop an American [Iron Dome](/wiki/Iron_Dome "Iron Dome"). [(France 24)](https://www.france24.com/en/americas/20250128-trump-signs-executive-orders-aimed-at-trans-troops-mandates-american-iron-dome)
  + [Second cabinet of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_cabinet_of_Donald_Trump "Second cabinet of Donald Trump")
    - The [United States Senate](/wiki/United_States_Senate "United States Senate") votes to confirm [Scott Bessent](/wiki/Scott_Bessent "Scott Bessent") as [U.S. Treasury Secretary](/wiki/United_States_Secretary_of_the_Treasury "United States Secretary of the Treasury"), making him the highest rank [LGBTQ](/wiki/LGBTQ "LGBTQ") official to run the [U.S. Treasury](/wiki/United_States_Treasury "United States Treasury") and the highest-ranking LGBTQ person in the United States. [(TIME)](https://time.com/7210423/scott-bessent-confirmed-trump-treasury-secretary/)
  + [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") [Office of Management and Budget](/wiki/Office_of_Management_and_Budget "Office of Management and Budget") acting director Matthew Vaeth orders [federal government](/wiki/Federal_government_of_the_United_States "Federal government of the United States") agencies to temporarily pause all federal financial assistance programs, with the exception of [Medicare](/wiki/Medicare_%28United_States%29 "Medicare (United States)") and [Social Security](/wiki/Social_Security_%28United_States%29 "Social Security (United States)"), that could be implicated by select [executive orders](/wiki/Executive_order "Executive order") from [President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump"). [(Politico)](https://www.politico.com/news/2025/01/27/trump-freezes-federal-aid-omb-00200891)

January 28, 2025 (2025-01-28) (Tuesday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_28&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_28&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_28&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [War against the Islamic State](/wiki/War_against_the_Islamic_State "War against the Islamic State")
  + [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)")
    - [Islamic State insurgency in Puntland](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland")
      * [Puntland](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland") [authorities](/wiki/Government_of_Puntland "Government of Puntland") ban illegal foreign entries and direct [telecom firms](/wiki/Telecommunications_company "Telecommunications company") to deactivate [SIM cards](/wiki/SIM_card "SIM card") linked to undocumented individuals and [Islamic State](/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_Somalia_Province "Islamic State – Somalia Province") operatives, aiming to disrupt the group's financial networks amidst ongoing anti-IS offensives by [Puntland forces](/wiki/Puntland_Security_Force "Puntland Security Force"). [(VOA)](https://www.voanews.com/a/puntland-blocks-illegal-entry-of-foreigners-in-is-crackdown/7953395.html) [(Garowe Online)](https://www.garoweonline.com/en/news/puntland/somalia-puntland-crackdown-targets-isis-linked-foreigners) [(International Organization for Migration)](https://dtm.iom.int/reports/somalia-border-point-flow-monitoring-november-2024)
      * Puntland's highest military court sentences two [influencers](/wiki/Influencer "Influencer") to prison terms *[in absentia](/wiki/Trial_in_absentia "Trial in absentia")* for promoting Islamic State propaganda and spreading [disinformation](/wiki/Disinformation "Disinformation") intended at discrediting [Puntland forces](/wiki/Puntland_Dervish_Force "Puntland Dervish Force")' ongoing operations. [(Hiiraan Online)](https://www.hiiraan.com/news4/2025/Jan/199996/puntland_sentences_two_social_media_influencers_for_supporting_isis.aspx) [(Idil News)](https://www.idilnews.com/puntland-military-court-sentences-two-men-for-promoting-isis-propaganda/)
      * At least four civilians are killed in an airstrike by an unknown [combat drone](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") in the Sihan area of [Qandala district](/wiki/Qandala_District "Qandala District") in Puntland's [Bari region](/wiki/Bari_Region "Bari Region"). [(Garowe Online)](https://www.garoweonline.com/en/news/puntland/somalia-an-airstrike-kills-four-civilians-from-the-same-family-in-puntland) [(Hiiraan Online)](https://www.hiiraan.com/news4/2025/Jan/199995/unidentified_drone_strike_kills_four_civilians_near_isis_stronghold_in_bari_region.aspx)
* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [M23 offensive](/wiki/M23_offensive_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "M23 offensive (2022–present)")
    - [Battle of Goma](/wiki/Battle_of_Goma_%282025%29 "Battle of Goma (2025)")
      * [M23](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") rebels take full control of [Goma International Airport](/wiki/Goma_International_Airport "Goma International Airport") in [Goma](/wiki/Goma "Goma"), [North Kivu](/wiki/North_Kivu "North Kivu"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"), according to senior diplomatic and [Congolese](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo") security officials. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/congos-m23-rebels-control-goma-airport-diplomatic-security-sources-say-2025-01-28/)
      * Four more [South African](/wiki/South_Africa "South Africa") [peacekeepers](/wiki/Peacekeeping "Peacekeeping") are killed after M23 forces launch a [mortar attack](/wiki/Mortar_%28weapon%29 "Mortar (weapon)") on their position at Goma Airport, bringing the total number of foreign peacekeepers killed in recent clashes to 17. [(Anadolu Ajansi)](https://www.aa.com.tr/en/africa/death-toll-among-peacekeepers-climbs-to-17-in-eastern-democratic-republic-of-congo/3464337)
      * [Rwandan Foreign Minister](/wiki/Ministry_of_Foreign_Affairs_and_Cooperation_%28Rwanda%29 "Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Cooperation (Rwanda)") [Olivier Nduhungirehe](/wiki/Olivier_Nduhungirehe "Olivier Nduhungirehe") says [Congolese president](/wiki/President_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "President of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") [Félix Tshisekedi](/wiki/F%C3%A9lix_Tshisekedi "Félix Tshisekedi") "will have to accept talks with M23 to end the situation once and for all". [(*The Hill*)](https://thehill.com/homenews/ap/ap-international/ap-congos-forces-try-to-slow-rwanda-backed-rebels-in-the-east-as-protests-break-out-in-the-capital/)
    - [2025 Kinshasa riots](/wiki/2025_Kinshasa_riots "2025 Kinshasa riots")
      * Mass [rioting](/wiki/Riot "Riot") takes place in [Kinshasa](/wiki/Kinshasa "Kinshasa"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo"), amid public outrage over the loss of [Goma](/wiki/Goma "Goma") to [Rwandan](/wiki/Rwanda "Rwanda")-backed rebels. Multiple embassies are stormed and attacked by anti-government protesters, including the embassies of [France](/wiki/France "France"), [Rwanda](/wiki/Rwanda "Rwanda"), and [Uganda](/wiki/Uganda "Uganda"). Widespread [looting](/wiki/Looting "Looting") is also reported in the capital. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/congo-protesters-attack-kinshasa-embassies-over-conflict-east-2025-01-28/)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [Gaza humanitarian crisis](/wiki/Gaza_humanitarian_crisis_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Gaza humanitarian crisis (2023–present)")
    - [Israel](/wiki/Israel "Israel") announces it will cease all contact with the [United Nations](/wiki/United_Nations "United Nations") relief agency for [Palestinians](/wiki/Palestinians "Palestinians"), [UNRWA](/wiki/UNRWA "UNRWA"), after a ban on the organization's work on [Israeli territory](/wiki/Borders_of_Israel "Borders of Israel") goes into effect on January 30. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/israel-to-cease-all-contact-with-unrwa-aid-agency/a-71439020)
* [Insurgency in Balochistan](/wiki/Insurgency_in_Balochistan "Insurgency in Balochistan")
  + Two [Pakistan Army](/wiki/Pakistan_Army "Pakistan Army") soldiers and five insurgents are killed in a [shootout](/wiki/Shootout "Shootout") in [Killa Abdullah District](/wiki/Killa_Abdullah_District "Killa Abdullah District"), [Balochistan, Pakistan](/wiki/Balochistan%2C_Pakistan "Balochistan, Pakistan"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/pakistan-militant-attack-security-post-balochistan-878ecfcbaf2174a672049b09226814c8)
* [Israeli invasion of Syria](/wiki/Israeli_invasion_of_Syria_%282024%E2%80%93present%29 "Israeli invasion of Syria (2024–present)")
  + [Israeli Defense Minister](/wiki/Israeli_Defense_Minister "Israeli Defense Minister") [Israel Katz](/wiki/Israel_Katz "Israel Katz") announces that [Israel Defense Forces](/wiki/Israel_Defense_Forces "Israel Defense Forces") will remain on the Syrian side of [Mount Hermon](/wiki/Mount_Hermon "Mount Hermon") indefinitely, apparently backtracking on repeated assurances from Israel that the move was temporary. [(*Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/defense-minister-in-syria-buffer-zone-says-idf-to-stay-indefinitely/) [(Middle East Eye)](https://www.middleeasteye.net/news/israeli-army-stay-jenin-syria-defence-minister)

**Business and economy**

* [German economic crisis](/wiki/German_economic_crisis_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "German economic crisis (2022–present)")
  + [Verdi](/wiki/Ver.di "Ver.di"), [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany")'s second-largest [trade union](/wiki/Trade_union "Trade union"), calls for a one-day [labor strike](/wiki/Labor_strike "Labor strike") for workers at [logistics](/wiki/Logistics "Logistics") and [courier](/wiki/Courier "Courier") company [DHL](/wiki/DHL "DHL"), which also manages [Deutsche Post](/wiki/Deutsche_Post "Deutsche Post"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/germany-verdi-union-calls-dhl-strike/a-71431352)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [Air Busan Flight 391](/wiki/Air_Busan_Flight_391 "Air Busan Flight 391")
  + Seven people are injured when an [Air Busan](/wiki/Air_Busan "Air Busan") [Airbus A321-200](/wiki/Airbus_A321-200 "Airbus A321-200") aircraft catches fire before [taking off](/wiki/Takeoff "Takeoff") from [Gimhae International Airport](/wiki/Gimhae_International_Airport "Gimhae International Airport") in [Busan](/wiki/Busan "Busan"), [South Korea](/wiki/South_Korea "South Korea"). All 169 people on board are evacuated from the aircraft. [(*Korea Herald*)](https://www.koreaherald.com/article/10408402)
* A [United States Air Force](/wiki/United_States_Air_Force "United States Air Force") [F-35](/wiki/F-35 "F-35") pilot ejects during a crash at [Eielson Air Force Base](/wiki/Eielson_Air_Force_Base "Eielson Air Force Base") in [Fairbanks](/wiki/Fairbanks%2C_Alaska "Fairbanks, Alaska"), [Alaska](/wiki/Alaska "Alaska"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"). The aircraft is destroyed. [(CBS News)](https://www.cbsnews.com/amp/news/f35-fighter-jet-crash-alaska-air-force-base/)

**Law and crime**

* [2025 Drents Museum heist](/wiki/2025_Drents_Museum_heist "2025 Drents Museum heist")
  + Following the heist of multiple [Dacian](/wiki/Dacians "Dacians") artifacts last Saturday at the [Drents Museum](/wiki/Drents_Museum "Drents Museum") in [Assen](/wiki/Assen "Assen"), [Netherlands](/wiki/Netherlands "Netherlands"), [Romanian](/wiki/Romania "Romania") [Minister of Culture](/wiki/Ministry_of_Culture_%28Romania%29 "Ministry of Culture (Romania)") [Lucian Romașcanu](/wiki/Lucian_Roma%C8%99canu "Lucian Romașcanu") fires the director of the [National History Museum of Romania](/wiki/National_History_Museum_of_Romania "National History Museum of Romania") in [Bucharest](/wiki/Bucharest "Bucharest"). [(NOS)](https://nos.nl/artikel/2553649-verdachten-kunstroof-komen-uit-noord-holland-directeur-roemeens-museum-ontslagen)
* [Censorship in Pakistan](/wiki/Censorship_in_Pakistan "Censorship in Pakistan")
  + The [Senate of Pakistan](/wiki/Senate_of_Pakistan "Senate of Pakistan") passes a bill to criminalize the spread of [disinformation](/wiki/Disinformation "Disinformation") in [Pakistan](/wiki/Pakistan "Pakistan"), with the possibility of up to 3 years imprisonment and fines of up to [Rs.](/wiki/Pakistani_rupee "Pakistani rupee") 2 million (US$7,121). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/pakistan-social-media-fake-news-law/a-71433026)
* [Kyoto Animation arson attack](/wiki/Kyoto_Animation_arson_attack "Kyoto Animation arson attack")
  + The [Kyoto](/wiki/Kyoto "Kyoto") [District Court](/wiki/Public_Prosecutors_Office_%28Japan%29#District_Public_Prosecutors_Office "Public Prosecutors Office (Japan)") finalizes the [death sentence](/wiki/Death_sentence "Death sentence") for [Shinji Aoba](/wiki/Kyoto_Animation_arson_attack#Perpetrator "Kyoto Animation arson attack"), the perpetrator of the [arson](/wiki/Arson "Arson") attack on a [Kyoto Animation](/wiki/Kyoto_Animation "Kyoto Animation") studio in 2019, after he withdraws his appeal to the court's ruling. [(*The Japan Times*)](https://www.japantimes.co.jp/news/2025/01/28/japan/crime-legal/kyoani-death-penalty-finalized/)
* Three people, including the perpetrator, are killed and two police officers are injured in a [mass shooting](/wiki/Mass_shooting "Mass shooting") at a [Martin's Supermarket](/wiki/Spartan_Nash#Retail_chains "Spartan Nash") in [Elkhart](/wiki/Elkhart%2C_Indiana "Elkhart, Indiana"), [Indiana](/wiki/Indiana "Indiana"), United States. [(AP News)](https://apnews.com/article/grocery-store-shooting-police-elkhart-indiana-92f58b0f4dce09296dab6e5e80431735)

**Politics and elections**

* [Second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump")
  + [2025 United States federal government grant pause](/wiki/2025_United_States_federal_government_grant_pause "2025 United States federal government grant pause")
    - [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") [federal judge](/wiki/United_States_federal_judge "United States federal judge") of the [District Court of D.C.](/wiki/United_States_District_Court_for_the_District_of_Columbia "United States District Court for the District of Columbia") [Loren AliKhan](/wiki/Loren_AliKhan "Loren AliKhan") temporarily blocks [President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump")'s [executive order](/wiki/List_of_executive_orders_in_the_second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "List of executive orders in the second presidency of Donald Trump") to pause funding for [federal assistance](/wiki/Administration_of_federal_assistance_in_the_United_States "Administration of federal assistance in the United States") in the country. [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/us-judge-temporarily-blocks-trumps-freeze-on-federal-aid/a-71440078) [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/donald-trump-pause-federal-grants-aid-f9948b9996c0ca971f0065fac85737ce)
  + The [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") [Office of Personnel Management](/wiki/United_States_Office_of_Personnel_Management "United States Office of Personnel Management") offers a "deferred resignation" scheme to the 2 million federal government employees to announce their resignation by February 6, while stating that employees who resigned would still receive salary and benefits until September 30, 2025. [(OPM)](https://www.opm.gov/fork)[(OPM FAQ)](https://www.opm.gov/fork/faq)[(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/us/white-house-offers-incentives-federal-employees-resign-warns-downsizing-2025-01-28/)[(FNN)](https://federalnewsnetwork.com/workforce/2025/01/trump-administration-offers-most-feds-deferred-resignation-if-they-quit-by-next-week/)
* [2024–2025 Serbian anti-corruption protests](/wiki/2024%E2%80%932025_Serbian_anti-corruption_protests "2024–2025 Serbian anti-corruption protests")
  + [Serbian](/wiki/Serbia "Serbia") [prime minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Serbia "Prime Minister of Serbia") [Miloš Vučević](/wiki/Milo%C5%A1_Vu%C4%8Devi%C4%87 "Miloš Vučević") resigns following protests prompted by the [Novi Sad railway station canopy collapse](/wiki/Novi_Sad_railway_station_canopy_collapse "Novi Sad railway station canopy collapse"). [(BBC)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/c1m5x1j3p2yo)
* [2025 Ontario general election](/wiki/2025_Ontario_general_election "2025 Ontario general election")
  + [Ontario Premier](/wiki/Premier_of_Ontario "Premier of Ontario") [Doug Ford](/wiki/Doug_Ford "Doug Ford") announces that a new general election in the [Canadian province](/wiki/Provinces_and_territories_of_Canada "Provinces and territories of Canada") of [Ontario](/wiki/Ontario "Ontario") will be held on February 27. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/americas/canadas-most-populous-province-ontario-vote-feb-27-2025-01-28/)

**Science and technology**

* [2025 in aviation](/wiki/2025_in_aviation "2025 in aviation")
  + [Boom Technology](/wiki/Boom_Technology "Boom Technology")'s [XB-1](/wiki/Boom_XB-1 "Boom XB-1") supersonic demonstrator [trijet](/wiki/Trijet "Trijet") becomes the first privately-funded [jet-powered plane](/wiki/Jet_aircraft "Jet aircraft") to break the [sound barrier](/wiki/Speed_of_sound "Speed of sound") at [Mojave Air and Space Port](/wiki/Mojave_Air_and_Space_Port "Mojave Air and Space Port") in [Mojave](/wiki/Mojave%2C_California "Mojave, California"), [California](/wiki/California "California"), United States. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/business/aerospace-defense/boom-supersonic-xb-1-breaks-sound-barrier-over-mojave-desert-2025-01-28/)
* [Doomsday Clock](/wiki/Doomsday_Clock "Doomsday Clock")
  + The [Bulletin of the Atomic Scientists](/wiki/Bulletin_of_the_Atomic_Scientists "Bulletin of the Atomic Scientists") announces that the Doomsday Clock has been moved up to 89 seconds before midnight. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/atomic-scientists-adjust-doomsday-clock-closer-than-ever-midnight-2025-01-28/)
* [Google](/wiki/Google "Google") confirms that it will rename the [Gulf of Mexico](/wiki/Gulf_of_Mexico "Gulf of Mexico") to *Gulf of America* on [Google Maps](/wiki/Google_Maps "Google Maps") for US users in line with the official position of the [Trump administration](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump"). [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/technology/2025/jan/28/google-maps-will-rename-gulf-of-mexico-as-gulf-of-america-in-us)
* [Social media](/wiki/Social_media "Social media") service [Bluesky](/wiki/Bluesky "Bluesky") announces it has reached a milestone of 30 million users. [(*The Verge*)](https://www.theverge.com/news/602049/bluesky-now-has-30-million-users)

January 29, 2025 (2025-01-29) (Wednesday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_29&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_29&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_29&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [M23 offensive](/wiki/M23_offensive_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "M23 offensive (2022–present)")
    - [2025 Goma offensive](/wiki/2025_Goma_offensive "2025 Goma offensive")
      * [M23](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") rebels solidify control of [Goma](/wiki/Goma "Goma"), [North Kivu Province](/wiki/North_Kivu_Province "North Kivu Province"), and are confirmed to be holding captured [Congolese troops](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Armed Forces of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") and allied [Wazalendo](/wiki/Wazalendo "Wazalendo") militants at the [Stade de l'Unité](/wiki/Stade_de_l%27Unit%C3%A9 "Stade de l'Unité"). They also begin advancing on [Bukavu](/wiki/Bukavu "Bukavu"), capital of the [South Kivu Province](/wiki/South_Kivu "South Kivu"), according to senior [Congolese](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo") officials and a [Rwandan](/wiki/Rwanda "Rwanda") diplomat. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/liveblog/2025/1/29/dr-congo-live-news-rwanda-backed-m23-rebels-tighten-grip-on-goma) [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/rwandas-kagame-says-he-agrees-with-us-need-ceasefire-congo-2025-01-29/)
      * In an emergency address to the nation, [Congolese president](/wiki/President_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "President of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") [Félix Tshisekedi](/wiki/F%C3%A9lix_Tshisekedi "Félix Tshisekedi") calls for calm and says "a vigorous and coordinated response against these terrorists and their sponsors is underway" by the armed forces, and also cancels participation in a regional summit with [Rwandan president](/wiki/List_of_presidents_of_Rwanda "List of presidents of Rwanda") [Paul Kagame](/wiki/Paul_Kagame "Paul Kagame"). [(*Foreign Policy*)](https://foreignpolicy.com/2025/01/29/congo-rwanda-m23-rebels-goma-tshisekedi-kagame/) [(*Le Monde*)](https://www.lemonde.fr/en/international/article/2025/01/30/dr-congo-president-says-army-mounting-vigorous-response-to-m23-advance_6737579_4.html)
    - Around 280 [Romanian](/wiki/Romanians "Romanians") [mercenaries](/wiki/Mercenary "Mercenary") fighting alongside the Congolese military in [North Kivu](/wiki/North_Kivu "North Kivu") surrender to the M23, according to the [Rwandan military](/wiki/Rwandan_Defence_Force "Rwandan Defence Force"). They are now being transported to [Kigali](/wiki/Kigali "Kigali") after being handed over to Rwandan authorities. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/cd0j4d7v229o)
* [War against the Islamic State](/wiki/War_against_the_Islamic_State "War against the Islamic State")
  + [War in Somalia](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)")
    - [Islamic State insurgency in Puntland](/wiki/Islamic_State_insurgency_in_Puntland "Islamic State insurgency in Puntland")
      * [Puntland](/wiki/Puntland "Puntland") authorities deport around a thousand undocumented [Ethiopians](/wiki/Ethiopians "Ethiopians") from the cities of [Bosaso](/wiki/Bosaso "Bosaso"), [Galkayo](/wiki/Galkayo "Galkayo"), [Qardho](/wiki/Qardho "Qardho"), and the state’s capital, [Garoowe](/wiki/Garoowe "Garoowe"), as part of an ongoing crackdown on foreigners without legal status, following the discovery of foreign fighters acting as [Islamic State](/wiki/Islamic_State "Islamic State") recruiters in the [Cal Miskaad](/wiki/Cal_Miskaad "Cal Miskaad") mountains of the [Bari Region](/wiki/Bari_Region "Bari Region"). [(Hiiraan Online)](https://www.hiiraan.com/news4/2025/Jan/200008/puntland_deports_hundreds_of_undocumented_ethiopians_over_isis_recruitment_concerns.aspx) [(Idil News)](https://www.idilnews.com/puntland-oo-dib-ugu-celisay-dalkooda-boqolaal-itoobiyaan-ah/) [(Horseed Media)](https://horseedmedia.net/puntland-oo-masaafurisay-boqolaal-ajaaniib-ah-oo-sharci-darro-ku-joogay-deegaanadeeda/399908/)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [2025 Gaza war ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire")
    - [U.S.](/wiki/U.S. "U.S.") [Middle East](/wiki/Middle_East "Middle East") Envoy [Steve Witkoff](/wiki/Steve_Witkoff "Steve Witkoff") visits the [Gaza Strip](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip") and meets with [Israeli](/wiki/Israel "Israel") [prime minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Israel "Prime Minister of Israel") [Benjamin Netanyahu](/wiki/Benjamin_Netanyahu "Benjamin Netanyahu") to assure that the [ceasefire](/wiki/Ceasefire "Ceasefire") remains intact. [(NPR)](https://www.npr.org/2025/01/29/nx-s1-5279178/us-mideast-envoy-steve-witkoff-gaza-israel-netanyahu)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Battle of Chasiv Yar](/wiki/Battle_of_Chasiv_Yar "Battle of Chasiv Yar")
    - [Russian forces](/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces "Russian Armed Forces") capture the city of [Chasiv Yar](/wiki/Chasiv_Yar "Chasiv Yar") in [Donetsk Oblast](/wiki/Donetsk_Oblast "Donetsk Oblast"), [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"), after a year of intense fighting for control of the [front line](/wiki/Front_line "Front line") city. [(*The Moscow Times*)](https://www.themoscowtimes.com/2025/01/29/chasiv-yar-falls-to-russian-forces-after-nearly-a-year-of-intense-fighting-a87781)

**Business and economy**

* [Expansion of Heathrow Airport](/wiki/Expansion_of_Heathrow_Airport "Expansion of Heathrow Airport")
  + [UK](/wiki/United_Kingdom "United Kingdom") [Chancellor of the Exchequer](/wiki/Chancellor_of_the_Exchequer "Chancellor of the Exchequer") [Rachel Reeves](/wiki/Rachel_Reeves "Rachel Reeves") approves the construction of a third [runway](/wiki/Runway "Runway") at [Greater London](/wiki/Greater_London "Greater London")'s [Heathrow Airport](/wiki/Heathrow_Airport "Heathrow Airport") after decades of delays. [(Sky News)](https://news.sky.com/story/chancellor-rachel-reeves-announces-backing-for-third-heathrow-runway-13298590)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 Prayag Kumbh Mela](/wiki/2025_Prayag_Kumbh_Mela "2025 Prayag Kumbh Mela")

    - At least 30 people are killed in a [crowd crush](/wiki/Crowd_crush "Crowd crush") at a [Hindu](/wiki/Hinduism "Hinduism") festival in [Prayagraj](/wiki/Prayagraj "Prayagraj"), [Uttar Pradesh](/wiki/Uttar_Pradesh "Uttar Pradesh"), [India](/wiki/India "India"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/live/cgq07z0yexvt)

  + A [Beechcraft 1900D](/wiki/Beechcraft_1900 "Beechcraft 1900") carrying employees of an [oil company](/wiki/Petroleum_industry "Petroleum industry") crashes in [Unity](/wiki/Unity_%28state%29 "Unity (state)"), [South Sudan](/wiki/South_Sudan "South Sudan"), killing 20 of the 21 people onboard, including one [Indian](/wiki/India "India") and two [Chinese](/wiki/China "China") nationals. [(CNN)](https://www.cnn.com/2025/01/29/africa/south-sudan-plane-crash-intl/index.html) [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/plane-crash-south-sudans-unity-state-kills-18-uns-radio-miraya-reports-2025-01-29/)
* [2025 Potomac River mid-air collision](/wiki/2025_Potomac_River_mid-air_collision "2025 Potomac River mid-air collision")
  + A [PSA Airlines](/wiki/PSA_Airlines "PSA Airlines") [Bombardier CRJ-700](/wiki/Bombardier_CRJ-700 "Bombardier CRJ-700") operating as [American Eagle](/wiki/American_Eagle_%28airline_brand%29 "American Eagle (airline brand)") Flight 5342 collides with a [U.S. Army](/wiki/United_States_Army "United States Army") [Sikorsky UH-60 Black Hawk](/wiki/Sikorsky_UH-60_Black_Hawk "Sikorsky UH-60 Black Hawk") over the [Potomac River](/wiki/Potomac_River "Potomac River") near [Reagan National Airport](/wiki/Ronald_Reagan_Washington_National_Airport "Ronald Reagan Washington National Airport") in [Washington, D.C.](/wiki/Washington%2C_D.C. "Washington, D.C."), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), killing at least 28 people between both aircraft and causing a shutdown of flights in and out of the airport. [(WUSA-9)](https://www.wusa9.com/article/travel/all-flights-halted-at-reagan-national-airport-due-to-plane-crash-potomac-river-dc/65-e2090f2d-0bca-4a4c-944c-215a6398a52d) [(NBC NEWS)](https://www.nbcnews.com/news/us-news/live-blog/live-updates-plane-crashes-potomac-river-collision-helicopter-reagan-n-rcna189942)
* Thirteen [artisanal miners](/wiki/Artisanal_mining "Artisanal mining"), including three children, are killed when a tunnel at a [gold mine](/wiki/Gold_mine "Gold mine") floods after a reservoir spill in [Kangaba](/wiki/Kangaba_Cercle "Kangaba Cercle"), [Koulikoro](/wiki/Koulikoro_Region "Koulikoro Region"), [Mali](/wiki/Mali "Mali"). [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/africa/mali-gold-mine-accident-kills-more-than-dozen-including-women-children-2025-02-01/)
* Five people, four from [Norway](/wiki/Norway "Norway") and one from [Switzerland](/wiki/Switzerland "Switzerland"), are killed in two separate avalanches while [off-piste skiing](/wiki/Off-piste_skiing "Off-piste skiing") in the [French Alps](/wiki/French_Alps "French Alps"). [(BBC)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/czep67j3w8do)
* A [Venezuelan](/wiki/Venezuela "Venezuela") [Ministry of Interior, Justice and Peace](/wiki/Ministry_of_Interior%2C_Justice_and_Peace_%28Venezuela%29 "Ministry of Interior, Justice and Peace (Venezuela)") [Cessna Citation II](/wiki/Cessna_Citation_II "Cessna Citation II") aircraft crashes shortly after takeoff from [Generalissimo Francisco de Miranda Air Base](/wiki/Generalissimo_Francisco_de_Miranda_Air_Base "Generalissimo Francisco de Miranda Air Base") in [Caracas](/wiki/Caracas "Caracas"), Venezuela, killing all three people on board. [(Caraota Digital)](https://caraotadigital.net/venezuela/avioneta-se-estrello-en-el-sector-el-volcan-en-el-hatillo-habia-despegado-desde-la-carlota/)

**Law and crime**

* [First 100 days of the second Donald Trump presidency](/wiki/First_100_days_of_the_second_Donald_Trump_presidency "First 100 days of the second Donald Trump presidency")
  + [U.S. President](/wiki/President_of_the_United_States "President of the United States") [Donald Trump](/wiki/Donald_Trump "Donald Trump") signs the [Laken Riley Act](/wiki/Laken_Riley_Act "Laken Riley Act") into law, the first legislation of [Trump's second term](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump"). [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/news/amp/rcna188917)
  + President Trump announces plans to transform the [United States detention facility](/wiki/Guantanamo_Bay_detention_camp "Guantanamo Bay detention camp") in [Cuba](/wiki/Cuba "Cuba")'s [Guantánamo Bay](/wiki/Guant%C3%A1namo_Bay "Guantánamo Bay") into a holding center for undocumented immigrants, capable of hosting 30,000 people. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/29/us-president-trump-to-transfer-undocumented-immigrants-to-guantanamo)
* [Police](/wiki/Baden-W%C3%BCrttemberg_Police "Baden-Württemberg Police") in [Stuttgart](/wiki/Stuttgart "Stuttgart"), [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany"), arrest 59 [French](/wiki/France "France") fans of the [Paris Saint-Germain](/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain "Paris Saint-Germain") football club for [hooliganism](/wiki/Hooliganism "Hooliganism") before a match against German club [VfB Stuttgart](/wiki/VfB_Stuttgart "VfB Stuttgart"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/germany-psg-fans-arrested-champions-league/a-71443613)
* Former [U.S. Senator](/wiki/U.S._Senator "U.S. Senator") [Bob Menendez](/wiki/Bob_Menendez "Bob Menendez") of [New Jersey](/wiki/New_Jersey "New Jersey") is sentenced to 11 years in prison, following his conviction on [bribery](/wiki/Bribery "Bribery") and [corruption](/wiki/Corruption "Corruption") charges. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/clyekv226l2o)

**Politics and elections**

* [Second presidency of Donald Trump](/wiki/Second_presidency_of_Donald_Trump "Second presidency of Donald Trump")
  + [2025 United States federal government grant pause](/wiki/2025_United_States_federal_government_grant_pause "2025 United States federal government grant pause")
    - The [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States") [Office of Management and Budget](/wiki/Office_of_Management_and_Budget "Office of Management and Budget") rescinds a memo from Monday that would have paused [federal financial assistance programs](/wiki/Administration_of_federal_assistance_in_the_United_States "Administration of federal assistance in the United States") implicated by select [executive orders](/wiki/Executive_orders "Executive orders") of President Donald Trump, following a temporary block of the order on Tuesday by a [federal judge](/wiki/Loren_AliKhan "Loren AliKhan"). Following the rescission, [White House Press Secretary](/wiki/White_House_Press_Secretary "White House Press Secretary") [Karoline Leavitt](/wiki/Karoline_Leavitt "Karoline Leavitt") states that the Trump administration will continue to pursue a freeze of federal funds. [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cyv48540n4po)
* [Syrian civil war](/wiki/Syrian_civil_war "Syrian civil war")
  + [Ahmed al-Sharaa](/wiki/Ahmed_al-Sharaa "Ahmed al-Sharaa") is declared the [president of Syria](/wiki/President_of_Syria "President of Syria") during the [transition period](/wiki/First_Syrian_transitional_government "First Syrian transitional government"), a month after [Bashar al-Assad](/wiki/Bashar_al-Assad "Bashar al-Assad") was [ousted](/wiki/Fall_of_the_Assad_regime "Fall of the Assad regime") by rebel forces. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/syrias-leader-sharaa-named-president-transitional-period-state-news-agency-says-2025-01-29/)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [M23 offensive](/wiki/M23_offensive_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "M23 offensive (2022–present)")
    - [2025 Goma offensive](/wiki/2025_Goma_offensive "2025 Goma offensive")
      * [Rwandan](/wiki/Rwanda "Rwanda")-backed [M23](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") rebels say they will march on the [Democratic Republic of the Congo](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Democratic Republic of the Congo") capital city [Kinshasa](/wiki/Kinshasa "Kinshasa") and install a new government as [Congolese president](/wiki/President_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "President of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") [Félix Tshisekedi](/wiki/F%C3%A9lix_Tshisekedi "Félix Tshisekedi") calls for a [mobilization](/wiki/Mobilization "Mobilization") of young males to reclaim lost territory. Congolese [defence minister](/wiki/Minister_of_Defence_%28Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo%29 "Minister of Defence (Democratic Republic of the Congo)") [Guy Kabombo Muadiamvita](/wiki/Guy_Kabombo_Muadiamvita "Guy Kabombo Muadiamvita") says there will be no [peace talks](/wiki/Peace_process "Peace process") with the rebels. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/congo-m23-goma-rwanda-tshisekedi-south-africa-ca81f34f52ea31b85dd845b049a0bb96)
      * After establishing a new administration in [Goma](/wiki/Goma "Goma"), [Congo River Alliance](/wiki/Congo_River_Alliance "Congo River Alliance") leader [Corneille Nangaa](/wiki/Corneille_Nangaa "Corneille Nangaa") confirms his forces now plan on overthrowing president Félix Tshisekedi. He also says services in the city will return to normal soon as the [United Nations](/wiki/United_Nations "United Nations") warns of a [humanitarian crisis](/wiki/Humanitarian_crisis "Humanitarian crisis"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.co.uk/news/articles/ckgn1k9nleno)
    - M23 forces advance into [South Kivu](/wiki/South_Kivu "South Kivu"), capturing several towns and villages, including [Kalungu](/wiki/Kalungu%2C_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Kalungu, Democratic Republic of the Congo") in [Kalehe Territory](/wiki/Kalehe_Territory "Kalehe Territory"). [(MSN)](https://www.msn.com/en-us/news/world/armed-rebels-seize-two-more-towns-after-huge-city-falls/ar-AA1y97nF)
* [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)")
  + [Puntland–Somaliland dispute](/wiki/Puntland%E2%80%93Somaliland_dispute "Puntland–Somaliland dispute")
    - [Spillover of Las Anod conflict](/wiki/Las_Anod_conflict_%282023%E2%80%93present%29 "Las Anod conflict (2023–present)")
      * [SSC Khaatumo](/wiki/Khatumo_State "Khatumo State") officials claim victory over [Somaliland forces](/wiki/Somaliland_National_Army "Somaliland National Army") after heavy fighting erupted with undisclosed casualties early Thursday in the Shangeed area, located between [Qoorlugud](/wiki/Qoorlugud "Qoorlugud") and [Buuhoodle](/wiki/Buuhoodle "Buuhoodle") of [Cayn](/wiki/Cayn "Cayn"),[Somalia](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia"). [(Hiiraan Online)](https://hiiraan.com/news/2025/Jan/wararka_maanta31-189189.htm?utm_source=hiiraan&utm_medium=WararkaMaantaFront)
* [2023 Quran burnings in Sweden](/wiki/2023_Quran_burnings_in_Sweden "2023 Quran burnings in Sweden"), [Islam and blasphemy](/wiki/Islam_and_blasphemy "Islam and blasphemy")
  + [Killing of Salwan Momika](/wiki/Killing_of_Salwan_Momika "Killing of Salwan Momika")
    - [Islam critic](/wiki/Criticism_of_Islam "Criticism of Islam") and [Quran burner](/wiki/Quran_desecration "Quran desecration") [Salwan Momika](/wiki/Salwan_Momika "Salwan Momika") is [assassinated](/wiki/Assassination "Assassination") at his apartment in [Södertälje](/wiki/S%C3%B6dert%C3%A4lje "Södertälje"), [Sweden](/wiki/Sweden "Sweden"). [(BBC News)](https://www.bbc.com/news/articles/cpdx2wqpg7zo)
* [Gaza war](/wiki/Gaza_war "Gaza war")
  + [2025 Gaza war ceasefire](/wiki/2025_Gaza_war_ceasefire "2025 Gaza war ceasefire"), [Gaza war hostage crisis](/wiki/Gaza_war_hostage_crisis "Gaza war hostage crisis")
    - [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") free eight hostages, three [Israelis](/wiki/Israelis "Israelis") and five [Thai](/wiki/Thailand "Thailand") nationals. [(*The Times of Israel*)](https://www.timesofisrael.com/hostages-agam-berger-arbel-yehoud-gadi-mozes-5-thai-nationals-freed-from-gaza-after-482-days/)
    - Israel releases 110 [Palestinian](/wiki/Palestinians "Palestinians") [prisoners](/wiki/Palestinian_prisoners_in_Israel "Palestinian prisoners in Israel") after initially delaying their release in protest of the chaotic scenes at the handover of several hostages in [Khan Yunis](/wiki/Khan_Yunis "Khan Yunis"), [Gaza](/wiki/Gaza_Strip "Gaza Strip"), earlier today, citing concerns for the hostages' safety. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/middle-east/palestinian-militants-arrive-gaza-site-before-hostage-handover-militant-sources-2025-01-30/)
  + [Hamas](/wiki/Hamas "Hamas") confirms that Israel killed [Mohammed Deif](/wiki/Mohammed_Deif "Mohammed Deif") along with [Marwan Issa](/wiki/Marwan_Issa "Marwan Issa"), Raed Thabet, [Rafa Salama](/wiki/Rafa_Salama "Rafa Salama"), [Ayman Nofal](/wiki/Ayman_Nofal "Ayman Nofal") and Ghazi Abu Tamaa. [(Al Arabiya)](https://www.alarabiya.net/arab-and-world/2025/01/30/%D8%B1%D8%B3%D9%85%D9%8A%D8%A7-%D8%AD%D9%85%D8%A7%D8%B3-%D8%AA%D9%86%D8%B9%D9%89-%D9%85%D8%AD%D9%85%D8%AF-%D8%A7%D9%84%D8%B6%D9%8A%D9%81)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Attacks on civilians in the Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Attacks_on_civilians_in_the_Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Attacks on civilians in the Russian invasion of Ukraine")
    - A [Russian](/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces "Russian Armed Forces") [drone strikes](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") a multi-storey [apartment building](/wiki/Apartment_building "Apartment building") in [Sumy](/wiki/Sumy "Sumy"), [Ukraine](/wiki/Ukraine "Ukraine"), killing nine people and injuring 13 others. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/russian-drone-strikes-apartment-block-ukraine-killing-four-governor-says-2025-01-30/)
* [French military withdrawal from West Africa](/wiki/French_military_withdrawal_from_West_Africa_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "French military withdrawal from West Africa (2022–present)")
  + The [French Armed Forces](/wiki/French_Armed_Forces "French Armed Forces") returns their last [military base](/wiki/Military_base "Military base") in [Chad](/wiki/Chad "Chad") to the [Chad National Army](/wiki/Chad_National_Army "Chad National Army"), bringing an end to [French](/wiki/France "France") military presence in the country. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/chad-france-military-bases-withdrawal-bd1c1e5a075f3a4b0dba01801c081728)

  + A [shootout](/wiki/Shootout "Shootout") between the [Pakistan Army](/wiki/Pakistan_Army "Pakistan Army") and [Pakistani Taliban](/wiki/Pakistani_Taliban "Pakistani Taliban") in [North Waziristan District](/wiki/North_Waziristan_District "North Waziristan District"), [Khyber Pakhtunkhwa](/wiki/Khyber_Pakhtunkhwa "Khyber Pakhtunkhwa"), [Pakistan](/wiki/Pakistan "Pakistan"), leaves two soldiers and six militants dead. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/pakistan-security-forces-raid-militant-hideout-b0a2eeaaed66ad249bc48ed50a03405b)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 Potomac River mid-air collision](/wiki/2025_Potomac_River_mid-air_collision "2025 Potomac River mid-air collision")
  + The [District of Columbia Fire and Emergency Medical Services Department](/wiki/District_of_Columbia_Fire_and_Emergency_Medical_Services_Department "District of Columbia Fire and Emergency Medical Services Department") says no survivors are expected after the midair collision between an [American Airlines](/wiki/American_Airlines "American Airlines") aicraft and a [military](/wiki/United_States_Armed_Forces "United States Armed Forces") [helicopter](/wiki/Military_helicopter "Military helicopter") last night over [Washington, D.C.](/wiki/Washington%2C_D.C. "Washington, D.C."), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), making it the deadliest aviation disaster in the U.S. since [American Airlines Flight 587](/wiki/American_Airlines_Flight_587 "American Airlines Flight 587") in 2001. [(CNN)](https://edition.cnn.com/us/live-news/plane-crash-dca-potomac-washington-dc-01-29-25/index.html)

**Health and environment**

* [Uganda](/wiki/Uganda "Uganda") confirms an outbreak of [Ebola](/wiki/Ebola "Ebola"), with the first death, a nurse at [Mulago National Specialised Hospital](/wiki/Mulago_National_Specialised_Hospital "Mulago National Specialised Hospital") in [Kampala](/wiki/Kampala "Kampala"), being confirmed yesterday. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/business/healthcare-pharmaceuticals/uganda-confirms-outbreak-ebola-capital-kampala-2025-01-30/)
* The United States [Federal Drug Administration](/wiki/Federal_Drug_Administration "Federal Drug Administration") approves [Vertex Pharmaceuticals](/wiki/Vertex_Pharmaceuticals "Vertex Pharmaceuticals")' new [Journavx](/wiki/Suzetrigine "Suzetrigine") drug, a non-[opioid](/wiki/Opioid "Opioid") [analgesic](/wiki/Analgesic "Analgesic") used to [treat acute pain](/wiki/Pain_management "Pain management") and potentially eliminate the risks of [opioid addiction](/wiki/Opioid_addiction "Opioid addiction") and [overdose](/wiki/Drug_overdose "Drug overdose"). [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/nonopioid-painkiller-fda-vertex-pharmaceuticals-b1dd4276fce3d88ff32e3062e95f408f) [(FDA)](https://www.fda.gov/news-events/press-announcements/fda-approves-novel-non-opioid-treatment-moderate-severe-acute-pain)

**Law and crime**

* [FBI Ten Most Wanted Fugitives](/wiki/FBI_Ten_Most_Wanted_Fugitives "FBI Ten Most Wanted Fugitives")
  + American [fugitive](/wiki/Most_wanted_list "Most wanted list") [Arnoldo Jimenez](/wiki/Arnoldo_Jimenez "Arnoldo Jimenez") is arrested in [Monterrey](/wiki/Monterrey "Monterrey"), [Mexico](/wiki/Mexico "Mexico"), after over a decade on the run for the murder of his wife. [(WMAQ-TV)](https://www.nbcchicago.com/news/local/top-10-most-wanted-fugitive-taken-into-custody-fbi-chicago-announces/3662385/)

**Politics and elections**

* Following weeks of unsuccessful negotiations, the [Centre Party](/wiki/Centre_Party_%28Norway%29 "Centre Party (Norway)") withdraws from the [Norwegian government](/wiki/St%C3%B8re_Cabinet "Støre Cabinet") over disagreements over the implementation of three directives in the [European Union's fourth energy package](/wiki/Energy_policy_of_the_European_Union "Energy policy of the European Union"), with the [Labour Party](/wiki/Labour_Party_%28Norway%29 "Labour Party (Norway)") continuing as a [single party minority government](/wiki/Minority_government "Minority government"). [(NRK)](https://www.nrk.no/norge/avviser-at-han-er-svekket-som-statsminister_-_-her-star-jeg_-jeg-er-ikke-vekk_-1.17239250)
* Thousands of people gather in [Berlin](/wiki/Berlin "Berlin"), [Germany](/wiki/Germany "Germany"), to protest against [Chancellor](/wiki/Chancellor_of_Germany "Chancellor of Germany")-candidate [Friedrich Merz](/wiki/Friedrich_Merz "Friedrich Merz") and the [Christian Democratic Union](/wiki/Christian_Democratic_Union_of_Germany "Christian Democratic Union of Germany") and [Christian Social Union](/wiki/Christian_Social_Union_in_Bavaria "Christian Social Union in Bavaria") parties after they collaborated with the [Alternative for Germany](/wiki/Alternative_for_Germany "Alternative for Germany") (AfD) party on a [non-binding motion](/wiki/Non-binding_resolution "Non-binding resolution") to restrict [immigration](/wiki/Immigration_to_Germany "Immigration to Germany"). Members of the [Bundestag](/wiki/Bundestag "Bundestag") debate on [motions](/wiki/Motion_%28legal%29 "Motion (legal)") to ban the AfD, alleging that its beliefs and legal practices are [unconstitutional](/wiki/Constitution_of_Germany "Constitution of Germany"). [(DW)](https://www.dw.com/en/germany-mass-protests-after-far-right-afd-helps-cdu-csu/a-71464257) [(Anadolu Ajansi)](https://www.aa.com.tr/en/europe/german-parliament-debates-potential-ban-on-far-right-afd/3467314)
* The [Nicaraguan](/wiki/Nicaragua "Nicaragua") [National Assembly](/wiki/National_Assembly_%28Nicaragua%29 "National Assembly (Nicaragua)") votes unanimously to pass several [constitutional](/wiki/Constitution_of_Nicaragua "Constitution of Nicaragua") reforms that grants the [government](/wiki/Government_of_Nicaragua "Government of Nicaragua") influence over the [media](/wiki/Mass_media_in_Nicaragua "Mass media in Nicaragua"), extend the presidential [term](/wiki/Term_limit "Term limit") to 6 years, and makes [President](/wiki/President_of_Nicaragua "President of Nicaragua") [Daniel Ortega](/wiki/Daniel_Ortega "Daniel Ortega")'s [wife](/wiki/First_Lady_of_Nicaragua "First Lady of Nicaragua") [Rosario Murillo](/wiki/Rosario_Murillo "Rosario Murillo") co-President. [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/30/nicaragua-approves-constitutional-reforms-giving-president-expansive-powers)

**Science and technology**

* [Apollo-type asteroid](/wiki/Apollo_asteroid "Apollo asteroid") [2024 YR4](/wiki/2024_YR4 "2024 YR4") triggers [global planetary defence procedures](/wiki/Asteroid_impact_avoidance "Asteroid impact avoidance") for the first time and rises to the top of the [Palermo Technical Impact Hazard Scale](/wiki/Palermo_Technical_Impact_Hazard_Scale "Palermo Technical Impact Hazard Scale") after recent observations confirmed it has a 1-in-77 (1.3%) chance of impacting [Earth](/wiki/Earth "Earth") on 22 December 2032. Follow up observations in 2028 will provide a more refined estimation of the likelihood of impact in 2032. [(*The Guardian*)](https://www.theguardian.com/science/2025/jan/30/asteroid-spotted-chance-colliding-with-earth-2032)

January 31, 2025 (2025-01-31) (Friday)

* [edit](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_31&action=edit&editintro=Portal:Current_events/Edit_instructions)
* [history](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_31&action=history)
* [watch](https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Portal:Current_events/2025_January_31&action=watch)

**Armed conflicts and attacks**

* [Sudanese civil war](/wiki/Sudanese_civil_war_%282023-present%29 "Sudanese civil war (2023-present)")
  + [Battle of Khartoum](/wiki/Battle_of_Khartoum_%282023-present%29 "Battle of Khartoum (2023-present)")
    - [2025 Bahri offensive](/wiki/2025_Bahri_offensive "2025 Bahri offensive")
      * The [Sudanese Armed Forces](/wiki/Sudanese_Armed_Forces "Sudanese Armed Forces") announce that they have nearly captured all of [Bahri](/wiki/Khartoum_North "Khartoum North"), [Khartoum State](/wiki/Khartoum_State "Khartoum State"), [Sudan](/wiki/Sudan "Sudan"). [(Radio Dabanga)](https://www.dabangasudan.org/en/all-news/article/sudan-army-further-advances-in-khartoum-bahri) [(*Sudan Tribune*)](https://sudantribune.com/article296726/)
* [Israeli invasion of Lebanon](/wiki/Israeli_invasion_of_Lebanon_%282024%E2%80%93present%29 "Israeli invasion of Lebanon (2024–present)")
  + [2024 Israel–Lebanon ceasefire agreement](/wiki/2024_Israel%E2%80%93Lebanon_ceasefire_agreement "2024 Israel–Lebanon ceasefire agreement")
    - Two people are killed and ten others are injured during [Israeli](/wiki/Israel "Israel") [airstrikes](/wiki/Airstrike "Airstrike") in the [Beqaa Valley](/wiki/Beqaa_Valley "Beqaa Valley"), [Lebanon](/wiki/Lebanon "Lebanon"). [(Al Jazeera)](https://www.aljazeera.com/news/2025/1/31/israel-attacks-lebanons-bekaa-valley-in-violation-of-ceasefire-deal)
* [Kivu conflict](/wiki/Kivu_conflict "Kivu conflict")
  + [M23 offensive](/wiki/M23_offensive_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "M23 offensive (2022–present)"), [Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda conflict](/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo%E2%80%93Rwanda_conflict "Democratic Republic of the Congo–Rwanda conflict")
    - The [Congolese military](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_the_Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo "Armed Forces of the Democratic Republic of the Congo") launches a counterattack against [M23](/wiki/March_23_Movement "March 23 Movement") rebels in [South Kivu](/wiki/South_Kivu "South Kivu") province with the assistance of the [Burundian military](/wiki/National_Defence_Force_%28Burundi%29 "National Defence Force (Burundi)"). [(Reuters)](https://www.yahoo.com/news/congos-army-burundian-allies-slow-122615740.html)
* [Russian invasion of Ukraine](/wiki/Russian_invasion_of_Ukraine "Russian invasion of Ukraine")
  + [Odesa strikes](/wiki/Odesa_strikes_%282022%E2%80%93present%29 "Odesa strikes (2022–present)")
    - [Russian forces](/wiki/Russian_Armed_Forces "Russian Armed Forces") launch [ballistic missiles](/wiki/Ballistic_missile "Ballistic missile") at the centre of [Odesa](/wiki/Odesa "Odesa") and [its port](/wiki/Port_of_Odesa "Port of Odesa"), severely damaging numerous civilian buildings, including the historic [Bristol Hotel](/wiki/Bristol_Hotel%2C_Odesa "Bristol Hotel, Odesa"). At least two people are reportedly injured. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/europe/russian-forces-launch-missile-attack-historic-centre-ukraines-odesa-2025-01-31/)
* [Mexican drug war](/wiki/Mexican_drug_war "Mexican drug war")
  + An [improvised explosive device](/wiki/Improvised_explosive_device "Improvised explosive device") left by [cartel](/wiki/Drug_cartel "Drug cartel") members detonates in [San Fernando](/wiki/San_Fernando%2C_Tamaulipas "San Fernando, Tamaulipas"), [Tamaulipas](/wiki/Tamaulipas "Tamaulipas"), [Mexico](/wiki/Mexico "Mexico"), killing two villagers and injuring a third. [(*El Sol de Tampico*)](https://oem.com.mx/elsoldetampico/policiaca/vehiculo-se-incendia-por-activacion-de-artefacto-explosivo-y-deja-dos-muertos-en-tamaulipas-21475612)
* [Somali Civil War](/wiki/Somali_Civil_War_%282009%E2%80%93present%29 "Somali Civil War (2009–present)")
  + [Somali President](/wiki/President_of_Somalia "President of Somalia") [Hassan Sheikh Mohamud](/wiki/Hassan_Sheikh_Mohamud "Hassan Sheikh Mohamud") and [Prime Minister](/wiki/List_of_prime_ministers_of_Somalia "List of prime ministers of Somalia") [Hamza Abdi Barre](/wiki/Hamza_Abdi_Barre "Hamza Abdi Barre") escape after security guards shoot down one of two [drones](/wiki/Drone_warfare "Drone warfare") hovering over [Villa Somalia](/wiki/Villa_Somalia "Villa Somalia") in [Mogadishu](/wiki/Mogadishu "Mogadishu"), [Somalia](/wiki/Somalia "Somalia"). The drones are believed to be used by [ISIL](/wiki/Islamic_State_%E2%80%93_Somalia_Province "Islamic State – Somalia Province") and [Al-Shabaab](/wiki/Al-Shabaab_%28militant_group%29 "Al-Shabaab (militant group)"). This comes after previous [Somali Civil Aviation Authority](/wiki/Somali_Civil_Aviation_Authority "Somali Civil Aviation Authority") warnings. [(Idil News)](https://www.idilnews.com/mogadishu-hassan-sheikh-mohamud-and-hamza-abdi-barre-rush-out-immediately-after-downing-a-drone-over-villa-somalia/) [(Horn Observer)](https://hornobserver.com/articles/3162/Somalias-Presidential-guards-reportedly-fired-at-several-drones-hovering-over-the-Presidents-office)

**Business and economy**

* [2025 Yugosphere retail boycotts](/wiki/2025_Yugosphere_retail_boycotts "2025 Yugosphere retail boycotts")
  + Following [boycotts](/wiki/Boycott "Boycott") in [Croatia](/wiki/Croatia "Croatia") on January 24, and in conjunction with a follow-up boycott in the country, residents of [Bosnia and Herzegovina](/wiki/Bosnia_and_Herzegovina "Bosnia and Herzegovina"), [Serbia](/wiki/Serbia "Serbia"), [Montenegro](/wiki/Montenegro "Montenegro"), and [North Macedonia](/wiki/North_Macedonia "North Macedonia") start a boycott of [retail stores](/wiki/Retail "Retail") in response to rising prices. [(Intellinews)](https://www.intellinews.com/shopping-boycotts-launched-across-the-balkans-364355/)
* [Multinational](/wiki/Multinational_corporation "Multinational corporation") [telecoms company](/wiki/Telecommunications_industry "Telecommunications industry") [BT Group](/wiki/BT_Group "BT Group") announces that it will [layoff](/wiki/Layoff "Layoff") 55,000 employees across its global workforce citing a significant drop in revenue in 2024 and "challenges in international markets". [(Business Plus)](https://businessplus.ie/jobs/bt-jobs-worldwide/)

**Disasters and accidents**

* [2025 California wildfires](/wiki/2025_California_wildfires "2025 California wildfires")
  + [January 2025 Southern California wildfires](/wiki/January_2025_Southern_California_wildfires "January 2025 Southern California wildfires")
    - The [California Department of Forestry and Fire Protection](/wiki/California_Department_of_Forestry_and_Fire_Protection "California Department of Forestry and Fire Protection") reports that the [Palisades](/wiki/Palisades_Fire "Palisades Fire") and [Eaton](/wiki/Eaton_Fire "Eaton Fire") [fires](/wiki/Wildfire "Wildfire") are contained. [(NBC News)](https://www.nbcnews.com/weather/wildfires/palisades-eaton-fire-la-contained-rcna188338)
* [Med Jets Flight 056](/wiki/Med_Jets_Flight_056 "Med Jets Flight 056")
  + A [Learjet 55](/wiki/Learjet_55 "Learjet 55") [air ambulance](/wiki/Air_medical_services "Air medical services") crashes in [Northeast Philadelphia](/wiki/Northeast_Philadelphia "Northeast Philadelphia"), [Pennsylvania](/wiki/Pennsylvania "Pennsylvania"), [United States](/wiki/United_States "United States"), after departing from [Northeast Philadelphia Airport](/wiki/Northeast_Philadelphia_Airport "Northeast Philadelphia Airport"), killing all six people onboard and damaging multiple homes and businesses. One person on the ground is also killed and 19 more injured. [(AP)](https://apnews.com/article/philadelphia-plane-crash-medical-transport-8617dab53471190832dd73db149489fa)
* Five people are killed and two more injured in [Aghjabadi](/wiki/Aghjabadi "Aghjabadi"), [Azerbaijan](/wiki/Azerbaijan "Azerbaijan"), after a child accidentally detonates a discovered [hand grenade](/wiki/Hand_grenade "Hand grenade") in their house. [(Xinhua)](https://english.news.cn/asiapacific/20250131/403744da959b4af48659f161dfa0b1c9/c.html)

**International relations**

* [2025 Philippine espionage case](/wiki/2025_Philippine_espionage_case "2025 Philippine espionage case"), [Territorial disputes in the South China Sea](/wiki/Territorial_disputes_in_the_South_China_Sea "Territorial disputes in the South China Sea")
  + [Philippine President](/wiki/President_of_the_Philippines "President of the Philippines") [Bongbong Marcos](/wiki/Bongbong_Marcos "Bongbong Marcos") states that he is careful of possible surveillance of [the country's](/wiki/Philippines "Philippines") [air](/wiki/Philippine_Air_Force "Philippine Air Force") and [naval](/wiki/Philippine_Navy "Philippine Navy") bases as well as the movement of vessels supplying [Philippine garrisons](/wiki/Armed_Forces_of_the_Philippines "Armed Forces of the Philippines") in the [South China Sea](/wiki/South_China_Sea "South China Sea") following a series of arrests of suspected [Chinese](/wiki/China "China") [spies](/wiki/Chinese_intelligence_activity_abroad "Chinese intelligence activity abroad") in the Philippines. [(CNA)](https://www.channelnewsasia.com/asia/philippines-president-disturbed-chinese-spy-claims-china-military-4908661)

**Law and crime**

* [United States–Venezuela relations](/wiki/United_States%E2%80%93Venezuela_relations "United States–Venezuela relations")
  + [Venezuela](/wiki/Venezuela "Venezuela") frees six [American](/wiki/Americans "Americans") hostages after U.S. Special Presidential Envoy for Special Missions [Richard Grenell](/wiki/Richard_Grenell "Richard Grenell") meets with [Venezuelan President](/wiki/President_of_Venezuela "President of Venezuela") [Nicolás Maduro](/wiki/Nicol%C3%A1s_Maduro "Nicolás Maduro"). [(*The Hill*)](https://thehill.com/policy/international/5120173-venezuela-hostages-trump-administration/)
* [Myanmar](/wiki/Myanmar "Myanmar")'s [ruling military junta](/wiki/State_Administration_Council "State Administration Council") extends the country's [state of emergency](/wiki/State_of_emergency "State of emergency") for another six months. [(Reuters)](https://www.reuters.com/world/asia-pacific/myanmar-extends-state-emergency-six-months-2025-01-31/)
* Philippine [National Bureau of Investigation](/wiki/National_Bureau_of_Investigation_%28Philippines%29 "National Bureau of Investigation (Philippines)") agents arrest 100 people in [Makati](/wiki/Makati "Makati"), [Metro Manila](/wiki/Metro_Manila "Metro Manila"), [Philippines](/wiki/Philippines "Philippines"), for allegedly running an [online scam](/wiki/Internet_fraud "Internet fraud") operation as [offshore gaming operators](/wiki/Philippine_offshore_gaming_operator "Philippine offshore gaming operator") are banned in the country. [(*Arab News*)](https://www.arabnews.com/node/2588572/amp)

**Politics and elections**

* [2024–2025 Belgian government formation](/wiki/2024%E2%80%932025_Belgian_government_formation "2024–2025 Belgian government formation")
  + An agreement is reached among five [Belgian](/wiki/Belgium "Belgium") [political parties](/wiki/List_of_political_parties_in_Belgium "List of political parties in Belgium") to form a new coalition [government](/wiki/Government_of_Belgium "Government of Belgium") to be headed by future [prime minister](/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Belgium "Prime Minister of Belgium") [Bart De Wever](/wiki/Bart_De_Wever "Bart De Wever"). [(Belga)](https://www.belganewsagency.eu/five-party-presidents-agree-on-new-federal-government-de-wever-i)
* [2025 Greek presidential election](/wiki/2025_Greek_presidential_election "2025 Greek presidential election")
  + The [Hellenic Parliament](/wiki/Hellenic_Parliament "Hellenic Parliament") fails to elect the new [President of Greece](/wiki/President_of_Greece "President of Greece") in the second round, calling for a third round of voting on February 6. [(*Greek City Times*)](https://greekcitytimes.com/2025/01/31/president-election-greece/)
